2020 年 5 月 NBER 共更新 223 篇工作论文，其中与中国研究相关的有 11 篇（62、75、86、112、121、123、159、172、178、185、205）。具体如下：#27230（第 62 篇，中国住房和土地市场中的空间错配）；#27217（第 75 篇，中国儿童疫苗接种的长期认知和教育效应）；#27206（第 86 篇，美国农业的创新、增长与结构变迁）；#27180（第 112 篇，国外市场可及性对农田租金率的影响）；#27171（第 121 篇，中国金融管理体系模式）；#27169（第 123 篇，华人散居研究人员对全球科学的贡献及中国在科研领域的追赶）；#27133（第 159 篇，贸易与福利（跨地方劳动力市场））；#27120（第 172 篇，危机期间健康保险的价值：医疗补助实施对大流行流感死亡率的影响）；#27114（第 178 篇，中美贸易战对美国投资的影响）；#27107（第 185 篇，教育与创新：文化大革命的长期阴影）；#27086（第 205 篇，中国COVID-19污染响应的模糊性）。

No. 1论文详情NBER w27292

The Anatomy of the Transmission of Macroprudential Policies

宏观审慎政策传导机制剖析

Viral V. Acharya, Katharina Bergant, Matteo Crosignani, Tim Eisert, Fergal J. McCann

Abstract

We analyze how regulatory constraints on household leverage—in the form of loan-to-income and loan-to-value limits—affect residential mortgage credit and house prices as well as other asset classes not directly targeted by the limits. Supervisory loan level data suggest that mortgage credit is reallocated from low-to high-income borrowers and from urban to rural counties. This reallocation weakens the feedback loop between credit and house prices and slows down house price growth in “hot” housing markets. Consistent with constrained lenders adjusting their portfolio choice, more-affected banks drive this reallocation and substitute their risk-taking into holdings of securities and corporate credit.

中文摘要

我们分析了以贷款收入比和贷款价值比形式存在的家庭杠杆监管约束如何影响住宅抵押贷款信贷和房价，以及未直接受这些约束限制的其他资产类别。监管层面的贷款数据显示，抵押贷款信贷从低收入借款人重新分配至高收入借款人，并从城市县重新分配至农村县。这种重新分配削弱了信贷与房价之间的反馈循环，并减缓了“过热”住房市场的房价增长。与受约束的贷款机构调整其投资组合选择相一致，受影响较大的银行推动了这种重新分配，并将其风险承担转向证券和企业信贷持有。

No. 2论文详情NBER w27291

Yield Performance of Corn under Heat Stress: A Comparison of Hybrid and Open-Pollinated Seeds during a Period of Technological Transformation, 1933-1955

热胁迫下玉米产量表现：技术转型期（1933-1955）杂交种与开放授粉种子的比较

Keith Meyers, Paul Rhode

Abstract

Starting in the 1930s, commercial hybrid corn seeds rapidly replaced the once predominant open-pollinated varieties planted by farmers. By the mid-1950s almost all corn grown in the United States was of hybrid varieties. Observers have argued that the drought tolerant qualities of these hybrids were a major factor driving farmers’ decisions regarding hybrid adoption, but there is little statistical evidence to substantiate this assertion. Hybrid seeds exhibited other attractive qualities, such as improved performance during prime weather conditions, resistance to wind damage, and increased suitability toward mechanized harvesting. Using historical evidence from Zvi Griliches’s archival records, we reconstruct data on hybrid corn adoption and yields at a more disaggregated geographic level than previously available. We match these data with historical weather records to measure the extent to which hybrid seeds mediated the adverse effects of extreme heat. Our findings suggest that hybrid corns grown in Iowa from 1928 to 1942 did exhibit heat tolerance relative to open-pollinated varieties. This result is unique to Iowa as this reduced temperature sensitivity does not appear when comparing hybrid and open-pollinated grown in other states.

中文摘要

自20世纪30年代起，商业杂交玉米种子迅速取代了农民曾广泛种植的开放授粉品种。到20世纪50年代中期，美国几乎所有的玉米都是杂交品种。观察者认为，这些杂交品种的耐旱特性是推动农民采用杂交种子的主要因素，但支持这一说法的统计证据很少。杂交种子还表现出其他吸引人的特性，例如在良好天气条件下表现更佳、抗风损能力更强以及更适合机械化收割。利用兹维·格里利谢斯档案记录中的历史证据，我们以比以往更细化的地理层面重建了杂交玉米采用率和产量的数据。我们将这些数据与历史天气记录相匹配，以衡量杂交种子在多大程度上缓解了极端高温的不利影响。我们的研究结果表明，1928年至1942年间在爱荷华州种植的杂交玉米相对于开放授粉品种确实表现出耐热性。这一结果仅适用于爱荷华州，因为在其他州种植的杂交种与开放授粉品种相比，并未出现这种温度敏感性降低的现象。

No. 3论文详情NBER w27290

Consumption Insurance in Networks with Asymmetric Information

信息不对称网络中的消费保险

Orazio Attanasio, Sonya Krutikova

Abstract

This paper uses a dataset from Tanzania with information on consumption, income and income shocks within and across family networks. Crucially and uniquely, it also contains data on the degree of information existing between each pair of households within family networks gCrucially and uniquely, it also contains data on the level of information each pair of households has about each other within family networks. We use these data to construct a novel measure of the quality of information both at the level of household pairs and at the level of the network. We also note that the individual level measures can be interpreted as measures of network centrality. We study risk sharing within these networks and explore whether the rejection of perfect risk sharing that we observe can be related to our measures of information quality. We show that households within family networks with better information are less vulnerable to idiosyncratic shocks. Furthermore, we show that more central households within networks are less vulnerable to idiosyncratic shocks. These results have important implications for the characterisation of the empirical failure of the perfect risk sharing hypothesis and point to the importance of information frictions.

中文摘要

本文使用坦桑尼亚的数据集，其中包含家庭网络内部及跨家庭网络的消费、收入和收入冲击信息。至关重要的是，该数据集还独特地包含了家庭网络内每对家庭之间存在的相互信息程度数据。我们利用这些数据，在家庭对层面和网络层面构建了一个新颖的信息质量度量指标。我们还注意到，个体层面的度量指标可被解释为网络中心性度量。我们研究了这些网络内的风险分担，并探讨我们观察到的对完美风险分担的拒绝是否与我们的信息质量度量相关。我们表明，信息质量更好的家庭网络内的家庭受特质冲击的影响较小。此外，我们表明，网络内更中心的家庭受特质冲击的影响较小。这些结果对完美风险分担假设实证失效的特征描述具有重要意义，并指出了信息摩擦的重要性。

No. 4论文详情NBER w27289

Epidemic Responses Under Uncertainty

不确定性下的流行病应对

Michael Barnett, Greg Buchak, Constantine Yannelis

Abstract

We examine how policymakers react to a pandemic with uncertainty around key epidemiological and economic policy parameters by embedding a macroeconomic SIR model in a robust control framework. Uncertainty about disease virulence and severity leads to stricter and more persistent quarantines, while uncertainty about the economic costs of mitigation leads to less stringent quarantines. On net, an uncertainty averse planner adopts stronger mitigation measures. Intuitively, the cost of underestimating the pandemic is out-of-control growth and permanent loss-of-life, while the cost of underestimating the economic consequences of quarantine is more transitory.

中文摘要

我们通过将宏观经济SIR模型嵌入稳健控制框架，考察了政策制定者在面临关键流行病学和经济政策参数不确定性时如何应对大流行病。关于疾病毒力和严重程度的不确定性导致更严格且更持久的隔离措施，而关于缓解措施经济成本的不确定性则导致较不严格的隔离措施。总体而言，厌恶不确定性的规划者会采取更强的缓解措施。直观上，低估大流行病的代价是疫情失控增长和永久性生命损失，而低估隔离经济后果的代价则更为短暂。

No. 5论文详情NBER w27288

Disguising Prejudice: Popular Rationales as Excuses for Intolerant Expression

伪装偏见：作为不宽容表达借口的流行理由

Leonardo Bursztyn, Ingar K. Haaland, Aakaash Rao, Christopher P. Roth

Abstract

We study the use of popular rationales to justify public anti-minority actions. Rationales to oppose minorities change some people's private opinions, leading them to take anti-minority actions even if they are not prejudiced against minorities. When these rationales become widespread, prejudiced people can pool with unprejudiced people who are persuaded, decreasing the stigma associated with anti-minority expression and enabling greater public opposition to minority groups. We examine this mechanism through several large-scale experiments in the context of anti-immigrant behavior in the United States. In a first experiment, subjects learn that a previous respondent authorized a donation to an anti-immigrant organization and then make an inference about the respondent's underlying motivations. Subjects informed that their matched respondent learned about a study claiming that immigrants increase crime rates before authorizing the donation see the respondent as less intolerant and more easily persuadable. In a second experiment, subjects learn about that same study and then choose whether to authorize a publicly observable donation to the anti-immigrant organization. Subjects who are informed that their exposure to the rationale will be publicly observable are substantially more likely to make the donation than subjects who are informed that their exposure will remain private. Our findings suggest that prominent public figures can lower the social cost of intolerant expression by popularizing rationales, contributing to waves of anti-minority behavior.

中文摘要

我们研究了使用流行理由来为公开的反少数群体行为辩护。反对少数群体的理由改变了一些人的私人观点，导致他们即使对少数群体没有偏见也会采取反少数群体行动。当这些理由变得普遍时，有偏见的人可以与那些被说服的无偏见者混在一起，从而减少与反少数群体表达相关的污名，并使得对少数群体的公开反对更加普遍。我们通过在美国反移民行为背景下的几项大规模实验来检验这一机制。在第一个实验中，受试者得知前一位受访者授权向一个反移民组织捐款，然后对受访者的潜在动机进行推断。那些被告知其匹配的受访者在授权捐款前了解了一项声称移民会增加犯罪率的研究的受试者，认为该受访者不那么不宽容且更容易被说服。在第二个实验中，受试者了解同一项研究，然后选择是否授权向该反移民组织进行公开可见的捐款。那些被告知其接触该理由的行为将被公开的受试者，比那些被告知其接触行为将保持私密的受试者，更有可能进行捐款。我们的研究结果表明，知名公众人物可以通过普及理由来降低不宽容表达的社会成本，从而助长反少数群体行为的浪潮。

No. 6论文详情NBER w27287

Spatial Economics for Granular Settings

面向细粒度设定的空间经济学

Jonathan I. Dingel, Felix Tintelnot

Abstract

We examine the application of quantitative spatial models to the growing body of fine spatial data used to study local economic outcomes. In granular settings in which people choose from a large set of potential residence-workplace pairs, observed outcomes in part reflect idiosyncratic choices. Using analytical examples, Monte Carlo simulations, and event studies of neighborhood employment booms, we demonstrate that calibration procedures that equate observed shares and modeled probabilities perform very poorly in these high-dimensional settings. Parsimonious specifications of spatial linkages deliver better counterfactual predictions. To quantify the uncertainty about counterfactual outcomes induced by the idiosyncratic component of individuals’ decisions, we introduce a quantitative spatial model with a finite number of individuals. Applying this model to Amazon’s proposed second headquarters in New York City reveals that its predicted consequences for most neighborhoods vary substantially across realizations of the individual idiosyncrasies.

中文摘要

我们考察了定量空间模型在日益增长的用于研究地方经济结果的精细空间数据中的应用。在人们从大量潜在居住地-工作地对中进行选择的细粒度设定中，观察到的结果部分反映了特质性选择。通过分析性示例、蒙特卡洛模拟以及邻里就业繁荣的事件研究，我们证明，将观察到的份额与模型概率等同起来的校准程序在这些高维设定中表现非常糟糕。空间联系的简约设定能提供更好的反事实预测。为了量化由个体决策的特质性成分引起的反事实结果的不确定性，我们引入了一个包含有限数量个体的定量空间模型。将该模型应用于亚马逊拟议的纽约市第二总部，结果显示，其对大多数邻里的预测后果在不同个体特质性实现之间差异显著。

No. 7论文详情NBER w27286

Demand-Side Constraints in Development: The Role of Market Size, Trade, and (In)Equality

发展中的需求侧约束：市场规模、贸易与（不）平等的作用

Pinelopi K. Goldberg, Tristan Reed

Abstract

What is the pathway to development in a world marked by rising economic nationalism and less international integration? This paper answers this question within a framework that emphasizes the role of demand-side constraints on national development, which is identified with sustained poverty reduction. In this framework, development is linked to the adoption of an increasing returns to scale technology by imperfectly competitive firms that need to pay the fixed setup cost of switching to that technology. Sustained poverty reduction is measured as a continuous decline in the share of the population living below $\$1.90$/day purchasing power parity in 2011 US dollars over a five year period. This outcome is affected in a statistically significant and economically meaningful way by domestic market size, which is measured as function of the income distribution, and international market size, which is measured as a function of legally-binding provisions to international trade agreements, including the General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade, the World Trade Organization and 279 preferential trade agreements. Counterfactual estimates suggest that, in the absence of international integration, the average resident of a low or lower-middle income country does not live in a market large enough to experience sustained poverty reduction. Domestic redistribution targeted towards generating a larger middle class can partially compensate for the lack of an international market.

中文摘要

在一个经济民族主义抬头、国际一体化程度降低的世界里，发展的路径是什么？本文在一个强调需求侧约束对国家发展（以持续减贫为标志）作用的框架内回答了这个问题。在该框架中，发展与不完全竞争企业采用规模报酬递增技术相关联，这些企业需要支付转向该技术的固定启动成本。持续减贫被衡量为五年期内生活在每天1.90美元购买力平价（2011年美元）以下的人口比例持续下降。这一结果受到国内市场规模（以收入分布的函数衡量）和国际市场规模（以国际贸易协定中具有法律约束力的条款的函数衡量，包括关税与贸易总协定、世界贸易组织以及279个优惠贸易协定）在统计上显著且经济上有意义的影响。反事实估计表明，如果没有国际一体化，低收入或中低收入国家的普通居民所居住的市场规模不足以实现持续减贫。旨在产生更大中产阶级的国内再分配可以部分弥补国际市场的缺失。

No. 8论文详情NBER w27285

The Environmental Benefits from Transportation Electrification: Urban Buses

交通电气化的环境效益：城市公交车

Stephen P. Holland, Erin T. Mansur, Nicholas Z. Muller, Andrew J. Yates

Abstract

We determine the environmental benefit of using electric buses rather than diesel or CNG for urban transit. For diesel and CNG we calculate air pollution damages by combining emission rates with damage valuations from the AP3 integrated assessment model and the social cost of carbon. For electric buses we calculate air pollution damages by combining the damage valuations with estimates of the marginal increase in emissions from electricity usage. The environmental benefit is positive on average across all counties in the contiguous U.S. when comparing electric to either diesel or CNG. The environmental benefit of operating an electric bus fleet (rather than diesel) is about $\$65$ million per year in Los Angeles and above $\$10$ million per year in six other MSAs. Including the environmental benefit, we calculate the net present value (NPV) of bus investment. Relative to diesel, the NPV benefit of an electric bus is positive in about two thirds of urban counties. Relative to CNG, the NPV benefit is negative in all counties.

中文摘要

我们确定了在城市交通中使用电动公交车而非柴油或压缩天然气（CNG）公交车的环境效益。对于柴油和CNG，我们通过将排放率与AP3综合评估模型中的损害估值以及碳的社会成本相结合来计算空气污染损害。对于电动公交车，我们通过将损害估值与电力使用导致的边际排放增加估计值相结合来计算空气污染损害。当将电动公交车与柴油或CNG进行比较时，美国本土所有县的平均环境效益为正。在洛杉矶，运营电动公交车队（而非柴油）的环境效益约为每年6500万美元，在其他六个大都市统计区（MSA）则超过每年1000万美元。考虑到环境效益，我们计算了公交车投资的净现值（NPV）。相对于柴油，电动公交车的净现值效益在大约三分之二的城市县为正。相对于CNG，所有县的净现值效益均为负。

No. 9论文详情NBER w27284

What’s Driving Entrepreneurship and Innovation in the Transport Sector?

什么在推动交通领域的创业与创新？

Derrick Choe, Alexander Oettl, Robert Seamans

Abstract

In this chapter we draw from existing literature and a range of statistics to describe economic, entrepreneurial and innovative activities in the transportation and warehousing sector of the U.S. economy. We suggest multiple avenues for future work, and argue for more research on the role of warehousing in particular. Recent trends suggest that the warehousing and storage subsector is experiencing rapid economic and technological changes, likely reflecting shifts in how consumers purchase goods. We also review several other recent innovations, including ride-sharing and autonomous vehicles, that are starting to affect this sector of the economy.

中文摘要

在本章中，我们借鉴现有文献和一系列统计数据，描述了美国经济中交通运输和仓储部门的经济、创业和创新活动。我们提出了未来研究的多种方向，并特别主张加强对仓储作用的研究。近期趋势表明，仓储和存储子部门正在经历快速的经济和技术变革，这可能反映了消费者购买商品方式的转变。我们还回顾了其他几项近期创新，包括拼车和自动驾驶汽车，这些创新正开始影响这一经济部门。

No. 10论文详情NBER w27283

Belief Overreaction and Stock Market Puzzles

信念过度反应与股市谜题

Pedro Bordalo, Nicola Gennaioli, Rafael La Porta, Andrei Shleifer

Abstract

We construct an index of long term expected earnings growth for S&P500 firms and show that it has remarkable power to jointly predict errors in these expectations and stock returns, in both the aggregate market and the cross section. The evidence supports a mechanism whereby good news cause investors to become too optimistic about earnings growth, for the market as a whole but especially for specific firms. This leads to inflated stock prices and, as beliefs are systematically disappointed, to subsequent low returns in the aggregate market and for specific firms in the cross section. Overreaction of measured long-term expectations helps resolve major asset pricing puzzles without time series or cross-sectional variation in required returns.

中文摘要

我们构建了标普500公司长期预期盈利增长指数，并表明该指数在预测这些预期的错误和股票回报方面具有显著能力，无论是在整体市场还是横截面上。证据支持一种机制，即好消息导致投资者对盈利增长过于乐观，对整个市场如此，对特定公司尤其如此。这导致股价膨胀，并且随着信念系统性地落空，随后在整体市场和横截面上的特定公司出现低回报。测量到的长期预期的过度反应有助于解决主要资产定价谜题，而无需在时间序列或横截面上变化所需回报。

No. 11论文详情NBER w27282

India's Lockdown: An Interim Report

印度封锁：中期报告

Debraj Ray, S. Subramanian

Abstract

We provide an interim report on the Indian lockdown provoked by the covid-19 pandemic. The main topics — ranging from the philosophy of lockdown to the provision of relief measures — transcend the Indian case. A recurrent theme is the enormous visibility of covid-19 deaths worldwide, with Governments everywhere propelled to respect this visibility, developing countries perhaps even more so. In advanced economies, the cost of achieving this reduction in visible deaths is “merely” a dramatic reduction in overall economic activity, coupled with far-reaching measures to compensate those who bear such losses. But for India, a developing country with great sectoral and occupational vulnerabilities, this dramatic reduction is more than economic: it means lives lost. These lost lives, through violence, starvation, indebtedness and extreme stress (both psychological and physiological) are invisible. It is this conjunction of visibility and invisibility that drives the Indian response. The lockdown meets all international standards so far; the relief package none.

中文摘要

我们提供了一份关于新冠疫情引发的印度封锁的中期报告。主要议题——从封锁理念到救济措施的实施——超越了印度案例。一个反复出现的主题是全球范围内新冠死亡人数的巨大可见性，各国政府都不得不尊重这种可见性，发展中国家可能更是如此。在发达经济体中，实现这种可见死亡减少的成本“仅仅是”整体经济活动的急剧减少，加上旨在补偿遭受损失者的深远措施。但对于印度这个具有巨大部门和职业脆弱性的发展中国家来说，这种急剧减少不仅仅是经济上的：它意味着生命的丧失。这些因暴力、饥饿、债务和极端压力（包括心理和生理）而失去的生命是看不见的。正是这种可见性与不可见性的结合推动了印度的应对措施。迄今为止，封锁符合所有国际标准；而救济方案则完全不符合。

No. 12论文详情NBER w27281

Nonlinear Production Networks with an Application to the Covid-19 Crisis

非线性生产网络及其在新冠疫情危机中的应用

David Baqaee, Emmanuel Farhi

Abstract

We study the effects of negative supply shocks and shocks to the composition of final demand on aggregate output in a disaggregated neoclassical model with multiple sectors, factors, and input-output linkages. We show how nonlinearities associated with complementarities in consumption and production amplify the effect of negative supply shocks by creating supply bottlenecks and disrupting supply chain networks. These nonlinearities are particularly potent when the shocks are more heterogeneous as the worst-affected sectors drag down the other sectors. Nonlinearities are strengthened when changes in preferences lead households to tilt the composition of their demand towards the crippled sectors directly and indirectly through their supply chains. And nonlinearities are further intensified when factors cannot easily be reallocated across sectors to reinforce weak links. A quantitative investigation suggests that nonlinearities may amplify the impact of the Covid-19 shock by between 10\\%-100\\%, depending on the horizon of analysis and the exact size of the shocks.

中文摘要

我们研究在一个包含多个部门、要素和投入产出关系的分解新古典模型中，负供给冲击和最终需求构成冲击对总产出的影响。我们展示了与消费和生产互补性相关的非线性如何通过造成供给瓶颈和破坏供应链网络来放大负供给冲击的影响。当冲击更加异质时，这些非线性尤其强大，因为受影响最严重的部门会拖累其他部门。当偏好变化导致家庭直接或通过供应链间接地将需求构成转向受损部门时，非线性会增强。当要素难以在部门间重新配置以加强薄弱环节时，非线性会进一步加剧。定量研究表明，根据分析的时间范围和冲击的确切规模，非线性可能将新冠冲击的影响放大10%到100%。

No. 13论文详情NBER w27280

Effects of Social Distancing Policy on Labor Market Outcomes

社交距离政策对劳动力市场结果的影响

Sumedha Gupta, Laura Montenovo, Thuy D. Nguyen, Felipe Lozano Rojas, Ian M. Schmutte, Kosali I. Simon, Bruce A. Weinberg, Coady Wing

Abstract

This paper examines the impact of the social distancing policies states adopted between March and April of 2020 in response to the COVID-19 epidemic. These actions, together with voluntary social distancing, appear to have reduced the rate of new COVID-19 cases and deaths, but raised concerns about the costs experienced by workers and businesses. Estimates from difference-in-difference models that leverage cross-state variation in the timing of business closures and stay-at-home mandates suggest that the employment rate fell by about 1.7 percentage points for every extra 10 days that a state experienced a stay-at-home mandate during the period March 12-April 12, 2020; select business closure laws were associated with similar employment effects. \nOur estimates imply that about 40% of the 12 percentage point decline in employment rates between January and April 2020 was due to a nationwide shock while about 60% was driven by state social distancing policies. The negative employment effects of state policies were larger for workers in "non-essential" industries, workers without a college degree, and early-career workers. Policy caused relatively modest changes in hours worked and earnings among those who remain employed. We find no concerning evidence of pre-trends in the monthly (low-frequency) CPS data, but use high-frequency data on work-related mobility measured from cellphones, job-loss-related internet searches, and initial unemployment claims to investigate the possibility that the large employment effects experienced in April could have occurred after the March CPS but but before policy adoption. In those analyses, we find pre-trends for some outcomes but not others. Thus we cannot fully rule out that some employment effects shortly predated the policies. As states relax business closures, ensuring gains in labor market activities in ways that continue to mitigate COVID-19 "surges" and public health risks will be key considerations to monitor.

中文摘要

本文考察了2020年3月至4月间各州为应对新冠疫情而采取的社交距离政策的影响。这些行动，加上自愿社交距离，似乎降低了新增新冠病例和死亡率的比率，但引发了关于工人和企业所承受成本的担忧。利用各州在商业关闭和居家令实施时间上的跨州差异，采用双重差分模型的估计表明，在2020年3月12日至4月12日期间，一个州每多经历10天居家令，就业率下降约1.7个百分点；特定的商业关闭法律与类似的就业效应相关。我们的估计表明，2020年1月至4月间12个百分点的就业率下降中，约40%是由全国性冲击造成的，而约60%是由州社交距离政策驱动的。州政策的负面就业效应在“非必要”行业的工人、没有大学学位的工人以及职业生涯早期的工人中更大。政策对仍在就业者的工作时间和收入造成了相对适度的变化。我们在月度（低频）当前人口调查数据中没有发现令人担忧的预趋势证据，但使用从手机测量的与工作相关的移动高频数据、与失业相关的互联网搜索以及首次失业救济申请，来调查4月份经历的大规模就业效应是否可能发生在3月当前人口调查之后但在政策实施之前。在这些分析中，我们发现某些结果存在预趋势，但其他结果则没有。因此，我们不能完全排除一些就业效应在政策实施前不久就出现的可能性。随着各州放松商业关闭，确保以继续减轻新冠疫情“激增”和公共卫生风险的方式促进劳动力市场活动的增长，将是需要监测的关键考虑因素。

No. 14论文详情NBER w27279

Post-9/11 War Deployments Increased Crime among Veterans

9/11后战争部署增加了退伍军人的犯罪率

Resul Cesur, Joseph J. Sabia, Erdal Tekin

Abstract

Several high-profile news stories have linked post-September 11 (9/11) combat service to violent crime among veterans. Nevertheless, there is scant causal evidence for this claim. We exploit the administrative procedures by which U.S. Armed Forces senior commanders conditionally randomly assign active duty servicemen to overseas deployments to estimate the causal impact of modern warfare on crime. Using data from two national surveys and a unified framework, we find consistent evidence that post-9/11 combat service substantially increased the probability of crime commission among veterans. Combat increases the likelihood of property and violent crime, arrest, gang membership, trouble with police, and punishment under the Uniform Code of Military Justice. Back-of-the-envelope calculations suggest that post-9/11 combat exposure generated approximately $\$26.7$ billion in additional crime costs. Finally, we document descriptive evidence that Traumatic Brain Injury and Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (PTSD) may be important mechanisms to explain post-9/11 combat-induced increases in crime.

中文摘要

几起备受关注的新闻报道将9/11后的战斗服役与退伍军人的暴力犯罪联系起来。然而，这一说法缺乏因果证据。我们利用美国武装部队高级指挥官有条件地随机分配现役军人到海外部署的行政程序，来估计现代战争对犯罪的因果影响。使用来自两项全国性调查的数据和一个统一框架，我们发现一致的证据表明，9/11后的战斗服役显著增加了退伍军人实施犯罪的概率。战斗增加了财产犯罪和暴力犯罪、被捕、加入帮派、与警察发生麻烦以及受到《统一军事司法法典》惩罚的可能性。粗略计算表明，9/11后的战斗暴露产生了约267亿美元的额外犯罪成本。最后，我们记录了描述性证据，表明创伤性脑损伤和创伤后应激障碍可能是解释9/11后战斗引发的犯罪增加的重要机制。

No. 15论文详情NBER w27278

Flying or Trapped?

飞翔还是被困？

Yunfang Hu, Takuma Kunieda, Kazuo Nishimura, Ping Wang

Abstract

We develop a unified theory with endogenous technology choice in human/knowledge capital accumulation to establish a rich array of equilibrium development paradigms, including poverty trap, middle income trap and flying geese growth. We then generalize the baseline structure and establish conditions for different development paradigms to arise. By calibrating the general model to fit the data from several representative economies with different income and growth patterns, we identify various prolonged flying geese episodes and middle income traps. By performing growth accounting, we find that improving human capital accumulation efficacy and mitigating barriers to human capital accumulation are most rewarding for advancing the economy and avoiding the middle income trap.

中文摘要

我们发展了一个统一理论，其中包含人力资本/知识资本积累中的内生技术选择，以建立一系列均衡发展范式，包括贫困陷阱、中等收入陷阱和雁行增长。然后，我们推广了基准结构，并建立了不同发展范式出现的条件。通过校准一般模型以拟合几个具有不同收入和增长模式的代表性经济体的数据，我们识别了各种长期的雁行阶段和中等收入陷阱。通过进行增长核算，我们发现提高人力资本积累效率和减少人力资本积累障碍对于推动经济发展和避免中等收入陷阱最为有益。

No. 16论文详情NBER w27277

Divided We Stay Home: Social Distancing and Ethnic Diversity

分裂使我们待在家里：社交距离与种族多样性

Georgy Egorov, Ruben Enikolopov, Alexey Makarin, Maria Petrova

Abstract

Voluntary social distancing plays a vital role in containing the spread of the disease during a pandemic. As a public good, it should be more commonplace in more homogeneous and altruistic societies. However, for healthy people, observing social distancing has private benefits, too. If sick individuals are more likely to stay home, healthy ones have fewer incentives to do so, especially if the asymptomatic transmission is perceived to be unlikely. Theoretically, we show that this interplay may lead to a stricter observance of social distancing in more diverse and less altruistic societies. Empirically, we find that, consistent with the model, the reduction in mobility following the first local case of COVID-19 was stronger in Russian cities with higher ethnic fractionalization and cities with higher levels of xenophobia. For identification, we predict the timing of the first case using pre-existing patterns of internal migration to Moscow. Using SafeGraph data on mobility patterns, we confirm that mobility reduction in the United States was also higher in counties with higher ethnic fractionalization. Our findings highlight the importance of strategic incentives of different population groups for the effectiveness of public policy.

中文摘要

在大流行期间，自愿社交距离在控制疾病传播中起着至关重要的作用。作为一种公共物品，它在更同质和更利他的社会中应该更为普遍。然而，对于健康人来说，遵守社交距离也有私人收益。如果病人更可能待在家里，健康人这样做的激励就会减少，尤其是在认为无症状传播不太可能的情况下。理论上，我们表明这种相互作用可能导致在更多样化和更不利他的社会中更严格地遵守社交距离。实证上，我们发现，与模型一致，在俄罗斯种族分裂程度更高的城市和仇外情绪更高的城市，首次本地新冠病例出现后流动性的减少更强。为了识别，我们利用先前存在的向莫斯科内部迁移的模式来预测首例病例的时间。使用关于移动模式的SafeGraph数据，我们证实美国种族分裂程度更高的县的流动性减少也更大。我们的发现强调了不同人口群体的战略激励对公共政策有效性的重要性。

No. 17论文详情NBER w27276

The Welfare Cost of a Current Account Imbalance: A "Clean" Effect

经常账户失衡的福利成本：一种“清洁”效应

Jungho Lee, Shang-Jin Wei, Jianhuan Xu

Abstract

According to the existing open-economy macroeconomics literature, a current account surplus is associated with a welfare loss only when distortions exist in either savings or investment, and bilateral imbalances do not matter when holding a country's overall imbalance constant. We propose a new welfare effect even in the absence of such distortions. We also show that the patterns of bilateral imbalances matter for welfare. In our theory, a trade imbalance -- the largest component of a current account imbalance -- interacts with a country's pollution control ("cleanness") regime to generate welfare effects outside the standard channels. In particular, a trade surplus alters the shipping costs and the composition of a country's imports in ways that increase the disutility of pollution.

中文摘要

根据现有的开放经济宏观经济学文献，经常账户盈余仅在储蓄或投资存在扭曲时才与福利损失相关，并且在保持一国总体失衡不变的情况下，双边失衡并不重要。我们提出了一种新的福利效应，即使在没有此类扭曲的情况下也存在。我们还表明，双边失衡的模式对福利有影响。在我们的理论中，贸易失衡——经常账户失衡的最大组成部分——与一国的污染控制（“清洁”）制度相互作用，通过标准渠道之外的途径产生福利效应。特别是，贸易顺差会改变运输成本和一国进口的构成，从而增加污染带来的负效用。

No. 18论文详情NBER w27275

Deadly Debt Crises: COVID-19 in Emerging Markets

致命债务危机：新兴市场中的COVID-19

Cristina Arellano, Yan Bai, Gabriel P. Mihalache

Abstract

Emerging markets have experienced large human and economic costs from COVID-19, and their tight fiscal space has limited the support extended to their citizens. We study the impact of an epidemic on economic and health outcomes by integrating epidemiological dynamics into a sovereign default model. The sovereign’s option to default tightens fiscal space and results in an epidemic with limited mitigation and depressed consumption. A quantitative analysis of our model accounts well for the dynamics of fatalities, social distancing, consumption, sovereign debt, and spreads in Latin America. We find that because of default risk, the welfare cost of the pandemic is about a third higher than it is in a version of the model with perfect financial markets. We study debt relief programs and find a compelling case for their implementation. These programs deliver large social gains, improving health and economic outcomes for the country at no cost to international lenders or financial institutions.

中文摘要

新兴市场因COVID-19遭受了巨大的人员和经济损失，其紧张的财政空间限制了向公民提供的支持。我们通过将流行病学动态纳入主权违约模型，研究了流行病对经济和健康结果的影响。主权国家的违约选择压缩了财政空间，导致疫情缓解措施有限且消费低迷。我们模型的定量分析很好地解释了拉丁美洲的死亡人数、社交距离、消费、主权债务和利差的动态变化。我们发现，由于违约风险，疫情造成的福利成本比金融市场完善的模型版本高出约三分之一。我们研究了债务减免计划，并发现了实施这些计划的令人信服的理由。这些计划带来了巨大的社会收益，改善了该国的健康和经济状况，且对国际贷款机构或金融机构不造成任何成本。

How to Get Away with Merger: Stealth Consolidation and Its Effects on US Healthcare

如何规避并购审查：隐形整合及其对美国医疗保健的影响

Thomas G. Wollmann

Abstract

US antitrust authorities are only notified of large mergers, so most transactions could escape antitrust scrutiny. I study premerger notification exemptions in the dialysis industry. I find that, in sharp contrast to reportable mergers, exempt ones almost completely avoid enforcement. As a result, exempt mergers increase concentration and reduce healthcare quality, as measured by hospitalization and mortality rates. I then estimate a structural model to simulate the equilibrium response of demand, quality, and enforcement to the elimination of exemptions. I find that the benefits of eliminating exemptions in the dialysis industry far exceed the costs.

中文摘要

美国反垄断机构仅会收到大型并购的通知，因此大多数交易可能逃脱反垄断审查。我研究了透析行业的并购前通知豁免。我发现，与应报告的并购形成鲜明对比的是，豁免的并购几乎完全避免了执法。因此，豁免的并购增加了市场集中度，并降低了医疗保健质量（以住院率和死亡率衡量）。然后，我估计了一个结构模型，以模拟需求、质量和执法对取消豁免的均衡反应。我发现，在透析行业取消豁免的收益远远超过成本。

How Should Policy Responses to the COVID-19 Pandemic Differ in the Developing World?

针对COVID-19疫情的政策应对在发展中国家应如何不同？

Titan Alon, Minki Kim, David Lagakos, Mitchell VanVuren

Abstract

This paper quantitatively analyzes how policy responses to the COVID-19 pandemic should differ in developing countries. To do so we build an incomplete-markets macroeconomic model with heterogeneous agents and epidemiological dynamics that features several of the key distinctions between advanced and developing economies germane to the pandemic. We focus in particular on differences in: age structure, fiscal capacity, healthcare capacity, informality, and the frequency of contacts between individuals at home, work, school and other locations. The model predicts that blanket lockdowns are less effective in developing countries, saving fewer lives per unit of lost GDP. In contrast, age-specific policies are even more effective, since they focus scarce public funds on shielding the smaller population of older individuals. School closures are also more effective at saving lives in developing countries, providing a greater reduction in secondary transmissions between children and older adults at home.

中文摘要

本文定量分析了针对COVID-19疫情的政策应对在发展中国家应如何不同。为此，我们构建了一个包含异质性主体和流行病学动态的不完全市场宏观经济模型，该模型涵盖了发达经济体与发展中经济体之间与疫情相关的几个关键区别。我们特别关注以下方面的差异：年龄结构、财政能力、医疗保健能力、非正规经济以及个人在家庭、工作、学校和其他场所的接触频率。该模型预测，全面封锁在发展中国家效果较差，每单位GDP损失所挽救的生命更少。相比之下，针对特定年龄的政策更为有效，因为它们将稀缺的公共资金集中于保护数量较少的老年人群。学校停课在发展中国家挽救生命方面也更有效，能更大程度地减少儿童与家中老年人之间的二次传播。

No. 21论文详情NBER w27272

Inside the Mind of a Stock Market Crash

股市崩盘背后的心理

Stefano Giglio, Matteo Maggiori, Johannes Stroebel, Stephen Utkus

Abstract

We analyze how investor expectations about economic growth and stock returns changed during the February-March 2020 stock market crash induced by the COVID-19 pandemic, as well as during the subsequent partial stock market recovery. We surveyed retail investors who are clients of Vanguard at three points in time: (i) on February 11-12, around the all-time stock market high, (ii) on March 11-12, after the stock market had collapsed by over 20%, and (iii) on April 16-17, after the market had rallied 25% from its lowest point. Following the crash, the average investor turned more pessimistic about the short-run performance of both the stock market and the real economy. Investors also perceived higher probabilities of both further extreme stock market declines and large declines in short-run real economic activity. In contrast, investor expectations about long-run (10-year) economic and stock market outcomes remained largely unchanged, and, if anything, improved. Disagreement among investors about economic and stock market outcomes also increased substantially following the stock market crash, with the disagreement persisting through the partial market recovery. Those respondents who were the most optimistic in February saw the largest decline in expectations, and sold the most equity. Those respondents who were the most pessimistic in February largely left their portfolios unchanged during and after the crash.

中文摘要

我们分析了在2020年2月至3月由COVID-19疫情引发的股市崩盘期间，以及随后的部分股市复苏期间，投资者对经济增长和股票回报的预期如何变化。我们在三个时间点对Vanguard的散户投资者客户进行了调查：(i) 2月11日至12日，股市处于历史高点附近；(ii) 3月11日至12日，股市暴跌超过20%之后；(iii) 4月16日至17日，股市从最低点反弹25%之后。崩盘后，普通投资者对股市和实体经济的短期表现变得更加悲观。投资者还认为股市进一步极端下跌和短期实体经济大幅下滑的概率更高。相比之下，投资者对长期（10年）经济和股市结果的预期基本保持不变，甚至有所改善。投资者之间对经济和股市结果的分歧在股市崩盘后也大幅增加，这种分歧在部分市场复苏期间持续存在。那些在2月份最为乐观的受访者预期下降幅度最大，并卖出了最多的股票。那些在2月份最为悲观的受访者在崩盘期间和之后基本保持其投资组合不变。

No. 22论文详情NBER w27271

Subjective Expectations and Demand for Contraception

主观预期与避孕需求

Grant Miller, Áureo de Paula, Christine Valente

Abstract

One-quarter of married, fertile-age women in Sub-Saharan Africa report not wanting a pregnancy and yet do not practice contraception. We collect detailed data on the subjective beliefs of married, adult women not wanting a pregnancy and estimate a structural model of contraceptive choices. Both our structural model and a validation exercise using an exogenous shock to beliefs show that correcting women’s beliefs about pregnancy risk absent contraception can increase use considerably. Our structural estimates further indicate that costly interventions like eliminating supply constraints would only modestly increase contraceptive use, while confirming the importance of partners’ preferences highlighted in related literature.

中文摘要

撒哈拉以南非洲地区四分之一的已婚育龄女性表示不想要孩子，但却没有采取避孕措施。我们收集了不想要孩子的已婚成年女性的主观信念的详细数据，并估计了一个避孕选择的结构模型。我们的结构模型以及使用信念外生冲击进行的验证练习都表明，纠正女性关于无避孕情况下怀孕风险的信念可以显著提高避孕使用率。我们的结构估计进一步表明，像消除供应限制这样成本高昂的干预措施只会适度增加避孕使用率，同时证实了相关文献中强调的伴侣偏好的重要性。

No. 23论文详情NBER w27270

Common Practice: Spillovers from Medicare on Private Health Care

常见做法：医疗保险对私人医疗保健的溢出效应

Michael L. Barnett, Andrew Olenski, Adam Sacarny

Abstract

Efforts to raise the productivity of the U.S. health care system have proceeded slowly. One potential explanation is the fragmentation of payment across insurers. Each insurer's efforts to improve care could influence how doctors practice medicine for other insurers, leading to unvalued externalities. We study these externalities by examining the unintended private insurance spillovers of a public insurer's intervention. In 2015, Medicare randomized warning letters to doctors to curtail overuse of antipsychotics. Even though the letters did not mention private insurance, they reduced prescribing to privately insured patients by 12%. The reduction to Medicare patients was 17%, and we cannot reject one-for-one spillovers. The results imply that physicians experience large costs to setting insurer-specific medical practice styles. If private insurers conducted a similar intervention with their own limited information, they would stem half as much prescribing as a social planner able and willing to better target the intervention. Our findings establish that insurers can affect health care well outside their direct purview, raising the question of how to match their private objectives with their scope of influence.

中文摘要

提高美国医疗保健系统生产力的努力进展缓慢。一个可能的解释是保险公司之间支付的碎片化。每个保险公司改善护理的努力可能会影响医生为其他保险公司行医的方式，从而产生未被重视的外部性。我们通过研究公共保险公司干预措施对私人保险的意外溢出效应来考察这些外部性。2015年，医疗保险随机向医生发送警告信，以遏制抗精神病药物的过度使用。尽管这些信件没有提及私人保险，但它们使向私人保险患者的处方量减少了12%。向医疗保险患者的处方量减少了17%，我们不能拒绝一对一溢出效应的假设。这些结果表明，医生为不同保险公司设定特定行医风格的成本很高。如果私人保险公司利用自身有限的信息进行类似的干预，它们所能遏制的处方量将只有一位能够且愿意更好地针对干预措施的社会规划者的一半。我们的发现证实，保险公司可以影响其直接管辖范围之外的医疗保健，这提出了如何将其私人目标与其影响力范围相匹配的问题。

No. 24论文详情NBER w27269

Measuring the Effect of Student Loans on College Persistence

衡量学生贷款对大学持续就读的影响

David Card, Alex Solis

Abstract

Governments around the world use grant and loan programs to ease the financial constraints that contribute to socioeconomic gaps in college completion. A growing body of research assesses the impact of grants; less is known about how loan programs affect persistence and degree completion. We use detailed administrative data from Chile to provide rigorous regression-discontinuity-based evidence on the impacts of loan eligibility for university students who retake the national admission test after their first year of studies. Those who score above a certain threshold become eligible for loans covering around 85% of tuition costs for the duration of their program. We find that access to loans increases the fraction who return to university for a second year by 20 percentage points, with two-thirds of the effect arising from a reduction in transfers to vocational colleges and one-third from a decline in the share who stop post-secondary schooling altogether. The longer-run impacts are smaller but remain highly significant, with a 12 percentage point impact on the fraction of marginally eligible retakers who complete a bachelor's degree.

中文摘要

世界各地的政府使用助学金和贷款项目来缓解导致大学完成率存在社会经济差距的财务约束。越来越多的研究评估了助学金的影响；但对贷款项目如何影响持续就读和学位完成知之甚少。我们利用智利的详细行政数据，为贷款资格对大学一年级后重考全国入学考试的学生的影响提供了基于断点回归的严谨证据。那些分数超过特定门槛的学生有资格获得贷款，该贷款覆盖其课程期间约85%的学费。我们发现，获得贷款使第二年重返大学的学生比例增加了20个百分点，其中三分之二的效果来自向职业学院的转学减少，三分之一来自完全停止中学后教育的人数下降。长期影响较小，但仍然高度显著，对勉强合格的复读生中完成学士学位比例的影响为12个百分点。

The Great Migration of Black Americans from the US South: A Guide and Interpretation

William J. Collins

Abstract

The Great Migration from the US South is a prominent theme in economic history research not only because it was a prime example of large scale internal migration, but also because it had far-reaching ramifications for American economic, social, and political change. This article offers a concise review of the literature focused on questions of timing, selection, and migrants’ outcomes, and then offers a more speculative interpretation of how the Great Migration fostered the advancement of Civil Rights. It concludes by pointing out areas where further exploration would be valuable.

中文摘要

Dying to Work: Effects of Unemployment Insurance on Health

为工作而死：失业保险对健康的影响

Alexander Ahammer, Analisa Packham

Abstract

Using administrative data for Upper Austrian workers from 2003--2013, we show that an extension in unemployment insurance (UI) duration increases unemployment length and impacts worker physical and mental health. These effects vary by gender. Specifically, we find that women eligible for an additional 9 weeks of UI benefits fill fewer opioid and antidepressant prescriptions and experience a lower likelihood of filing a disability claim, as compared to non-eligible unemployed women. Moreover, estimates indicate within-household spillovers for young children. For men, we find that extending UI benefit duration increases the likelihood of a cardiac event and eventual disability retirement filing.

中文摘要

Reconstructing the Yield Curve

重构收益率曲线

Yan Liu, Jing Cynthia Wu

Abstract

The constant-maturity zero-coupon Treasury yield curve is one of the most studied datasets. We reconstruct the yield curve using a non-parametric kernel-smoothing method with a novel adaptive bandwidth specifically designed to fit the Treasury yield curve. Our curve is globally smooth while still capturing important local variation. Economically, we show that applying our data leads to different conclusions from using the leading alternative data of Gürkaynak et al. (2007) (GSW) when we repeat two popular studies of Cochrane and Piazzesi (2005) and Giglio and Kelly (2018). Statistically, we show our dataset preserves information in the raw data and has much smaller pricing errors than GSW. Our new yield curve is maintained and updated online, complemented by bandwidths that summarize information content in the raw data.

中文摘要

恒定期限的零息国债收益率曲线是研究最广泛的数据集之一。我们使用一种非参数核平滑方法重构收益率曲线，该方法采用了一种新颖的自适应带宽，专门设计用于拟合国债收益率曲线。我们的曲线在全局上是平滑的，同时仍能捕捉重要的局部变化。在经济上，我们表明，当重复Cochrane和Piazzesi（2005）以及Giglio和Kelly（2018）的两项流行研究时，使用我们的数据会得出与使用Gürkaynak等人（2007）（GSW）的主要替代数据不同的结论。在统计上，我们表明我们的数据集保留了原始数据中的信息，并且其定价误差远小于GSW。我们新的收益率曲线会在线维护和更新，并辅以总结原始数据信息含量的带宽。

Framing, Information, and Welfare

框架、信息与福利

Andrew Caplin, Daniel J. Martin

Abstract

Consumers often face an overwhelming amount of information when deciding between products, and one of the primary policymaking tools available to improve their informativeness is the framing of this information. We introduce a general theoretical approach that characterizes when one frame is revealed to provide robustly higher welfare than another. Because it is testable, adaptable, and both necessary and sufficient, our condition determines both whether frames are robustly welfare ranked in a particular data set and the overall proportion of data sets in which frames can be so ranked.

中文摘要

消费者在决定产品时常常面临海量信息，而改善信息有效性的主要政策工具之一就是信息的框架设计。我们引入了一种通用的理论方法，该方法刻画了何时一个框架被揭示为比另一个框架提供稳健更高的福利。由于我们的条件是可检验的、可适应的，并且既是必要的也是充分的，因此它既能确定在特定数据集中框架是否具有稳健的福利排序，也能确定在所有数据集中框架可以被如此排序的总体比例。

COVID-19 Doesn't Need Lockdowns to Destroy Jobs: The Effect of Local Outbreaks in Korea

COVID-19无需封锁即可摧毁就业：韩国局部疫情的影响

Sangmin Aum, Sang Yoon (Tim) Lee, Yongseok Shin

Abstract

Unlike most countries, Korea did not implement a lockdown in its battle against COVID-19, instead successfully relying on testing and contact tracing. Only one region, Daegu-Gyeongbuk (DG), had a significant number of infections, traced to a religious sect. This allows us to estimate the causal effect of the outbreak on the labor market using difference-in-differences. We find that a one per thousand increase in infections causes a 2 to 3 percent drop in local employment. Non-causal estimates of this coefficient from the US and UK, which implemented large-scale lockdowns, range from 5 to 6 percent, suggesting that at most half of the job losses in the US and UK can be attributed to lockdowns. We also find that employment losses caused by local outbreaks in the absence of lockdowns are (i) mainly due to reduced hiring by small establishments, (ii) concentrated in the accommodation/food, education, real estate, and transportation industries, and (iii) worst for the economically vulnerable workers who are less educated, young, in low-wage occupations, and on temporary contracts, even controlling for industry effects. All these patterns are similar to what we observe in the US and UK: The unequal effects of COVID-19 are the same with or without lockdowns. Our finding suggests that the lifting of lockdowns in the US and UK may lead to only modest recoveries in employment unless COVID-19 infection rates fall.

中文摘要

与大多数国家不同，韩国在抗击COVID-19时没有实施封锁，而是成功依赖检测和接触者追踪。只有一个地区，即大邱-庆北（DG），出现了大量感染病例，可追溯至一个宗教团体。这使我们能够使用双重差分法估计疫情对劳动力市场的因果效应。我们发现，每千人中感染人数增加一例，会导致当地就业率下降2%至3%。来自实施大规模封锁的美国和非因果估计的这一系数范围为5%至6%，这表明美国和英国的失业损失中最多有一半可归因于封锁。我们还发现，在没有封锁的情况下，由局部疫情造成的就业损失（i）主要源于小型企业的招聘减少，（ii）集中在住宿/餐饮、教育、房地产和交通运输行业，以及（iii）对经济弱势工人（如受教育程度较低、年轻、从事低薪职业和签订临时合同的工人）影响最严重，即使在控制了行业效应后也是如此。所有这些模式与美国和英国观察到的相似：无论有无封锁，COVID-19的不平等影响是相同的。我们的发现表明，除非COVID-19感染率下降，否则美国和英国解除封锁可能只会带来就业的温和复苏。

Breaking Routine for Energy Savings: An Appliance-level Analysis of Small Business Behavior under Dynamic Prices

打破常规以节约能源：动态价格下小企业行为的电器层面分析

Jiyong Eom, Frank A. Wolak

Abstract

Small businesses are typically committed to providing a positive customer experience and therefore may exhibit a response to dynamic electricity prices different from residential or industrial customers. We conduct a field experiment to determine the extent to which small businesses respond through re-configuration of typical routines throughout the experiment period versus through adjustments to specific dynamic pricing events. Using a customer-level survey of appliance ownership, we estimate the hourly response patterns of individual appliances to participation in the experiment versus individual dynamic pricing events. Consistent with our re-configuration hypothesis, small businesses primarily curtail electricity usage throughout the experiment period, although we also find a small imprecisely estimated response to dynamic pricing events on top of the re-configuration effect. Appliances not critical to a positive customer experience such as dish dryers, food storage units, lights, electric motors & pumps, and industrial heaters are the major sources of the energy savings from the re-configuration actions of these small businesses.

中文摘要

小企业通常致力于提供积极的客户体验，因此其对动态电价可能表现出与居民或工业客户不同的反应。我们进行了一项实地实验，以确定小企业在多大程度上通过在整个实验期间重新配置典型惯例，以及通过针对特定动态定价事件进行调整来做出反应。利用客户层面的电器拥有情况调查，我们估算了单个电器对参与实验与对单个动态定价事件的每小时响应模式。与我们的重新配置假设一致，小企业主要在整个实验期间削减用电量，尽管我们也发现，在重新配置效应之上，对动态定价事件存在一个微小且估计不精确的响应。对积极客户体验不关键的电器，如餐具烘干机、食品储存设备、照明、电动机和泵以及工业加热器，是这些小企业通过重新配置行动实现节能的主要来源。

Simplified Electricity Market Models with Significant Intermittent Renewable Capacity: Evidence from Italy

具有显著间歇性可再生能源容量的简化电力市场模型：来自意大利的证据

Christoph Graf, Federico Quaglia, Frank A. Wolak

Abstract

Using hourly offer curves from the Italian day-ahead market and the real-time re-dispatch market for the period January 1, 2017 to December 31, 2018, we show how thermal generation unit owners are able to profit from differences between a simplified day-ahead market design that ignores system security constraints as well as generation unit operating constraints, and real-time system operation where these constraints must be respected. We find that thermal generation unit owners increase or decrease their day-ahead offer prices depending on the probability that their final output will be increased or decreased relative to their day-ahead schedules because of real-time operating constraints. First, we estimate generation unit-level models of the probability of each of these outcomes conditional on forecast demand and renewable production in Italy and neighboring countries. Our most conservative estimate of the impact of a change in the probability a unit owner will have its day-ahead schedule increased in the real-time re-dispatch market implies a day-ahead offer price increase of 5 EUR/MWh if this probability changes by 0.1. If the probability of a day-ahead schedule decrease rises by 0.1 the unit owner's offer price is predicted to be 6 EUR/MWh less. Over our sample period, we find that the economic re-dispatch cost averaged approximately 15% of the total cost of energy consumption valued at the day-ahead price.

中文摘要

利用2017年1月1日至2018年12月31日期间意大利日前市场和实时再调度市场的每小时报价曲线，我们展示了火电机组所有者如何能够利用简化的日前市场设计（忽略系统安全约束和机组运行约束）与必须遵守这些约束的实时系统运行之间的差异获利。我们发现，火电机组所有者会根据其最终出力相对于日前计划因实时运行约束而被增加或减少的概率，来调高或调低其日前报价。首先，我们估计了机组层面的模型，这些模型基于意大利及邻国的预测需求和可再生能源产量，来预测每种结果的条件概率。我们对机组所有者日前计划在实时再调度市场中被增加的概率变化影响的最保守估计是，如果该概率变化0.1，则日前报价将增加5欧元/兆瓦时。如果日前计划被减少的概率上升0.1，则预计该机组所有者的报价将减少6欧元/兆瓦时。在我们的样本期内，我们发现经济再调度成本平均约占按日前价格计算的总能源消费成本的15%。

Olivia S. Mitchell

Abstract

In the wake of the global pandemic known as COVID-19, retirees, along with those hoping to retire someday, have been shocked into a new awareness of the need for better risk management tools to handle longevity and aging. An Experimental Comparison of Carbon Pricing Under Uncertainty in Electricity Markets

不确定性下电力市场碳定价的实验比较

Trevor L. Davis, Mark C. Thurber, Frank A. Wolak

Abstract

We report on an economic experiment that compares outcomes in electricity markets subject to carbon-tax and cap-and-trade policies. Under conditions of uncertainty, price-based and quantity-based policy instruments cannot be truly equivalent, so we compared three matched carbon-tax/cap-and-trade pairs with equivalent emissions targets, mean emissions, and mean carbon prices, respectively. Across these matched pairs, the cap-and-trade mechanism produced much higher wholesale electricity prices (38.5% to 52.6% higher) and lower total electricity production (2.5% to 4.0% lower) than the “equivalent” carbon tax, without any lower carbon emissions. Market participants who forecast a lower price of carbon in the cap-and-trade games ran their units more than those who forecast a higher price of carbon, which caused emissions from the dirtiest generating units (Coal and Gas Peakers) to be significantly higher (15.2% to 33.0%) than in the carbon tax games. These merit order “mistakes” in the cap-and-trade games suggest an important advantage of the carbon tax as policy: namely, that the cost of carbon can treated by firms as a known input to production.

中文摘要

我们报告了一项经济实验，该实验比较了在碳税和总量控制与交易政策下电力市场的结果。在不确定性条件下，基于价格和基于数量的政策工具无法真正等价，因此我们比较了三组匹配的碳税/总量控制与交易对，它们分别对应等价的排放目标、平均排放量和平均碳价格。在这些匹配对中，与“等价”的碳税相比，总量控制与交易机制产生了高得多的批发电价（高出38.5%至52.6%）和更低的总发电量（低2.5%至4.0%），而碳排放并未降低。在总量控制与交易博弈中，预测碳价较低的参与者比预测碳价较高的参与者运行其机组更多，这导致最脏的发电机组（燃煤和燃气调峰机组）的排放量显著高于碳税博弈（高出15.2%至33.0%）。总量控制与交易博弈中的这些排序“错误”表明碳税作为政策的一个重要优势：即企业可以将碳成本视为已知的生产投入。

Measuring the Spatial Distribution of Health Rankings in the United States

衡量美国健康排名的空间分布

Will Davis, Alexander D. Gordan, Rusty Tchernis

Abstract

We rank counties in the United States of America with respect to population health. We utilize the five observable county health variables used to construct the University of Wisconsin Population Health Institute’s County Health Rankings (CHRs). Our method relies on a factor analysis model to directly compute weights for our rankings, incorporate county population sizes into the variances, and allow for spillovers of health stock across county lines. We find that demographic and economic variation explain a large portion of the variation in health rankings. We address the importance of uncertainty caused by imputation of missing data and show that the use of rankings leads to inherently greater uncertainty. Analyzing the health of counties both within and across state lines shows substantial degrees of disparity. We find some disagreement between our ranks and the CHRs, but we show that much can be learned by combining results from both methods.

中文摘要

我们对美国各县的人口健康状况进行排名。我们使用了用于构建威斯康星大学人口健康研究所县健康排名（CHRs）的五个可观测的县健康变量。我们的方法依赖于因子分析模型来直接计算排名的权重，将县人口规模纳入方差，并允许健康存量跨县界溢出。我们发现人口和经济变化解释了健康排名变化的很大一部分。我们探讨了由缺失数据插补引起的不确定性的重要性，并表明使用排名会导致固有的更大不确定性。分析州内和跨州各县的健康状况显示出显著的不平等程度。我们发现我们的排名与CHRs之间存在一些分歧，但我们表明，结合两种方法的结果可以学到很多东西。

No. 35论文详情NBER w27258

Bank Market Power and Monetary Policy Transmission: Evidence from a Structural Estimation

银行市场势力与货币政策传导：来自结构估计的证据

Yifei Wang, Toni M. Whited, Yufeng Wu, Kairong Xiao

Abstract

We quantify the impact of bank market power on monetary policy transmission through banks to borrowers. We estimate a dynamic banking model in which monetary policy affects imperfectly competitive banks’ funding costs. Banks optimize the pass-through of these costs to borrowers and depositors, while facing capital and reserve regulation. We find that bank market power explains much of the transmission of monetary policy to borrowers, with an effect comparable to that of bank capital regulation. When the federal funds rate falls below 0.9%, market power interacts with bank capital regulation to produce a reversal of the effect of monetary policy.

中文摘要

我们量化了银行市场势力对通过银行向借款人传导货币政策的影响。我们估计了一个动态银行模型，其中货币政策影响不完全竞争银行的融资成本。银行在面临资本和准备金监管的同时，优化这些成本向借款人和存款人的传导。我们发现，银行市场势力解释了货币政策向借款人传导的很大一部分，其影响与银行资本监管的影响相当。当联邦基金利率降至0.9%以下时，市场势力与银行资本监管相互作用，导致货币政策效果发生逆转。

No. 36论文详情NBER w27257

Robust Identification of Investor Beliefs

投资者信念的稳健识别

Xiaohong Chen, Lars P. Hansen, Peter G. Hansen

Abstract

This paper develops a new method informed by data and models to recover information about investor beliefs. Our approach uses information embedded in forward-looking asset prices in conjunction with asset pricing models. We step back from presuming rational expectations and entertain potential belief distortions bounded by a statistical measure of discrepancy. Additionally, our method allows for the direct use of sparse survey evidence to make these bounds more informative. Within our framework, market-implied beliefs may differ from those implied by rational expectations due to behavioral/psychological biases of investors, ambiguity aversion, or omitted permanent components to valuation. Formally, we represent evidence about investor beliefs using a novel nonlinear expectation function deduced using model-implied moment conditions and bounds on statistical divergence. We illustrate our method with a prototypical example from macro-finance using asset market data to infer belief restrictions for macroeconomic growth rates.

中文摘要

本文开发了一种由数据和模型共同提供信息的新方法，以恢复关于投资者信念的信息。我们的方法利用前瞻性资产价格中嵌入的信息，并结合资产定价模型。我们不再预设理性预期，而是考虑由统计差异度量所约束的潜在信念扭曲。此外，我们的方法允许直接使用稀疏的调查证据，以使这些约束更具信息量。在我们的框架内，市场隐含的信念可能因投资者的行为/心理偏差、模糊厌恶或估值中遗漏的永久性成分而与理性预期隐含的信念不同。形式上，我们使用由模型隐含的矩条件和统计散度界限推导出的新颖非线性期望函数来表示关于投资者信念的证据。我们通过一个宏观金融的典型例子来说明我们的方法，该例子使用资产市场数据来推断宏观经济增速的信念约束。

No. 37论文详情NBER w27256

Banks as Lenders of First Resort: Evidence from the COVID-19 Crisis

银行作为第一贷款人：来自COVID-19危机的证据

Lei Li, Philip E. Strahan, Song Zhang

Abstract

In March of 2020, banks faced the largest increase in liquidity demands ever observed. Firms drew funds on a massive scale from pre-existing credit lines and loan commitments in anticipation of cash flow disruptions from the economic shutdown designed to contain the COVID-19 crisis. The increase in liquidity demands was concentrated at the largest banks, who serve the largest firms. Pre-crisis financial condition did not limit banks’ liquidity supply. Coincident inflows of funds to banks from both the Federal Reserve’s liquidity injection programs and from depositors, along with strong pre-shock bank capital, explain why banks were able to accommodate these liquidity demands.

中文摘要

2020年3月，银行面临有史以来最大的流动性需求增长。企业大规模从已有的信贷额度和贷款承诺中提取资金，以应对旨在遏制COVID-19危机的经济停摆所导致的现金流中断。流动性需求的增长集中在服务大型企业的大型银行。危机前的财务状况并未限制银行的流动性供给。来自美联储流动性注入计划和存款人的资金同时流入银行，加上危机前强劲的银行资本，解释了为什么银行能够满足这些流动性需求。

No. 38论文详情NBER w27255

Retaliatory Use of Public Standards in Trade

贸易中公共标准的报复性使用

Kjersti Nes, K Aleks Schaefer

Abstract

This research investigates the extent to which countries use public standards as a means of political retaliation in the international policy arena. We construct a dataset that matches the adoption of sanitary and phytosanitary (SPS) standards between 1996-2015 with SPS committee data on specific trade concerns and annual, bilateral trade flows. We evaluate the presence and frequency of retaliation by assessing the extent to which measures imposed by one country against another increase the probability that the country targeted by the original measure will respond with a measure of their own. We observe that this type of tit-for-tat behavior commonly occurred outside the product group of the original measure and for politically strategic goods. At the two-digit level, we find that about 3,000 bilateral trade flows globally--or just over $\$110$ billion in trade--were subject to retaliatory standards in 2015.

中文摘要

本研究调查了各国在国际政策领域中将公共标准用作政治报复手段的程度。我们构建了一个数据集，将1996年至2015年间卫生与植物卫生（SPS）标准的采用与SPS委员会关于特定贸易关切的数据以及年度双边贸易流相匹配。我们通过评估一国对另一国实施的措施在多大程度上增加了被措施针对国以自身措施回应的概率，来评估报复的存在和频率。我们观察到，这种针锋相对的行为通常发生在原始措施的产品组之外，并且针对政治战略商品。在两位码层面，我们发现2015年全球约有3000个双边贸易流——即略超过1100亿美元的贸易——受到了报复性标准的影响。

No. 39论文详情NBER w27254

Transportation Infrastructure in the US

美国的交通基础设施

Gilles Duranton, Geetika Nagpal, Matthew Turner

Abstract

Support for massive investments in transportation infrastructure, possibly with a change in the share of spending on transit, seems widespread. Such proposals are often motivated by the belief that our infrastructure is crumbling, that infrastructure causes economic growth, that current funding regimes disadvantage rural drivers at the expense of urban public transit, or that capacity expansions will reduce congestion. In fact, most US transportation infrastructure is not deteriorating and the existing scientific literature does not show that infrastructure creates growth or reduces congestion. However, current annual expenditure on public transit buses exceeds that on interstate construction and maintenance. A careful examination of how funding is allocated across modes is suggested by the evidence. Massive new expenditures are not.

中文摘要

对交通基础设施进行大规模投资的支持似乎很普遍，可能伴随着公共交通支出份额的变化。此类提议通常基于以下信念：我们的基础设施正在崩溃、基础设施能促进经济增长、当前的资金机制以牺牲城市公共交通为代价使农村司机处于不利地位，或者扩容将减少拥堵。事实上，美国大部分交通基础设施并未恶化，现有的科学文献并未表明基础设施能创造增长或减少拥堵。然而，目前每年在公共交通巴士上的支出超过了州际公路建设和维护的支出。证据表明，需要仔细审视资金如何在各种交通方式之间分配。大规模的新支出则并非必要。

No. 40论文详情NBER w27253

Competition Laws and Corporate Innovation

竞争法与公司创新

Ross Levine, Chen Lin, Lai Wei, Wensi Xie

Abstract

A central debate in economics concerns the relationship between competition and innovation, with some stressing that competition discourages innovation by reducing post-innovation rents and others emphasizing that more contestable markets spur currently dominant and other firms to invest more in innovation. We examine the impact of competition laws on innovation. We create a unique firm-level dataset on patenting activities that includes over 1.4 million firm-year observations, across 68 countries, from 1991 through 2015. Using a new, comprehensive dataset on competition laws, we find that more stringent competition laws are associated with increases in firms’ number of self-generated patents and the citation-impact and explorative nature of those patents. We also conduct the first examination of the relationship between competition laws and firms’ acquisition of patents from other firms. We find that competition increases patent acquisitions but lowers the ratio of acquired to self-generated patents. The results hold when using country-industry data on 186 countries over the 1888-2015 period.

中文摘要

经济学中的一个核心争论涉及竞争与创新之间的关系，一些人强调竞争通过减少创新后租金来抑制创新，而另一些人则强调更具竞争性的市场会促使当前占主导地位的公司和其他公司增加创新投入。我们研究了竞争法对创新的影响。我们创建了一个独特的公司层面专利活动数据集，涵盖了1991年至2015年间68个国家的超过140万个公司-年度观测值。利用一个新的、全面的竞争法数据集，我们发现更严格的竞争法与公司自主生成专利数量的增加、这些专利的引用影响和探索性性质的提升相关。我们还首次考察了竞争法与公司从其他公司收购专利之间的关系。我们发现竞争增加了专利收购，但降低了收购专利与自主生成专利的比率。在使用186个国家1888-2015年期间的国家-行业数据时，这些结果依然成立。

No. 41论文详情NBER w27252

Are Trade Agreements Good For You?

贸易协定对你有益吗？

Giovanni Maggi, Ralph Ossa

Abstract

We examine how deep agreements on domestic regulations affect welfare in a world where such agreements are influenced by producer lobbies. The answer to this question depends in a critical way on whether the agreement focuses on product standards or on production regulations. International cooperation on product standards can decrease welfare, and this is more likely to happen when producer lobbies are stronger. On the other hand, international cooperation on production regulations tends to enhance welfare when lobbying pressures are strong. A key determinant of the welfare impact of deep agreements is whether the interests of producer lobbies in different countries are aligned or in conflict: the former situation tends to occur in the case of product standards, while the latter situation tends to occur in the case of production regulations.

中文摘要

我们研究了在生产者游说团体影响下，关于国内法规的深度协定如何影响福利。这个问题的答案关键取决于协定关注的是产品标准还是生产法规。关于产品标准的国际合作可能降低福利，当生产者游说团体势力更强时，这种情况更可能发生。另一方面，当游说压力强大时，关于生产法规的国际合作往往能提升福利。深度协定福利影响的一个关键决定因素是不同国家生产者游说团体的利益是趋同还是冲突：前一种情况往往出现在产品标准方面，而后一种情况往往出现在生产法规方面。

No. 42论文详情NBER w27251

Cost Saving and the Freezing of Corporate Pension Plans

成本节约与企业养老金计划的冻结

Joshua D. Rauh, Irina Stefanescu, Stephen P. Zeldes

Abstract

Companies that freeze defined benefit pension plans save the equivalent of 13.5 percent of the long-horizon payroll of current employees. Furthermore, firms with higher prospective accruals are more likely to freeze their plans. Cost savings would not be possible in a benchmark model in which i) all workers receive compensation equal to their marginal product and ii) workers value equally all identical-cost forms of pension benefits. We find evidence consistent both with firms’ reneging on implicit contracts to provide workers with high pension accruals later in their careers and with shifts in employee valuation of different forms of retirement benefits.

中文摘要

冻结固定收益养老金计划的公司节省了相当于当前员工长期工资13.5%的成本。此外，预期应计养老金较高的公司更有可能冻结其计划。在一个基准模型中，成本节约是不可能的，该模型假设：i) 所有工人获得的报酬等于其边际产出，且 ii) 工人对所有成本相同的养老金福利形式给予同等价值。我们发现的证据既与公司违背隐性合同（即承诺在员工职业生涯后期提供高额养老金应计）一致，也与员工对不同形式退休福利的估值变化一致。

No. 43论文详情NBER w27250

Research Registries: Facts, Myths, and Possible Improvements

研究注册：事实、迷思与可能的改进

Eliot Abrams, Jonathan Libgober, John A. List

Abstract

The past few decades have ushered in an experimental revolution in economics whereby scholars are now much more likely to generate their own data. While there are virtues associated with this movement, there are concomitant difficulties. Several scientific disciplines, including economics, have launched research registries in an effort to attenuate key inferential issues. This study assesses registries both empirically and theoretically, with a special focus on the AEA registry. We find that over 90% of randomized control trials (RCTs) in economics do not register, only 50% of the RCTs that register do so before the intervention begins, and the majority of these preregistrations are not detailed enough to significantly aid inference. Our empirical analysis further shows that using other scientific registries as aspirational examples is misguided, as their perceived success in tackling the main issues is largely a myth. In light of these facts, we advance a simple economic model to explore potential improvements. A key insight from the model is that removal of the (current) option to register completed RCTs could increase the fraction of trials that register. We also argue that linking IRB applications to registrations could further increase registry effectiveness.

中文摘要

过去几十年，经济学领域掀起了一场实验革命，学者们现在更可能自行生成数据。尽管这一运动有其优点，但也伴随着困难。包括经济学在内的多个科学学科已启动研究注册，以努力缓解关键的推断问题。本研究从实证和理论两个角度评估了注册，特别关注美国经济学会（AEA）的注册。我们发现，经济学中超过90%的随机对照试验（RCT）没有注册，只有50%注册的RCT在干预开始前完成注册，并且这些预注册中的大多数不够详细，无法显著帮助推断。我们的实证分析进一步表明，将其他科学注册作为值得效仿的榜样是错误的，因为它们在解决主要问题上的所谓成功在很大程度上是一种迷思。基于这些事实，我们提出了一个简单的经济模型来探索可能的改进。模型的一个关键见解是，取消（当前）注册已完成RCT的选项，可能会提高注册试验的比例。我们还认为，将机构审查委员会（IRB）申请与注册联系起来，可以进一步提高注册的有效性。

No. 44论文详情NBER w27248

Panel Forecasts of Country-Level Covid-19 Infections

国家层面新冠肺炎感染的面板预测

Laura Liu, Hyungsik Roger Moon, Frank Schorfheide

Abstract

We use dynamic panel data models to generate density forecasts for daily Covid-19 infections for a panel of countries/regions. At the core of our model is a specification that assumes that the growth rate of active infections can be represented by autoregressive fluctuations around a downward sloping deterministic trend function with a break. Our fully Bayesian approach allows us to flexibly estimate the cross-sectional distribution of heterogeneous coefficients and then implicitly use this distribution as prior to construct Bayes forecasts for the individual time series. According to our model, there is a lot of uncertainty about the evolution of infection rates, due to parameter uncertainty and the realization of future shocks. We find that over a one-week horizon the empirical coverage frequency of our interval forecasts is close to the nominal credible level. Weekly forecasts from our model are published at https://laurayuliu.com/covid19-panel-forecast/.

中文摘要

我们使用动态面板数据模型，为一组国家/地区的每日新冠肺炎感染人数生成密度预测。我们模型的核心是一个设定，假设活跃感染增长率可以表示为围绕一个带有断点的向下倾斜确定性趋势函数的自回归波动。我们的全贝叶斯方法使我们能够灵活地估计异质性系数的横截面分布，然后隐含地使用该分布作为先验，为各个时间序列构建贝叶斯预测。根据我们的模型，由于参数不确定性和未来冲击的实现，感染率的演变存在很大的不确定性。我们发现，在一周的预测期内，我们区间预测的经验覆盖频率接近名义可信水平。我们模型的每周预测发布在 https://laurayuliu.com/covid19-panel-forecast/。

No. 45论文详情NBER w27247

A Unifying Approach to Measuring Climate Change Impacts and Adaptation

衡量气候变化影响与适应的统一方法

Antonio Bento, Noah S. Miller, Mehreen Mookerjee, Edson R. Severnini

Abstract

We develop a unifying approach to estimating climate impacts and adaptation, and apply it to study the impact of climate change on local air pollution. Economic agents are usually constrained when responding to daily weather shocks, but may adjust to long-run climatic changes. By simultaneously exploiting variation in weather and climate, we identify both the short- and long-run impacts on economic outcomes, and measure adaptation directly as the difference between those responses. As a result, we identify adaptation without making extrapolations of weather responses over time or space, and overcome omitted variable bias concerns in prior approaches.

中文摘要

我们开发了一种统一的方法来估计气候影响和适应，并将其应用于研究气候变化对当地空气污染的影响。经济主体通常在应对日常天气冲击时受到约束，但可能会适应长期的气候变化。通过同时利用天气和气候的变化，我们识别了其对经济结果的短期和长期影响，并直接衡量适应，即这些响应之间的差异。因此，我们无需对天气响应进行时间或空间上的外推即可识别适应，并克服了先前方法中遗漏变量偏差的问题。

No. 46论文详情NBER w27246

The Impacts of COVID-19 on Minority Unemployment: First Evidence from April 2020 CPS Microdata

COVID-19对少数族裔失业的影响：来自2020年4月当前人口调查微观数据的初步证据

Robert W. Fairlie, Kenneth Couch, Huanan Xu

Abstract

COVID-19 abruptly impacted the labor market with the unemployment rate jumping to 14.7 percent less than two months after state governments began adopting social distancing measures. Unemployment of this magnitude has not been seen since the Great Depression. This paper provides the first study of how the pandemic impacted minority unemployment using CPS microdata through April 2020. African-Americans experienced an increase in unemployment to 16.6 percent, less than anticipated based on previous recessions. In contrast, Latinx, with an unemployment rate of 18.2 percent, were disproportionately hard hit by COVID-19. Adjusting for concerns of the BLS regarding misclassification of unemployment, we create an upper-bound measure of the national unemployment rate of 26.5 percent, which is higher than the peak observed in the Great Depression. The April 2020 upper-bound unemployment rates are an alarming 31.8 percent for blacks and 31.4 percent for Latinx. Difference-in-difference estimates suggest that blacks were, at most, only slightly disproportionately impacted by COVID-19. Non-linear decomposition estimates indicate that a slightly favorable industry distribution partly protected them from being hit harder by COVID-19. The most impacted group are Latinx. Difference-in-difference estimates unequivocally indicate that Latinx were disproportionately impacted by COVID-19. An unfavorable occupational distribution and lower skills contributed to why Latinx experienced much higher unemployment rates than whites. These findings of early impacts of COVID-19 on unemployment raise important concerns about long-term economic effects for minorities.

中文摘要

COVID-19突然冲击了劳动力市场，在州政府开始采取社交距离措施后不到两个月，失业率飙升至14.7%。自大萧条以来，从未见过如此规模的失业。本文利用截至2020年4月的当前人口调查（CPS）微观数据，首次研究了疫情如何影响少数族裔失业。非裔美国人的失业率上升至16.6%，低于基于以往经济衰退的预期。相比之下，拉丁裔的失业率为18.2%，受到COVID-19的严重打击。考虑到美国劳工统计局（BLS）对失业错误分类的担忧，我们创建了全国失业率的上限衡量指标为26.5%，高于大萧条期间观察到的峰值。2020年4月，非裔美国人的上限失业率高达31.8%，拉丁裔为31.4%。双重差分估计表明，非裔美国人最多只受到COVID-19的轻微不成比例影响。非线性分解估计表明，略微有利的行业分布部分保护了他们免受COVID-19更严重的打击。受影响最大的群体是拉丁裔。双重差分估计明确表明，拉丁裔受到COVID-19的不成比例影响。不利的职业分布和较低的技能是导致拉丁裔失业率远高于白人的原因。这些关于COVID-19对失业早期影响的发现，引发了对少数族裔长期经济影响的重要担忧。

No. 47论文详情NBER w27245

Fatalism, Beliefs, and Behaviors During the COVID-19 Pandemic

COVID-19疫情期间的宿命论、信念与行为

Jesper Akesson, Sam Ashworth-Hayes, Robert Hahn, Robert D. Metcalfe, Itzhak Rasooly

Abstract

Little is known about how people’s beliefs concerning the Coronavirus Disease 2019 (COVID-19) influence their behavior. To shed light on this, we conduct an online experiment (n = 3,610) with US and UK residents. Participants are randomly allocated to a control group or to one of two treatment groups. The treatment groups are shown upperor lower-bound expert estimates of the infectiousness of the virus. We present three main empirical findings. First, individuals dramatically overestimate the dangerousness and infectiousness of COVID-19 relative to expert opinion. Second, providing people with expert information partially corrects their beliefs about the virus. Third, the more infectious people believe that COVID-19 is, the less willing they are to take protective measures, a finding we dub the “fatalism effect”. We develop a formal model that can explain the fatalism effect and discuss its implications for optimal policy during the pandemic.

中文摘要

关于人们对2019冠状病毒病（COVID-19）的信念如何影响其行为，目前知之甚少。为了阐明这一点，我们对美国和英国居民进行了一项在线实验（n = 3,610）。参与者被随机分配到对照组或两个处理组之一。处理组被展示专家对病毒传染性的上限或下限估计。我们提出三个主要的实证发现。首先，相对于专家意见，个体严重高估了COVID-19的危险性和传染性。其次，向人们提供专家信息可以部分纠正他们对病毒的信念。第三，人们认为COVID-19的传染性越强，他们就越不愿意采取保护措施，我们将这一发现称为“宿命论效应”。我们开发了一个形式化模型来解释宿命论效应，并讨论了其对疫情期间最优政策的启示。

No. 48论文详情NBER w27244

Reopening Scenarios

重启情景

David Baqaee, Emmanuel Farhi, Michael J. Mina, James H. Stock

Abstract

We use a five-age epidemiological model, combined with 66-sector economic accounting, to address a variety of questions concerning the economic reopening. We calibrate/estimate the model using contact survey data and data on weekly historical individual actions and non-pharmaceutical interventions in the weeks ending March 8 – May 16, 2020. Going forward, we model a decision-maker (governor) as following reopening guidelines like those proposed by the White House and the CDC. The sectoral accounting, combined with information on personal proximity and ability to work from home by sector, make it possible to construct a GDP-to-Risk index of which sectors provide the greatest increment in GDP per marginal increase in R0. Through simulations, we find that: a strong economic reopening is possible; a “smart” reopening, preferencing some sectors over others, makes only modest improvements over a broad reopening; and all this hinges on retaining strong restrictions on non-work social contacts. If non-work contacts – going to bars, shopping without social distancing and masks, large group gatherings, etc. – return only half-way to the pre-COVID-19 baseline, the current decline in deaths reverses leading to a second wave of business closures.

中文摘要

我们使用一个五年龄组流行病学模型，结合66个部门的经济核算，来解决关于经济重启的各种问题。我们利用接触调查数据以及截至2020年3月8日至5月16日这几周的每周历史个人行为和非药物干预数据，对模型进行校准/估计。展望未来，我们将决策者（州长）建模为遵循白宫和疾病控制与预防中心（CDC）提出的重启指南。部门核算，结合各部门的个人接触程度和居家办公能力信息，使得构建一个GDP-风险指数成为可能，该指数衡量哪些部门在每单位R0边际增加中贡献了最大的GDP增量。通过模拟，我们发现：强劲的经济重启是可能的；“智能”重启，即优先考虑某些部门而非其他部门，相对于广泛重启仅带来适度改善；而这一切都取决于对非工作社交接触保持严格限制。如果非工作接触——去酒吧、不保持社交距离和不戴口罩购物、大型团体聚会等——仅恢复到COVID-19前基线水平的一半，当前死亡人数的下降趋势就会逆转，导致第二波企业关闭。

No. 49论文详情NBER w27243

The Adverse Effect of the COVID-19 Labor Market Shock on Immigrant Employment

COVID-19劳动力市场冲击对移民就业的不利影响

George J. Borjas, Hugh Cassidy

Abstract

Employment rates in the United States fell dramatically between February 2020 and April 2020 as the repercussions of the COVID-19 pandemic reverberated through the labor market. This paper uses data from the CPS Basic Monthly Files to document that the employment decline was particularly severe for immigrants. Historically, immigrant men were more likely to be employed than native men. The COVID-related labor market disruptions eliminated the immigrant employment advantage. By April 2020, immigrant men had lower employment rates than native men. Part of the relative increase in the immigrant rate of job loss arises because immigrants were less likely to work in jobs that could be performed remotely and suffered disparate employment consequences as the lockdown permitted workers with more “remotable” skills to continue their work from home. Undocumented men were particularly hard hit by the pandemic, with their rate of job loss far exceeding the rate of job loss of legal immigrants.

中文摘要

2020年2月至4月期间，随着COVID-19疫情的影响波及劳动力市场，美国的就业率大幅下降。本文利用当前人口调查月度基础文件的数据，记录了移民就业下降尤为严重的情况。历史上，移民男性的就业率高于本土男性。与疫情相关的劳动力市场中断消除了移民的就业优势。到2020年4月，移民男性的就业率低于本土男性。移民失业率相对上升的部分原因在于，移民从事可远程完成工作的可能性较低，并且随着封锁措施允许拥有更多“可远程”技能的员工继续在家工作，他们遭受了不同的就业后果。无证移民男性受疫情冲击尤为严重，其失业率远超合法移民的失业率。

No. 50论文详情NBER w27242

Sufficient Statistics Revisited

充分统计量再探

Henrik Kleven

Abstract

This paper reviews and generalizes the sufficient statistics approach to policy evaluation. The idea of the approach is that the welfare effect of policy changes can be expressed in terms estimable reduced-form elasticities, allowing for policy evaluation without estimating the structural primitives of fully specified models. The approach relies on three assumptions: that policy changes are small, that government policy is the only source of market imperfection, and that a set of high-level restrictions on the environment and on preferences can be used to reduce the number of elasticities to be estimated. We generalize the approach in all three dimensions. It is possible to develop transparent sufficient statistics formulas under very general conditions, but the estimation requirements increase greatly. Starting from such general formulas elucidates that feasible empirical implementations are in fact structural approaches.

中文摘要

本文回顾并推广了政策评估的充分统计量方法。该方法的核心思想是，政策变化的福利效应可以用可估计的简化形式弹性来表示，从而无需估计完全指定模型的结构性基础即可进行政策评估。该方法依赖于三个假设：政策变化是微小的、政府政策是市场不完善的唯一来源、以及一组关于环境和偏好的高层次限制可用于减少需要估计的弹性数量。我们从所有三个维度推广了该方法。在非常一般的条件下，可以推导出透明的充分统计量公式，但估计要求大大增加。从这样的一般公式出发，阐明了可行的实证实施实际上就是结构性方法。

No. 51论文详情NBER w27241

Human Capital Investment in the Presence of Child Labor

存在童工情况下的人力资本投资

Natalie Bau, Martin Rotemberg, Manisha Shah, Bryce Steinberg

Abstract

Policies that improve human capital in early life are a promising tool for altering the lifelong trajectories of disadvantaged children. However, in many low-income countries, children and their parents face trade-offs between schooling and productive work. If there are positive returns to human capital in child labor, then children who receive more of some types of early life investments, such as those that improve health or nutrition, may attend less school. Exploiting early life rainfall shocks in India as a source of exogenous variation in early life investment, we show that child labor attenuates the positive effects of early life investment and increased early life investment increases school dropout in districts with high child labor. This lower investment in education has persistent long-term consequences in adulthood, resulting in lower household consumption. We show that our results are robust to instrumenting for child labor prevalence using local crop mix. Reductions in educational investment in response to positive early life shocks appear to reduce overall welfare in high-child labor districts.

中文摘要

改善儿童早期人力资本的政策是改变弱势儿童终身轨迹的有前景工具。然而，在许多低收入国家，儿童及其父母面临上学与生产性工作之间的权衡。如果童工中的人力资本存在正回报，那么接受更多某些类型早期投资（如改善健康或营养的投资）的儿童可能上学更少。利用印度早期降雨冲击作为早期投资的外生变异来源，我们表明童工削弱了早期投资的积极效应，并且在童工率高的地区，早期投资的增加反而提高了辍学率。这种教育投资的减少在成年期产生了持续的长期后果，导致家庭消费降低。我们证明，使用当地作物组合作为童工流行率的工具变量，结果依然稳健。在童工率高的地区，对积极早期冲击的教育投资减少似乎降低了整体福利。

No. 52论文详情NBER w27240

Persistent Effects of Violent Media Content

暴力媒体内容的持续影响

Jason M. Lindo, Isaac D. Swensen, Glen R. Waddell

Abstract

We document the immediate and long-term effects of violent media. Specifically, we evaluate the effects of The Ultimate Fighter, a hit TV show that features fighters competing in violent mixed martial arts and which brought Ultimate Fighting Championship into the mainstream. We estimate the effect of early exposure to this show using panel data from police agencies across the United States and a strategy that uses network ratings prior to the show's premier as an instrumental variable. We show that early exposure significantly reduced crime: these effects are particularly evident for assault, began in the month the show premiered, and persisted for many years. These estimates do not reflect systematic differences across geographic areas in their trends in crime rates prior to 2005. To complement our main results, we also investigate the effects of "UFC Main Events," which air in bars and on Pay-Per-View. This analysis additionally suggests reductions in violence caused by viewership.

中文摘要

我们记录了暴力媒体的即时和长期影响。具体而言，我们评估了《终极斗士》的效果，这是一档热门电视节目，以选手参加暴力综合格斗为特色，并将终极格斗锦标赛带入主流。我们利用美国各地警察机构的面板数据，以及以节目首播前网络收视率作为工具变量的策略，估计了早期接触该节目的影响。我们表明，早期接触显著减少了犯罪：这些影响在袭击案件中尤为明显，始于节目首播当月，并持续多年。这些估计并不反映2005年之前各地区犯罪率趋势的系统性差异。为补充主要结果，我们还调查了在酒吧和按次付费频道播出的“UFC主赛”的影响。这一分析进一步表明，观看节目导致了暴力行为的减少。
