DEglobalizaion and Social Safety Nets in Post-Covid-19 Era: Textbook Macroeconomic Analysis

后疫情时代的去全球化与社会安全网：教科书式宏观经济分析

Assaf Razin, Efraim Sadka, Alexander Horst Schwemmer

Abstract

Globalization is expected to be reversed, at least partially, in the post pandemic era. The Great Financial Recession of 2008–10 marked a historic turning point in the direction of weakening the degree of global economic integration. Now, in the post-pandemic era, policymakers appear poised to take deliberate steps to reinforce the movement toward de-globalization. At the same time, safety nets are expected to be strengthened. In this paper, we develop a model, with which we analyze central macroeconomic interactions between globalization and safety nets. We put together stylized elements of trade globalization, financial globalization, international tax competition, immigration, and welfare state, all in a two-skill, two-period stylized model, where policy (taxes and social benefits) is determined through majority voting.

中文摘要

预计在后疫情时代，全球化将至少部分逆转。2008-10年的金融危机标志着全球经济一体化程度减弱方向上的历史转折点。如今，在后疫情时代，政策制定者似乎准备采取审慎措施，以加强去全球化趋势。与此同时，安全网预计将得到加强。在本文中，我们构建了一个模型，用以分析全球化与社会安全网之间的核心宏观经济互动。我们在一个两技能、两时期的简化模型中，整合了贸易全球化、金融全球化、国际税收竞争、移民和福利国家的典型要素，其中政策（税收和社会福利）通过多数投票决定。

No. 54论文详情NBER w27238

The Seeds of Ideology: Historical Immigration and Political Preferences in the United States

意识形态的种子：美国历史上的移民与政治偏好

Paola Giuliano, Marco Tabellini

Abstract

We test the relationship between historical immigration to the United States and political ideology today. We hypothesize that European immigrants brought with them their preferences for the welfare state, and that this had a long-lasting effect on the political ideology of US born individuals. Our analysis proceeds in three steps. First, we document that the historical presence of European immigrants is associated with a more liberal political ideology and with stronger preferences for redistribution among US born individuals today. Next, we show that this correlation is not driven by the characteristics of the counties where immigrants settled or other specific, socioeconomic immigrants’ traits. Finally, we conjecture and provide evidence that immigrants brought with them their preferences for the welfare state from their countries of origin. Consistent with the hypothesis that immigration left its footprint on American ideology via cultural transmission from immigrants to natives, we show that our results are stronger when inter-group contact between natives and immigrants, measured with either intermarriage or residential integration, was higher. Our findings also indicate that immigrants influenced American political ideology during one of the largest episodes of redistribution in US history — the New Deal – and that such effects persisted after the initial shock.

中文摘要

我们检验了美国历史上的移民与当今政治意识形态之间的关系。我们假设欧洲移民带来了他们对福利国家的偏好，并且这对美国出生个体的政治意识形态产生了长期影响。我们的分析分三步进行。首先，我们记录了欧洲移民的历史存在与当今美国出生个体中更自由的政治意识形态以及对再分配的更强偏好之间的关联。其次，我们表明这种相关性并非由移民定居的县的特征或其他特定的社会经济移民特征所驱动。最后，我们推测并提供证据表明，移民从原籍国带来了他们对福利国家的偏好。与移民通过文化传播将意识形态印记留给本土居民的假设一致，我们表明，当本土居民与移民之间的群体间接触（以通婚或居住融合衡量）更高时，我们的结果更强。我们的发现还表明，移民在美国历史上最大的再分配事件之一——新政期间影响了美国政治意识形态，并且这种影响在初始冲击后持续存在。

No. 55论文详情NBER w27237

The Persuasive Effect of Fox News: Non-Compliance with Social Distancing During the Covid-19 Pandemic

福克斯新闻的说服效应：COVID-19疫情期间不遵守社交距离的行为

Andrey Simonov, Szymon K. Sacher, Jean-Pierre H. Dubé, Shirsho Biswas

Abstract

We test for and measure the effects of cable news in the US on regional differences in compliance with recommendations by health experts to practice social distancing during the early stages of the COVID-19 pandemic. We use a quasi-experimental design to estimate the causal effect of Fox News viewership on stay-at-home behavior by using only the incremental local viewership due to the quasi-random assignment of channel positions in a local cable line-up. We find that a 10% increase in Fox News cable viewership (approximately 0:13 higher viewer rating points) leads to a 1.3 percentage point reduction in the propensity to stay at home. We find a persuasion rate of Fox News on non-compliance with stay-at-home behavior during the crisis of about 5:7% - 28:4% across our various social distancing metrics.

中文摘要

我们检验并衡量了美国有线电视新闻对COVID-19疫情早期阶段各地区遵守卫生专家社交距离建议程度差异的影响。我们采用准实验设计，利用当地有线电视节目表中频道位置的准随机分配所导致的福克斯新闻本地收视率增量，来估计福克斯新闻收视率对居家行为的因果效应。我们发现，福克斯新闻有线电视收视率每增加10%（约0.13个收视率点），居家倾向降低1.3个百分点。我们计算出，在危机期间，福克斯新闻对不遵守居家行为的不服从说服率，在我们各种社交距离指标中约为5.7%至28.4%。

No. 56论文详情NBER w27236

Mobility Zones

流动区域

Ferdinando Monte

Abstract

This short note constructs Mobility Zones to facilitate the discussion on the geographic extent of individual mobility restrictions to control the spread of Covid-19. Mobility Zones are disjoint sets of counties where a given level of individual mobility directly or indirectly connects all counties within each set. I compute Mobility Zones for the United States and each state using smartphone-based mobility data between counties. The average area and population of Mobility Zones have slightly grown at the onset of the epidemic and have sharply shrunk afterward. Pre-Covid-19 Mobility Zones may be useful in calibrating quantitative studies of targeted restriction policies, or for policymakers deciding on the adoption of specific mobility measures. Two examples suggest the use of Mobility Zones to inform within-state differences and cross-state coordination in mobility restriction policies.

中文摘要

这篇短评构建了流动区域，以促进关于控制COVID-19传播的个人流动限制地理范围的讨论。流动区域是不相交的县集合，其中给定水平的个人流动性直接或间接连接每个集合内的所有县。我利用县际智能手机流动性数据，为美国和各州计算了流动区域。流动区域的平均面积和人口在疫情初期略有增长，之后急剧缩小。COVID-19之前的流动区域可能有助于校准针对限制政策的定量研究，或为政策制定者决定采用特定流动措施提供参考。两个例子表明，流动区域可用于指导州内差异和跨州协调的流动限制政策。

Impacts of State Reopening Policy on Human Mobility

州重新开放政策对人口流动性的影响

Thuy D. Nguyen, Sumedha Gupta, Martin Andersen, Ana Bento, Kosali I. Simon, Coady Wing

Abstract

This study quantifies the effect of state reopening policies on daily mobility, travel, and mixing behavior during the COVID-19 pandemic. We harness cell device signal data to examine the effects of the timing and pace of reopening plans in different states. We quantify the increase in mobility patterns during the reopening phase by a broad range of cell-device-based metrics. Soon (four days) after reopening, we observe a 6% to 8% mobility increase. In addition, we find that temperature and precipitation are strongly associated with increased mobility across counties. The mobility measures that reflect visits to a greater variety of locations responds the most to reopening policies, while total time in vs. outside the house remains unchanged. The largest increases in mobility occur in states that were late adopters of closure measures, suggesting that closure policies may have represented more of a binding constraint in those states. Together, these four observations provide an assessment of the extent to which people in the U.S. are resuming movement and physical proximity as the COVID-19 pandemic continues.

中文摘要

本研究量化了COVID-19疫情期间州重新开放政策对日常流动性、出行和混合行为的影响。我们利用手机设备信号数据，考察不同州重新开放计划的时间和节奏所产生的影响。通过一系列基于手机设备的指标，我们量化了重新开放阶段流动性模式的增加。在重新开放后不久（四天内），我们观察到流动性增加了6%至8%。此外，我们发现温度和降水量与各县流动性的增加密切相关。反映访问更多种类地点的流动性指标对重新开放政策的反应最为显著，而在室内与室外总时间保持不变。流动性增长最大的州是那些较晚采取封锁措施的州，这表明封锁政策在这些州可能代表了更具约束性的限制。综合这四项观察结果，我们评估了在COVID-19疫情持续期间，美国人恢复出行和身体接近程度的程度。

No. 58论文详情NBER w27234

Why Has the US Economy Recovered So Consistently from Every Recession in the Past 70 Years?

为什么美国经济在过去70年中每次衰退后都能如此一致地复苏？

Robert E. Hall, Marianna Kudlyak

Abstract

A remarkable fact about the historical US business cycle is that, after unemployment reached its peak in a recession, and a recovery begins, the annual reduction in the unemployment rate is stable at around one tenth of the current level of unemployment. We document this fact in a companion paper, Hall and Kudlyak (2020a). Here, we consider explanations for the surprising consistency of recoveries. We show that the evolution of the labor market from recession to recovery involves more than the direct effect of persistent unemployment of job-losers from the recession shock -- unemployment during the recovery is above normal for people who did not lose jobs during the recession. We explore models of the labor market's self-recovery that imply gradual working off of unemployment following a recession shock. We emphasize the feedback from high unemployment to the forces driving job creation. These models also explain why the recovery of market-wide unemployment is so much slower than the rate at which individual unemployed workers find new jobs. The reasons include the fact that the path that individual job-losers follow back to stable employment often includes several brief interim jobs.

中文摘要

关于美国历史商业周期的一个显著事实是，在失业率于衰退中达到峰值并开始复苏后，失业率的年降幅稳定在当前失业水平的大约十分之一。我们在配套论文Hall and Kudlyak (2020a)中记录了这一事实。在此，我们探讨复苏惊人一致性的解释。我们表明，从衰退到复苏的劳动力市场演变不仅涉及衰退冲击中失业者持续失业的直接影响——复苏期间的失业率对于在衰退期间未失业的人群也高于正常水平。我们探索劳动力市场自我恢复的模型，这些模型暗示衰退冲击后失业会逐渐消除。我们强调高失业率对推动就业创造力量的反馈作用。这些模型也解释了为什么整个市场的失业率恢复速度远慢于个体失业工人找到新工作的速度。原因包括个体失业者回归稳定就业的路径通常包含几个短暂的临时工作。

No. 59论文详情NBER w27233

Three Myths about Federal Regulation

关于联邦监管的三个迷思

Patrick A. McLaughlin, Casey B. Mulligan

Abstract

Despite evidence to the contrary, three common myths persist about federal regulations. The first myth is that many regulations concern the environment, but in fact only a small minority of regulations are environmental. The second myth is that most regulations contain quantitative estimates of costs or benefits. However, these quantitative estimates appear rarely in published rules, contradicting the impression given by executive orders and Office of Management and Budget guidance, which require cost-benefit analysis (CBA) and clearly articulate sound economic principles for conducting CBA. Environmental rules have relatively higher-quality CBAs, at least by the low standards of other federal rules. The third myth, which is particularly relevant to the historic regulations promulgated during the COVID-19 pandemic, is the misperception that regulatory costs are primarily clerical, rather than opportunity or resource costs. If technocrats have triumphed in the regulatory arena, their victory has not been earned by the merits of their analysis.

中文摘要

尽管有相反证据，关于联邦监管的三个常见迷思仍然存在。第一个迷思是许多监管涉及环境，但实际上只有少数监管是环境相关的。第二个迷思是大多数监管包含成本或收益的定量估计。然而，这些定量估计在已发布的规则中很少出现，这与要求成本效益分析（CBA）并明确阐述进行CBA的合理经济原则的行政命令和管理与预算办公室指导相矛盾。环境规则具有相对较高质量的CBA，至少按其他联邦规则的低标准来看如此。第三个迷思，尤其与COVID-19疫情期间颁布的历史性监管相关，是错误认为监管成本主要是文书成本，而非机会成本或资源成本。如果技术官僚在监管领域取得了胜利，他们的胜利并非因其分析的价值而赢得。

No. 60论文详情NBER w27232

The Hammer and the Scalpel: On the Economics of Indiscriminate versus Targeted Isolation Policies during Pandemics

锤子与手术刀：论大流行期间无差别与针对性隔离政策的经济学

Varadarajan V. Chari, Rishabh Kirpalani, Christopher Phelan

Abstract

We develop a simple dynamic economic model of epidemic transmission designed to be consistent with widely used SIR biological models of the transmission of epidemics, while incorporating economic benefits and costs as well. Our main finding is that targeted testing and isolation policies deliver large welfare gains relative to optimal policies when these tools are not used. Specifically, we find that when testing and isolation are not used, optimal policy delivers a welfare gain equivalent to a 0.6% permanent increase in consumption relative to no intervention. The welfare gain arises because under the optimal policy, the planner engineers a sharp recession that reduces aggregate output by about 40% for about 3 months. This sharp contraction in economic activity reduces the rate of transmission and reduces cumulative deaths by about 0.1%. When testing policies are used, optimal policy delivers a welfare gain equivalent to a 3% permanent increase in consumption. The associated recession is milder in that aggregate output declines by about 15% and cumulative deaths are reduced by .3%. Much of this welfare gain comes from isolating infected individuals. When individuals who are suspected to be infected are isolated without any testing, optimal policy delivers a welfare gain equivalent to a 2% increase in permanent consumption.

中文摘要

我们开发了一个简单的流行病传播动态经济模型，旨在与广泛使用的流行病传播SIR生物模型保持一致，同时纳入经济收益和成本。我们的主要发现是，当不使用这些工具时，与最优政策相比，有针对性的检测和隔离政策能带来巨大的福利收益。具体来说，我们发现当不使用检测和隔离时，最优政策带来的福利收益相当于永久性消费增加0.6%，相对于不干预。福利收益的产生是因为在最优政策下，规划者设计了一场急剧的衰退，使总产出在大约3个月内减少约40%。这种经济活动的急剧收缩降低了传播率，并使累计死亡人数减少约0.1%。当使用检测政策时，最优政策带来的福利收益相当于永久性消费增加3%。相关的衰退较为温和，总产出下降约15%，累计死亡人数减少0.3%。这一福利收益的大部分来自隔离感染者。当疑似感染者未经检测就被隔离时，最优政策带来的福利收益相当于永久性消费增加2%。

No. 61论文详情NBER w27231

The Term Structure of Covered Interest Rate Parity Violations

覆盖利率平价违反的期限结构

Patrick Augustin, Mikhail Chernov, Lukas Schmid, Dongho Song

Abstract

We quantify the impact of risk-based and non-risk-based intermediary constraints (IC) on the term structure of CIP violations. Using a stochastic discount factor (SDF) inferred from interest rate swaps, we value currency derivatives. The wedge between model-implied and observed derivative prices reflects the impact of non-risk-based IC because our SDF incorporates risk-based IC. There is no wedge at short horizons, while the wedge accounts for 40% of long-term CIP violations. Consistent with IC theory, the wedge correlates with the shadow cost of intermediary capital, and the SDF-implied interest rate is a weighted average of collateralized and uncollateralized interest rates.

中文摘要

我们量化了基于风险和非基于风险的中介约束（IC）对CIP违反期限结构的影响。使用从利率互换推断出的随机贴现因子（SDF），我们对货币衍生品进行估值。模型隐含衍生品价格与观察到的衍生品价格之间的楔子反映了非基于风险IC的影响，因为我们的SDF包含了基于风险的IC。在短期期限上不存在楔子，而楔子占长期CIP违反的40%。与IC理论一致，楔子与中介资本的影子成本相关，且SDF隐含利率是抵押和无抵押利率的加权平均值。

No. 62论文详情NBER w27230

Spatial Misallocation in Chinese Housing and Land Markets

中国住房和土地市场中的空间错配

Yongheng Deng, Yang Tang, Ping Wang, Jing Wu

Abstract

Housing and land prices in China have experienced dramatic hikes over the past decade or two. Moreover, housing and land prices have also become more dispersed across Chinese cities. This paper intends to explore how housing and land market frictions may affect not only the aggregate but also the spatial distribution of housing and land prices and hence the extent of spatial misallocation. We first document the spatial variations of housing and land market frictions. In particular, larger tier-1 cities receive less housing and land subsidies, compared to tier-2 and tier-3 cities, whereas land frictions have been mitigated over time. We then embed both types of market frictions into a dynamic competitive spatial equilibrium framework featured with endogenous rural-urban migration. The calibrated model can reasonably mimic the price hikes in the data. Our counterfactual analysis reveals that, in a frictionless economy, the levels of housing and land prices would both be higher; while the housing price hike would slow down, the land price would grow more rapidly. Moreover, the housing price would not be slow down unless housing frictions can be largely mitigated.

中文摘要

过去一二十年间，中国住房和土地价格经历了急剧上涨。此外，住房和土地价格在中国城市间的分散程度也有所增加。本文旨在探讨住房和土地市场摩擦如何不仅影响住房和土地价格的总体水平，还影响其空间分布，进而影响空间错配的程度。我们首先记录了住房和土地市场摩擦的空间差异。特别是，与二线和三线城市相比，较大的一线城市获得的住房和土地补贴较少，而土地摩擦随时间推移已有所缓解。然后，我们将这两种市场摩擦嵌入一个以城乡内生迁移为特征的动态竞争性空间均衡框架中。校准后的模型能够合理模拟数据中的价格上涨。我们的反事实分析表明，在无摩擦经济中，住房和土地价格水平都会更高；而住房价格上涨速度会放缓，土地价格则会增长更快。此外，除非住房摩擦得到大幅缓解，否则住房价格不会放缓。

No. 63论文详情NBER w27229

Were Urban Cowboys Enough to Control COVID-19? Local Shelter-in-Place Orders and Coronavirus Case Growth

城市牛仔足以控制COVID-19吗？地方居家令与冠状病毒病例增长

Dhaval M. Dave, Andrew I. Friedson, Kyutaro Matsuzawa, Joseph J. Sabia, Samuel Safford

Abstract

One of the most common policy prescriptions to reduce the spread of COVID-19 has been to legally enforce social distancing through state or local shelter-in-place orders (SIPOs). This paper is the first to explore the comparative effectiveness of early county-level SIPOs versus later statewide mandates in curbing COVID-19 growth. We exploit the unique laboratory of Texas, a state in which the early adoption of local SIPOs by densely populated counties covered almost two-thirds of the state’s population prior to Texas’s adoption of a statewide SIPO on April 2, 2020. Using an event study framework, we document that countywide SIPO adoption is associated with a 14 percent increase in the percent of residents who remain at home full-time, a social distancing effect that is largest in urbanized and densely populated counties. Then, we find that in early adopting counties, COVID-19 case growth fell by 19 to 26 percentage points two-and-a-half weeks following adoption of a SIPO, a result robust to controls for county-level heterogeneity in outbreak timing, coronavirus testing, and border SIPO policies. This effect is driven nearly entirely by highly urbanized and densely populated counties. We find that approximately 90 percent of the curbed growth in COVID-19 cases in Texas came from the early adoption of SIPOs by urbanized counties, suggesting that the later statewide shelter-in-place mandate yielded relatively few health benefits.

中文摘要

减少COVID-19传播最常见的政策处方之一是通过州或地方居家令（SIPO）依法强制实施社交距离。本文首次探讨了早期县级居家令与后期全州强制令在遏制COVID-19增长方面的相对有效性。我们利用了德克萨斯州这一独特实验室，该州人口密集县早期采用的地方居家令在2020年4月2日德克萨斯州采用全州居家令之前覆盖了该州近三分之二的人口。使用事件研究框架，我们记录了全县居家令的采用与全职居家居民比例增加14%相关，这一社交距离效应在城市化且人口密集的县最为显著。然后，我们发现，在早期采用居家令的县，采用居家令后两周半，COVID-19病例增长率下降了19至26个百分点，这一结果在控制县级疫情爆发时间、冠状病毒检测和边境居家令政策的异质性后依然稳健。这一效应几乎完全由高度城市化和人口密集的县驱动。我们发现，德克萨斯州COVID-19病例增长受抑制的约90%来自城市化县早期采用居家令，这表明后来的全州居家令强制令带来的健康益处相对较少。

No. 64论文详情NBER w27228

The Macroeconomics of a Pandemic: A Minimalist Model

大流行的宏观经济学：一个极简模型

Luis Felipe Céspedes, Roberto Chang, Andrés Velasco

Abstract

We build a minimalist model of the macroeconomics of a pandemic, with two essential components. The first is productivity-related: if the virus forces firms to shed labor beyond a certain threshold, productivity suffers. The second component is a credit market imperfection: because lenders cannot be sure a borrower will repay, they only lend against collateral. Expected productivity determines collateral value; in turn, collateral value can limit borrowing and productivity. As a result, adverse shocks have large magnification effects, in an unemployment and asset price deflation doom loop. There may be multiple equilibria, so that pessimistic expectations can push the economy to a bad equilibrium with limited borrowing and low employment and productivity. The model helps identify policies to fight the effects of the pandemic. Traditional expansionary fiscal policy has no beneficial effects, while cutting interest rates has a limited effect if the initial real interest rate is low. By contrast, several unconventional policies, including wage subsidies, helicopter drops of liquid assets, equity injections, and loan guarantees, can keep the economy in a full-employment, high-productivity equilibrium. Such policies can be fiscally expensive, so their implementation is feasible only with ample fiscal space or emergency financing from abroad.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个大流行宏观经济学的极简模型，包含两个基本组成部分。第一个与生产率相关：如果病毒迫使企业解雇劳动力超过一定阈值，生产率就会受损。第二个组成部分是信贷市场不完善：因为贷款人无法确定借款人是否会偿还，他们只以抵押品为条件放贷。预期生产率决定抵押品价值；反过来，抵押品价值可能限制借贷和生产率。结果，不利冲击具有巨大的放大效应，形成失业和资产价格通缩的厄运循环。可能存在多重均衡，因此悲观预期可能将经济推向借贷有限、就业和生产率低下的坏均衡。该模型有助于确定对抗大流行影响的政策。传统扩张性财政政策没有有益效果，而如果初始实际利率较低，降息效果有限。相比之下，几种非常规政策，包括工资补贴、直升机撒钱注入流动资产、股权注入和贷款担保，可以使经济保持在充分就业、高生产率的均衡中。此类政策可能在财政上代价高昂，因此其实施只有在拥有充足财政空间或来自国外的紧急融资时才可行。

No. 65论文详情NBER w27227

Necessary Evidence For A Risk Factor’s Relevance

风险因子相关性的必要证据

Alexander M. Chinco, Samuel M. Hartzmark, Abigail B. Sussman

Abstract

Textbook finance theory assumes that investors strategically try to insure themselves against bad future states of the world when forming portfolios. This is a testable assumption, surveys are ideally suited to test it, and we develop a framework for doing so. Our framework combines survey experiments with field data to test this assumption as it pertains to any candidate risk factor. We study consumption growth to demonstrate the approach. While participants strategically respond to changes in the mean and volatility of stock returns when forming their portfolios, there is no evidence that investors view this canonical risk factor as relevant.

中文摘要

教科书金融理论假设投资者在构建投资组合时，会策略性地试图为未来不利的世界状态提供保障。这是一个可检验的假设，调查非常适合检验它，我们为此开发了一个框架。我们的框架将调查实验与实地数据相结合，以检验这一假设，该假设适用于任何候选风险因子。我们通过研究消费增长来演示该方法。虽然参与者在构建投资组合时会策略性地应对股票收益均值和波动率的变化，但没有证据表明投资者认为这一经典风险因子具有相关性。

No. 66论文详情NBER w27226

Bounding the Predictive Values of COVID-19 Antibody Tests

COVID-19抗体检测预测值的界限确定

Charles F. Manski

Abstract

COVID-19 antibody tests have imperfect accuracy. There has been lack of clarity on the meaning of reported rates of false positives and false negatives. For risk assessment and clinical decision making, the rates of interest are the positive and negative predictive values of a test. Positive predictive value (PPV) is the chance that a person who tests positive has been infected. Negative predictive value (NPV) is the chance that someone who tests negative has not been infected. The medical literature regularly reports different statistics, sensitivity and specificity. Sensitivity is the chance that an infected person receives a positive test result. Specificity is the chance that a non-infected person receives a negative result. Knowledge of sensitivity and specificity permits one to predict the test result given a person’s true infection status. These predictions are not directly relevant to risk assessment or clinical decisions, where one knows a test result and wants to predict whether a person has been infected. Given estimates of sensitivity and specificity, PPV and NPV can be derived if one knows the prevalence of the disease, the rate of illness in the population. There is considerable uncertainty about the prevalence of COVID-19. This paper addresses the problem of inference on the PPV and NPV of COVID-19 antibody tests given estimates of sensitivity and specificity and credible bounds on prevalence. I explain the methodological problem, show how to estimate bounds on PPV and NPV, and apply the findings to some tests authorized by the FDA.

中文摘要

COVID-19抗体检测的准确性并非完美。关于报告的假阳性和假阴性率的含义一直缺乏清晰性。对于风险评估和临床决策，人们关注的是检测的阳性预测值和阴性预测值。阳性预测值是指检测呈阳性的人实际被感染的概率。阴性预测值是指检测呈阴性的人实际未被感染的概率。医学文献通常报告不同的统计量，即敏感性和特异性。敏感性是指感染者获得阳性检测结果的概率。特异性是指未感染者获得阴性结果的概率。了解敏感性和特异性，可以根据一个人的真实感染状态预测检测结果。这些预测与风险评估或临床决策并不直接相关，因为在临床决策中，人们已知检测结果，并希望预测一个人是否被感染。在已知敏感性和特异性估计值的情况下，如果知道疾病的患病率（即人群中的发病率），就可以推导出阳性预测值和阴性预测值。COVID-19的患病率存在相当大的不确定性。本文探讨了在给定敏感性和特异性估计值以及患病率的可信界限下，对COVID-19抗体检测的阳性预测值和阴性预测值进行推断的问题。我解释了方法论问题，展示了如何估计阳性预测值和阴性预测值的界限，并将研究结果应用于一些经FDA授权的检测。

No. 67论文详情NBER w27225

Deputization

授权代理

Bruce I. Carlin, Tarik Umar, Hanyi Yi

Abstract

A policy of deputization asks agents to monitor others without providing explicit incentives. It is often used to prevent dangerous activities. To calibrate whether and why it works, we study recent laws that deputized financial professionals to help fight elder financial abuse. We show deputization led to a 4%-6% decrease in suspected cases and a 4.5% drop in personal bankruptcies. Women, minorities, and unmarried people benefited more. Effectiveness operated through higher community-mindedness and deeper social connections. Egoistic incentives, legal concerns, publicity, and religiosity were less important. This suggests that regulators can rely on social networks to solve tough problems.

中文摘要

授权代理政策要求代理人监督他人，而不提供明确的激励措施。它通常用于预防危险活动。为了校准其是否有效以及为何有效，我们研究了近期授权金融专业人士协助打击老年人金融虐待的法律。我们发现，授权代理导致疑似案件减少4%-6%，个人破产率下降4.5%。女性、少数族裔和未婚人士受益更多。其有效性通过更高的社区意识和更深的社会联系发挥作用。利己激励、法律顾虑、宣传和宗教信仰的重要性较低。这表明监管机构可以依赖社会网络来解决棘手问题。

No. 68论文详情NBER w27224

Global Supply Chains in the Pandemic

疫情中的全球供应链

Barthélémy Bonadio, Zhen Huo, Andrei A. Levchenko, Nitya Pandalai-Nayar

Abstract

We study the role of global supply chains in the impact of the Covid-19 pandemic on GDP growth using a multi-sector quantitative framework implemented on 64 countries. We discipline the labor supply shock across sectors and countries using the fraction of work in the sector that can be done from home, interacted with the stringency with which countries imposed lockdown measures. One quarter of the total model-implied real GDP decline is due to transmission through global supply chains. However, “renationalization” of global supply chains does not in general make countries more resilient to pandemic-induced contractions in labor supply. This is because eliminating reliance on foreign inputs increases reliance on the domestic inputs, which are also disrupted due to nationwide lockdowns. In fact, trade can insulate a country imposing a stringent lockdown from the pandemic-shock, as its foreign inputs are less disrupted than its domestic ones. Finally, unilateral lifting of the lockdowns in the largest economies can contribute as much as 2.5%to GDP growth in some of their smaller trade partners.

中文摘要

我们利用一个基于64个国家的多部门量化框架，研究了全球供应链在COVID-19疫情对GDP增长影响中的作用。我们使用部门工作中可居家完成的比例，与国家实施封锁措施的严格程度进行交互，来约束跨部门和跨国家的劳动力供给冲击。模型隐含的实际GDP下降总额中，有四分之一是由于通过全球供应链的传导所致。然而，全球供应链的“再国有化”通常并不会使各国对疫情引发的劳动力供给收缩更具韧性。这是因为消除对外国投入的依赖会增加对国内投入的依赖，而国内投入也因全国性封锁而受到干扰。事实上，贸易可以使实施严格封锁的国家免受疫情冲击的影响，因为其外国投入受到的干扰小于国内投入。最后，最大经济体的单方面解除封锁，可以为其一些较小贸易伙伴的GDP增长贡献高达2.5%。

No. 69论文详情NBER w27223

Voluntary Regulation: Evidence from Medicare Payment Reform

自愿监管：来自医疗保险支付改革的证据

Liran Einav, Amy Finkelstein, Yunan Ji, Neale Mahoney

Abstract

Government programs are often offered on an optional basis to market participants. We explore the economics of such voluntary regulation in the context of a Medicare payment reform, in which one medical provider receives a single, predetermined payment for a sequence of related healthcare services, instead of separate service-specific payments. This “bundled payment” program was originally implemented as a 5-year randomized trial, with mandatory participation by hospitals assigned to the new payment model, but after two years participation was unexpectedly made voluntary for half of these hospitals. Using detailed claim-level data, we document that voluntary participation is more likely for hospitals who can increase revenue without changing behavior (“selection on levels”) and for hospitals that had large changes in behavior when participation was mandatory (“selection on slopes”). To assess outcomes under counterfactual regimes, we estimate a simple model of responsiveness to and selection into the program. We find that the current voluntary regime generates inefficient transfers to hospitals and reduces social welfare compared to the status quo, but that alternative (feasible) designs could substantially reduce these inefficient transfers. Our analysis highlights key design elements to consider under voluntary regulation.

中文摘要

政府项目通常以可选方式提供给市场参与者。我们在医疗保险支付改革的背景下探讨这种自愿监管的经济学，其中医疗服务提供者为一组相关的医疗服务获得单一的、预先确定的支付，而不是针对每项服务的单独支付。这种“捆绑支付”项目最初作为一项为期5年的随机试验实施，被分配到新支付模式的医院必须参与，但两年后，其中一半医院的参与意外地变为自愿。利用详细的索赔层面数据，我们记录了自愿参与更可能发生在那些无需改变行为就能增加收入的医院（“水平选择”）以及那些在强制参与时行为发生巨大变化的医院（“斜率选择”）。为了评估反事实制度下的结果，我们估计了一个关于对项目的响应性和选择性的简单模型。我们发现，与现状相比，当前的自愿制度产生了向医院的无效率转移并降低了社会福利，但替代性的（可行的）设计可以大幅减少这些无效率转移。我们的分析强调了在自愿监管下需要考虑的关键设计要素。

No. 70论文详情NBER w27222

Tokenomics: Dynamic Adoption and Valuation

代币经济学：动态采用与估值

Lin William Cong, Ye Li, Neng Wang

Abstract

We develop a dynamic asset-pricing model of cryptocurrencies/tokens that allow users to conduct peer-to-peer transactions on digital platforms. The equilibrium value of tokens is determined by aggregating heterogeneous users' transactional demand rather than discounting cashflows as in standard valuation models. Endogenous platform adoption builds upon user network externality and exhibits an S-curve — it starts slow, becomes volatile, and eventually tapers off. Introducing tokens lowers users' transaction costs on the platform by allowing users to capitalize on platform growth. The resulting intertemporal feedback between user adoption and token price accelerates adoption and dampens user-base volatility.

中文摘要

我们开发了一个加密货币/代币的动态资产定价模型，这些代币允许用户在数字平台上进行点对点交易。代币的均衡价值是通过汇总异质性用户的交易需求来确定的，而不是像标准估值模型那样对现金流进行贴现。内生平台采用基于用户网络外部性，并呈现S曲线——起步缓慢，变得波动，最终趋于平稳。引入代币通过允许用户利用平台增长来降低用户在平台上的交易成本。由此产生的用户采用与代币价格之间的跨期反馈加速了采用，并抑制了用户基础的波动性。

No. 71论文详情NBER w27221

When is Debt Odious? A Theory of Repression and Growth Traps

何时债务是恶债？一种关于压制与增长陷阱的理论

Viral V. Acharya, Raghuram Rajan, Jack Shim

Abstract

How is a developing country affected by its odious government’s ability to borrow in international markets? We examine the dynamics of a country’s growth, consumption, and sovereign debt, assuming that the government is myopic and wants to maximize short-term, socially unproductive, spending. Interestingly, access to external borrowing can extend the government’s effective horizon; the government’s ability to borrow hinges on its convincing investors they will be repaid, which gives it a stake in the future. The lengthening of the government’s effective horizon can incentivize it to tax less, resulting in higher steady-state household consumption than if it could not borrow. However, in a developing country that saves little, the government may engage in more repressive policies to enhance its debt capacity, which only ensures that successor governments repress as well. This leads to a “growth trap” where household steady-state consumption is lower than if the government had no access to debt. We characterize circumstances in which odious government leads to odious debt and those in which it does not, and discuss policies that might ameliorate the welfare of the citizenry.

中文摘要

一个发展中国家的恶政政府在国际市场上借款的能力如何影响该国？我们考察了一个国家的增长、消费和主权债务的动态，假设政府是短视的，并希望最大化短期的、对社会无生产力的支出。有趣的是，外部借款的渠道可以延长政府的有效视野；政府借款的能力取决于它能否让投资者相信他们会得到偿还，这使政府与未来利益相关。政府有效视野的延长可以激励其减少征税，从而导致比无法借款时更高的稳态家庭消费。然而，在一个储蓄很少的发展中国家，政府可能会采取更具压制性的政策来增强其债务能力，这只会确保继任政府也进行压制。这导致了一种“增长陷阱”，即家庭稳态消费低于政府无法获得债务时的水平。我们描述了恶政政府导致恶债的情形以及不导致恶债的情形，并讨论了可能改善公民福利的政策。

No. 72论文详情NBER w27220

The Cost of Privacy: Welfare Effects of the Disclosure of COVID-19 Cases

隐私的成本：COVID-19病例披露的福利效应

David O. Argente, Chang-Tai Hsieh, Munseob Lee

Abstract

South Korea publicly disclosed detailed location information of individuals that tested positive for COVID-19. We quantify the effect of public disclosure on the transmission of the virus and economic losses in Seoul. The change in commuting patterns due to public disclosure lowers the number of cases by 200 thousand and the number of deaths by 7.7 thousand in Seoul over two years. Compared to a city-wide lock-down that results in the same number of cases over two years as the disclosure scenario, the economic cost of such a lockdown is almost four times higher.

中文摘要

韩国公开披露了COVID-19检测呈阳性个体的详细位置信息。我们量化了公开披露对病毒传播和首尔经济损失的影响。由于公开披露导致的通勤模式变化，在两年内使首尔的病例数减少了20万，死亡人数减少了7700人。与导致两年内病例数与披露情景相同的全市封锁相比，这种封锁的经济成本几乎高出四倍。

No. 73论文详情NBER w27219

Global Comparatives Statics in General Equilibrium: Model Building from Theoretical Foundations

一般均衡中的全局比较静态分析：从理论基础构建模型

James R. Markusen

Abstract

International trade economists made seminal contributions to general equilibrium theory, moving away from an emphasis on existence of equilibrium to algebraic formulations which enabled us to characterize key relationships between parameters and variables, such as that between tariffs and domestic factor prices and welfare. But the analysis remained limited in value for policy evaluation: the analysis was local, it provided only qualitative results, it was limited to very small models, and strictly interior solutions had to be assumed. The contribution of this paper is pedagogic and methodological, providing a primer for those wishing to do or teach general-equilibrium counterfactuals on (for example) structural models. I show how the tools from early local comparative statics analyses can be generalized via the use of Shepard’s lemma, duality, complementarity and the Karush-Kuhn-Tucker theorem into a global, quantitative analysis of large changes in high-dimension models which also allows for regime changes and corner solutions. I then show how the resulting non-linear complementarity problem directly translates into a numerical model using GAMS (general algebraic modeling system).

中文摘要

国际贸易经济学家对一般均衡理论做出了开创性贡献，从强调均衡存在性转向代数公式化，使我们能够刻画参数与变量之间的关键关系，例如关税与国内要素价格及福利之间的关系。但该分析在政策评估方面的价值仍然有限：分析是局部的，仅提供定性结果，局限于非常小的模型，并且必须假设严格的内点解。本文的贡献在于教学和方法论层面，为那些希望（例如）在结构模型上进行或教授一般均衡反事实分析的人提供入门指南。我展示了如何通过使用谢泼德引理、对偶性、互补性和卡鲁什-库恩-塔克定理，将早期局部比较静态分析的工具推广为高维模型中大规模变化的全局定量分析，该分析还允许制度变化和角点解。然后，我展示了由此产生的非线性互补问题如何直接转化为使用GAMS（通用代数建模系统）的数值模型。

No. 74论文详情NBER w27218

Implications of Stochastic Transmission Rates for Managing Pandemic Risks

随机传播率对管理大流行风险的影响

Harrison Hong, Neng Wang, Jinqiang Yang

Abstract

We develop a model of pandemic risk management and ﬁrm valuation. We introduce aggregate transmission shocks into an epidemic model and link valuations to infections via an asset-pricing framework with vaccines. Infections lower earnings growth but ﬁrms can mitigate damages. We estimate a large reproduction number R0 and transmission volatility for COVID-19. Using these estimates, we assess the accuracy of deterministic approximations based on R0. Our model generates predictions consistent with data: unexpected infection resurgence, non-monotonic mitigation policies, and higher price-to-earnings ratios during a pandemic. Valuations would be signiﬁcantly lower absent mitigation and a high vaccine arrival rate.

中文摘要

我们开发了一个大流行风险管理和企业估值模型。我们将总体传播冲击引入流行病模型，并通过一个包含疫苗的资产定价框架将估值与感染联系起来。感染会降低盈利增长，但企业可以减轻损害。我们估计了COVID-19的高基本再生数R0和传播波动性。利用这些估计，我们评估了基于R0的确定性近似的准确性。我们的模型产生了与数据一致的预测：意外的感染复燃、非单调的缓解政策以及大流行期间更高的市盈率。如果没有缓解措施和高疫苗到达率，估值将显著降低。

No. 75论文详情NBER w27217

The Long-Term Cognitive and Schooling Effects of Childhood Vaccinations in China

中国儿童疫苗接种的长期认知和教育效应

Hamid R. Oskorouchi, Alfonso Sousa-Poza, David E. Bloom

Abstract

By exploiting rich retrospective data on childhood immunization, socioeconomics, and health status in China (the China Health and Retirement Longitudinal Study), we assess the long-term effects of childhood vaccination on cognitive and educational outcomes in that country. To do so, we apply various techniques (e.g., propensity score and coarsened exact matching and correlated random effects) to different sets of conditioning variables and subsamples to estimate the average treatment on the treated effect of childhood vaccination. Our results confirm that vaccinations before the age of 15 have long-term positive and economically meaningful effects on nonhealth outcomes such as education and cognitive skills. These effects are relatively strong, with vaccinated individuals enjoying about one more year of schooling and performing substantially better later in life on several cognitive tests.

中文摘要

通过利用中国关于儿童免疫、社会经济状况和健康状态的丰富回顾性数据（中国健康与养老追踪调查），我们评估了该国儿童疫苗接种对认知和教育结果的长期影响。为此，我们应用了多种技术（例如，倾向得分匹配、粗略精确匹配和相关随机效应）到不同的条件变量集和子样本中，以估计儿童疫苗接种对受处理者的平均处理效应。我们的结果证实，15岁之前的疫苗接种对教育和认知技能等非健康结果具有长期积极且在经济上显著的影响。这些影响相对较强，接种疫苗的个体平均多享受约一年的教育，并在晚年多项认知测试中表现显著更好。

No. 76论文详情NBER w27216

US Unemployment Insurance Replacement Rates During the Pandemic

疫情期间的美国失业保险替代率

Peter Ganong, Pascal J. Noel, Joseph S. Vavra

Abstract

We use micro data on earnings together with the details of each state’s unemployment insurance (UI) system to compute the distribution of UI benefits after the uniform $\$600$ Federal Pandemic Unemployment Compensation (FPUC) supplement implemented by the CARES Act. We find that between April and July 2020, 76% of workers eligible for regular Unemployment Compensation have statutory replacement rates above 100%, meaning that they are eligible for benefits which exceed lost wages. The median statutory replacement rate is 145%. We also compute comprehensive replacement rates, which account for employer provided non-wage compensation and differential tax treatment of labor income and UI. 69% of UI-eligible unemployed have comprehensive replacement rates above 100% and the median comprehensive replacement rate is 134%. The presence of the FPUC has important implications for the incidence of the recession and reverses income patterns which would have otherwise arisen across income levels, occupations, and industries.

中文摘要

我们利用个人收入的微观数据以及各州失业保险系统的细节，计算了在《CARES法案》实施的统一600美元联邦大流行失业补偿补充金之后失业保险福利的分布。我们发现，在2020年4月至7月期间，76%有资格获得常规失业补偿的工人的法定替代率超过100%，这意味着他们有资格获得超过损失的工资的福利。中位法定替代率为145%。我们还计算了综合替代率，该替代率考虑了雇主提供的非工资补偿以及劳动收入和失业保险的差别税收待遇。69%有资格领取失业保险的失业者综合替代率超过100%，中位综合替代率为134%。联邦大流行失业补偿的存在对经济衰退的影响分布具有重要意义，并逆转了原本会在不同收入水平、职业和行业之间出现的收入模式。

No. 77论文详情NBER w27215

The Economics of Urban Density

城市密度的经济学

Gilles Duranton, Diego Puga

Abstract

Urban density boosts productivity and innovation, improves access to goods and services, reduces typical travel distances, encourages energy-efficient construction and transport, and facilitates sharing scarce amenities. However, density is also synonymous with crowding, makes living and moving in cities more costly, and concentrates exposure to pollution and disease. We explore the appropriate measurement of density and describe how it is both a cause and a consequence of the evolution of cities. We then discuss whether and how policy should target density and why the trade-off between its pros and cons is unhappily resolved by market and political forces.

中文摘要

城市密度能提高生产力和创新，改善商品和服务的获取，减少典型出行距离，鼓励节能建筑和交通，并促进共享稀缺便利设施。然而，密度也等同于拥挤，使在城市生活和出行成本更高，并集中了污染和疾病的暴露风险。我们探讨了密度的适当衡量方法，并描述了它如何既是城市演变的原因也是其结果。然后，我们讨论了政策是否以及如何应以密度为目标，以及为什么其利弊之间的权衡被市场和政治力量不幸地解决。

No. 78论文详情NBER w27214

Cyclical Lending Standards: A Structural Analysis

周期性贷款标准：一项结构性分析

Kaiji Chen, Patrick C. Higgins, Tao Zha

Abstract

Lending standards are a direct measure of credit conditions. We use the micro data merged from three separate sources to construct this measure and document that an uncertain macroeconomic outlook, rather than banks' balance sheet positions, was an important reason that a majority of banks tightened bank lending standards during the Great Recession. Our extensive data analysis disciplines how we introduce credit frictions in the banking sector into a macroeconomic model. The model estimation reveals that an exogenous shock to credit supply drives cyclical lending standards and accounts for a significant portion of fluctuations in bank loans and aggregate output.

中文摘要

贷款标准是信贷条件的直接衡量指标。我们使用来自三个不同来源合并的微观数据来构建这一指标，并记录到，在大衰退期间，不确定的宏观经济前景（而非银行的资产负债表状况）是大多数银行收紧银行贷款标准的重要原因。我们广泛的数据分析约束了我们将银行部门的信贷摩擦引入宏观经济模型的方式。模型估计揭示，对信贷供给的外生冲击驱动了周期性贷款标准，并解释了银行贷款和总产出波动的很大一部分。

No. 79论文详情NBER w27213

In Search of Distress Risk in Emerging Markets

寻找新兴市场的困境风险

Gonzalo Asis, Anusha Chari, Adam Haas

Abstract

This paper employs a novel multi-country dataset of corporate defaults to develop a model of distress risk specific to emerging markets. The data suggest that global financial variables such as US interest rates and shifts in global liquidity and risk aversion have significant predictive power for forecasting corporate distress risk in emerging markets. We document a positive distress risk premium in emerging market equities and show that the impact of a global "risk-off" environment on default risk is greater for firms whose returns are more sensitive to a composite global factor.

中文摘要

本文利用一个新颖的多国企业违约数据集，开发了一个特定于新兴市场的困境风险模型。数据表明，全球金融变量，如美国利率以及全球流动性和风险偏好的变化，对预测新兴市场的企业困境风险具有显著的预测能力。我们记录了新兴市场股票中正的困境风险溢价，并表明，对于其收益对综合全球因素更敏感的公司，全球“避险”环境对违约风险的影响更大。

No. 80论文详情NBER w27212

Financing Vaccines for Global Health Security

为全球卫生安全融资疫苗

Jonathan T. Vu, Benjamin K. Kaplan, Shomesh Chaudhuri, Monique K. Mansoura, Andrew W. Lo

Abstract

Recent outbreaks of infectious pathogens such as Zika, Ebola, and COVID-19 have underscored the need for the dependable availability of vaccines against emerging infectious diseases (EIDs). The cost and risk of R&D programs and uniquely unpredictable demand for EID vaccines have discouraged vaccine developers, and government and nonprofit agencies have been unable to provide timely or sufficient incentives for their development and sustained supply. We analyze the economic returns of a portfolio of EID vaccine assets, and find that under realistic financing assumptions, the expected returns are significantly negative, implying that the private sector is unlikely to address this need without public-sector intervention. We have sized the financing deficit for this portfolio and analyze several potential solutions, including price increases, enhanced public-private partnerships, and subscription models through which individuals would pay annual fees to obtain access to a portfolio of vaccines in the event of an outbreak.

中文摘要

近期寨卡、埃博拉和COVID-19等传染性病原体的爆发，凸显了对针对新兴传染病的疫苗可靠供应的需求。研发项目的成本和风险，以及新兴传染病疫苗独特不可预测的需求，阻碍了疫苗开发商，而政府和非营利机构未能为其开发和持续供应提供及时或充分的激励。我们分析了一个新兴传染病疫苗资产组合的经济回报，发现在现实的融资假设下，预期回报显著为负，这意味着私营部门在没有公共部门干预的情况下不太可能满足这一需求。我们估算了该投资组合的融资缺口，并分析了几个潜在的解决方案，包括提价、加强公私合作伙伴关系，以及个人通过支付年费以获得在疫情爆发时获取疫苗组合的订阅模式。

No. 81论文详情NBER w27211

Heterogeneous Actions, Beliefs, Constraints and Risk Tolerance During the COVID-19 Pandemic

COVID-19疫情期间的异质性行为、信念、约束与风险承受力

Ying Fan, A. Yeşim Orhun, Dana Turjeman

Abstract

During a pandemic, an individual's choices can determine outcomes not only for the individual but also for the entire community. Beliefs, constraints and preferences may shape behavior. This paper documents demographic differences in behaviors, beliefs, constraints and risk preferences across gender, income and political affiliation lines during the new coronavirus disease (COVID-19) pandemic. Our main analyses are based on data from an original nationally representative survey covering 5,500 adult respondents in the U.S. We find substantial gaps in behaviors and beliefs across gender, income and partisanship lines; in constraints across income levels; and in risk tolerance among men and women. Based on location data from a large sample of smartphones, we also document significant differences in mobility across demographics, which are consistent with our findings based on the survey data.

中文摘要

在疫情期间，个人的选择不仅决定自身结果，也影响整个社区。信念、约束和偏好可能塑造行为。本文记录了新冠疫情期间，不同性别、收入和党派群体在行为、信念、约束和风险偏好方面的人口统计学差异。我们的主要分析基于一项覆盖美国5500名成年受访者的全国代表性原始调查数据。我们发现，不同性别、收入和党派群体在行为和信念上存在显著差距；不同收入水平在约束上存在差距；男性和女性在风险承受力上存在差距。基于大量智能手机样本的位置数据，我们还记录了不同人口群体在流动性上的显著差异，这与我们基于调查数据的发现一致。

No. 82论文详情NBER w27210

Collateralized Marriage

抵押婚姻

Jeanne Lafortune, Corinne Low

Abstract

We study the role of wealth in the marriage contract by developing a model of the household where investments in public goods can be made at the cost of future earnings. If couples cannot commit ex ante to a suﬃciently equal post-divorce allocation, specialization and public good creation will be sub-optimal. However, accumulating joint assets, which the marriage contract speciﬁes are to be divided in the case of divorce, can reduce this problem by oﬀering insurance to the lower earning partner. Our model demonstrates that access to this “collateralized” version of the contract will lead to more household specialization, more public goods, and a higher value of marriage. To test the model’s predictions, we use homeownership as a proxy for access to joint savings technology, since homes are particularly likely to be divided in a way that favors the lower earning partner. We use idiosyncratic variation in housing prices at the time of marriage and an instrumental variables strategy to show that quasi-exogenous variation in homeownership access leads to greater specialization. We then show that as policies made marriage and non-marital fertility more similar in other ways, wealth has become a more important determinant of who marries. Our model and empirical results suggest wealthy individuals can access a more advantageous marriage contract, which has important policy implications.

中文摘要

我们通过构建一个家庭模型来研究财富在婚姻契约中的作用，在该模型中，公共品投资可能以牺牲未来收入为代价。如果夫妻无法事前承诺足够平等的离婚后分配，那么专业化和公共品创造将无法达到最优。然而，积累婚姻契约规定在离婚时需分割的共同资产，可以通过为低收入伴侣提供保险来缓解这一问题。我们的模型表明，获得这种“抵押”形式的契约将导致更多的家庭专业化、更多的公共品以及更高的婚姻价值。为了检验模型的预测，我们使用住房所有权作为获得共同储蓄技术的代理变量，因为住房尤其可能以有利于低收入伴侣的方式进行分割。我们利用结婚时房价的特异性波动和工具变量策略，证明住房所有权获取的准外生变化导致了更大的专业化。然后我们表明，随着政策使婚姻和非婚生育在其他方面更加相似，财富已成为决定谁结婚的更重要因素。我们的模型和实证结果表明，富人可以获取更有利的婚姻契约，这具有重要的政策含义。

No. 83论文详情NBER w27209

Housing Search Frictions: Evidence from Detailed Search Data and a Field Experiment

住房搜索摩擦：来自详细搜索数据和实地实验的证据

Peter Bergman, Eric W. Chan, Adam Kapor

Abstract

We randomized school quality information onto the listings of a nationwide housing website for low-income families. We use this variation and data on families' search and location choices to estimate a model of housing search and neighborhood choice that incorporates imperfect information and potentially biased beliefs. We find that imperfect information and biased beliefs cause families to live in neighborhoods with lower-performing, more segregated schools. Families underestimate school quality conditional on neighborhood characteristics. If we had ignored this information problem, we would have estimated that families value school quality relative to their commute downtown by half that of the truth.

中文摘要

我们在一个面向低收入家庭的全国性住房网站房源信息中随机加入了学校质量信息。我们利用这一变化以及家庭搜索和选址决策的数据，估计了一个包含不完全信息和潜在有偏信念的住房搜索与社区选择模型。我们发现，不完全信息和有偏信念导致家庭居住在拥有表现更差、更隔离学校的社区。家庭在给定社区特征的情况下低估了学校质量。如果我们忽略这一信息问题，我们估计的家庭对学校质量的重视程度（相对于通勤至市中心）将只有真实值的一半。

No. 84论文详情NBER w27208

Corporate Hiring under COVID-19: Labor Market Concentration, Downskilling, and Income Inequality

COVID-19下的企业招聘：劳动力市场集中度、技能降级与收入不平等

Murillo Campello, Gaurav Kankanhalli, Pradeep Muthukrishnan

Abstract

Big data on job-vacancy postings reveal several dimensions of the impact of COVID-19 on the U.S. job market. Firms have cut back on postings for high-skill jobs more than for low-skill jobs, with small firms nearly halting their new hiring altogether. New-hiring cuts and downskilling are most pronounced in local labor markets lacking depth (where employment is concentrated within a few firms), in low-income areas, and in areas with greater income inequality. Cuts are deeper in industries where workers are more unionized and in the non-tradable sector. Access to finance modulates corporate hiring, with credit-constrained firms curtailing their job postings the most. Our study shows how the early-2020 global pandemic is shaping the dynamics of hiring, identifying the firms, jobs, places, industries, and labor markets most affected by it. Our results point to important challenges to the scale and speed of a recovery.

中文摘要

基于职位空缺发布的大数据揭示了COVID-19对美国就业市场影响的多个维度。企业削减高技能岗位招聘的幅度大于低技能岗位，小企业几乎完全停止了新招聘。新招聘削减和技能降级在缺乏深度的本地劳动力市场（即就业集中在少数几家企业）、低收入地区以及收入不平等程度更高的地区最为显著。在工会化程度更高的行业和非贸易部门，招聘削减更为严重。融资渠道调节着企业招聘，信贷受限的企业职位发布削减最多。我们的研究展示了2020年初的全球大流行如何塑造招聘动态，识别出受影响最严重的企业、岗位、地区、行业和劳动力市场。我们的结果指出了复苏规模和速度面临的重大挑战。

No. 85论文详情NBER w27207

Can the Covid Bailouts Save the Economy?

新冠疫情救助能否拯救经济？

Vadim Elenev, Tim Landvoigt, Stijn Van Nieuwerburgh

Abstract

The covid-19 crisis has led to a sharp deterioration in firm and bank balance sheets. The government has responded with a massive intervention in corporate credit markets. We study equilibrium dynamics of macroeconomic quantities and prices, and how they are affected by government policy. The interventions prevent a much deeper crisis by reducing corporate bankruptcies by about half and short-circuiting the doom loop between corporate and financial sector fragility. The additional fiscal cost is zero since program spending replaces what would otherwise have been spent on intermediary bailouts. The model predicts rising interest rates on government debt and slow debt pay-down. We analyze an alternative intervention that targets aid to firms at risk of bankruptcy. While this policy prevents more bankruptcies and has lower fiscal cost, it only enjoys marginally higher welfare. Finally, we study longer-run consequences for firm leverage and intermediary health when pandemics become the new normal.

中文摘要

新冠疫情危机导致企业和银行资产负债表急剧恶化。政府以大规模干预企业信贷市场作为回应。我们研究了宏观经济总量和价格的均衡动态，以及政府政策如何影响它们。这些干预措施通过将企业破产减少约一半并阻断企业与金融部门脆弱性之间的厄运循环，防止了更严重的危机。额外的财政成本为零，因为项目支出取代了原本用于中介救助的支出。该模型预测政府债务利率上升且债务偿还缓慢。我们分析了一种针对濒临破产企业的替代干预措施。虽然这一政策能防止更多破产且财政成本更低，但它仅带来边际上更高的福利。最后，我们研究了大流行成为新常态时对企业杠杆和中介机构健康的长期影响。

No. 86论文详情NBER w27206

Innovation, Growth and Structural Change in American Agriculture

美国农业的创新、增长与结构变迁

Julian M. Alston, Philip G. Pardey

Abstract

U.S. agriculture was transformed during the 20th century by waves of innovation with mechanical, biological, chemical, and information technologies. Compared with a few decades ago, today’s agriculture is much less labor intensive and farms are much larger and more specialized, supplying a much-evolved market for farm products. Over recent decades, the global landscape for agricultural R&D has shifted away from farms, away from the public sector toward the private sector, and away from the United States towards agriculturally important middle-income countries, especially China, India and Brazil. U.S. investments in agricultural R&D are stalling even though meta-evidence shows that past U.S. investments in agricultural R&D have yielded very favorable returns: median reported benefit-cost ratios in the range of 12:1. Sustained U.S. investment and innovation will be required to preserve past productivity gains in the face of climate change, coevolving pests and diseases, and changing technological regulations—let alone increase productivity. Great potential exists for innovation in crop and livestock genetics and digital farming technologies to generate new products and production processes, but innovators are facing increasingly strong headwinds from social and political forces that seek to dictate technology choices.

中文摘要

20世纪，美国农业经历了机械、生物、化学和信息技术创新浪潮的变革。与几十年前相比，今天的农业劳动密集度大大降低，农场规模更大、更专业化，服务于一个高度演变的农产品市场。近几十年来，全球农业研发格局已从农场转移，从公共部门转向私营部门，并从美国转向农业重要的中等收入国家，特别是中国、印度和巴西。尽管元证据表明美国过去的农业研发投资已产生非常可观的回报（报告的中位效益成本比约为12:1），但美国的农业研发投资正在停滞。面对气候变化、共同进化的病虫害以及不断变化的技术法规，要保持过去的生产率增长——更不用说提高生产率——需要持续的美国投资和创新。在作物和牲畜遗传学以及数字农业技术方面，创新具有巨大潜力，可以创造新产品和生产流程，但创新者正面临来自试图左右技术选择的社会和政治力量日益强大的阻力。

Do Environmental Markets Cause Environmental Injustice? Evidence from California's Carbon Market

环境市场会导致环境不公正吗？来自加州碳市场的证据

Danae Hernandez-Cortes, Kyle C. Meng

Abstract

Market-based environmental policies are widely adopted on the basis of allocative efficiency. However, there is growing concern that market-induced spatial reallocation of pollution could widen existing pollution concentration gaps between disadvantaged and other communities. We examine how this \\environmental justice" (EJ) gap changed following the 2013 introduction of California's carbon market, the world's second largest and the most subjected to EJ critiques. We estimate that the program lowered GHG, PM2:5, PM10, and NOx emissions by 3-9% annually between 2012-2017 for sample industrial facilities regulated only by the carbon market. Using a pollution dispersal model to characterize resulting spatial changes in pollution concentrations, we find the program caused EJ gaps in PM2:5, PM10, and NOx from these facilities to narrow by 6-10% annually. We demonstrate that explicit modeling of pollution dispersal is critical for detecting these results.

中文摘要

基于市场的环境政策因其配置效率而被广泛采用。然而，人们日益担心市场诱导的污染空间重新分配可能扩大弱势社区与其他社区之间现有的污染浓度差距。我们研究了2013年引入加州碳市场（全球第二大且受环境正义批评最多的碳市场）后，这一“环境正义”差距如何变化。我们估计，在2012-2017年间，对于仅受碳市场监管的样本工业设施，该计划每年使温室气体、PM2.5、PM10和氮氧化物排放量降低3-9%。利用污染扩散模型描述由此产生的污染浓度空间变化，我们发现该计划使这些设施造成的PM2.5、PM10和氮氧化物环境正义差距每年缩小6-10%。我们证明，明确建模污染扩散对于检测这些结果至关重要。

No. 88论文详情NBER w27204

Cigarette Taxes and Smoking in the Long Run

香烟税与长期吸烟行为

Andrew I. Friedson, Daniel I. Rees

Abstract

Researchers have focused on the contemporaneous relationship between cigarette taxes and smoking, while the longer-run effects of cigarette taxes have received little attention. Using individual-level panel data from 1970-2017, we estimate the effects of cigarette taxes experienced as a teenager on smoking later in life. We find that a one-dollar increase in the cigarette tax experienced between the ages of 12 and 17 is associated with substantial reductions in smoking participation and intensity among adults in their 20s through mid-60s. Among first-time mothers, it is associated with a reduction in the likelihood of smoking the year of giving birth.

中文摘要

研究者们一直关注香烟税与吸烟之间的同期关系，而香烟税的长期效应却很少受到关注。利用1970-2017年的个体层面面板数据，我们估算了青少年时期经历的香烟税对日后生活吸烟行为的影响。我们发现，在12至17岁期间经历的香烟税每增加1美元，与20多岁至60多岁成年人吸烟参与率和强度的显著降低相关。对于初为人母的女性，这与分娩当年吸烟可能性的降低相关。

No. 89论文详情NBER w27203

Patents, Innovation, and Development

专利、创新与发展

Bronwyn H. Hall

Abstract

I survey some recent research on the role of patents in encouraging innovation and growth in developing economies, beginning with a brief history of international patent systems and facts about the current use of patents around the world. I discuss research on the implications of patents for international technology transfer and domestic innovation. This is followed by a review of recent work by myself and co-authors on regional patent systems, the impact of patents on firm performance, and the impact on pharmaceutical patenting and domestic innovation. The conclusion suggests that patents may be relatively unimportant in development, even for middle income countries.

中文摘要

我调查了一些关于专利在鼓励发展中经济体创新和增长方面作用的最新研究，首先简要回顾了国际专利制度的历史以及当前全球专利使用情况的事实。我讨论了关于专利对国际技术转让和国内创新影响的研究。随后回顾了我和合著者近期关于区域专利制度、专利对企业绩效的影响以及专利对药品专利和国内创新影响的工作。结论表明，专利在发展过程中可能相对不重要，即使对中等收入国家也是如此。

No. 90论文详情NBER w27202

Modeling the Impacts of Agricultural Support Policies on Emissions from Agriculture

模拟农业支持政策对农业排放的影响

David Laborde, Abdullah Mamun, Will Martin, Valeria Piñeiro, Rob Vos

Abstract

To understand the impacts of support programs on global emissions, this paper considers the impacts of domestic subsidies, price distortions at the border, and investments in emission-reducing technologies on global greenhouse gas (GHG) emissions from agriculture. In a step towards a full evaluation of the impacts, it uses a counterfactual global model scenario showing how much emissions from agricultural production would change if agricultural support were abolished worldwide. The analysis indicates that, without subsidies paid directly to farmers, output of some emission-intensive activities and agricultural emissions would be smaller. Without agricultural trade protection, however, emissions would be higher. This is partly because protection reduces global demand more than it increases global agricultural supply, and partly because some countries that currently tax agriculture have high emission intensities. Policies that directly reduce emission intensities yield much larger reductions in emissions than those that reduce emission intensities by increasing overall productivity because overall productivity growth creates a rebound effect by reducing product prices and expanding output. A key challenge is designing policy reforms that effectively reduce emissions without jeopardizing other key goals such as improving nutrition and reducing poverty. This analysis is an important building block towards a full understanding the impacts of reforms to agricultural support on mitigation of greenhouse gas emissions and adaptation to climate change. That full analysis is being undertaken in current work incorporating land use changes and examining the impacts of specific reforms on mitigation, resilience and economic outcomes.

中文摘要

为了理解支持计划对全球排放的影响，本文考虑了国内补贴、边境价格扭曲以及减排技术投资对全球农业温室气体排放的影响。作为全面评估影响的一步，它使用了一个反事实的全球模型情景，展示了如果全球取消农业支持，农业生产排放将如何变化。分析表明，如果没有直接支付给农民的补贴，一些排放密集型活动的产出和农业排放将会减少。然而，如果没有农业贸易保护，排放将会更高。这部分是因为保护措施减少全球需求的程度大于其增加全球农业供给的程度，部分是因为一些目前对农业征税的国家具有高排放强度。直接降低排放强度的政策比通过提高整体生产率来降低排放强度的政策能带来更大的减排效果，因为整体生产率增长通过降低产品价格和扩大产出产生了反弹效应。一个关键挑战是设计有效的政策改革，在不损害改善营养和减少贫困等其他关键目标的情况下减少排放。这项分析是全面理解农业支持改革对温室气体减排和气候变化适应影响的重要基石。该全面分析正在当前工作中进行，纳入了土地利用变化，并考察了具体改革对减排、韧性和经济结果的影响。

No. 91论文详情NBER w27201

Urbanization in the Developing World: Too Early or Too Slow?

发展中国家的城市化：太早还是太慢？

J. Vernon Henderson, Matthew A. Turner

Abstract

We describe patterns of urbanization in the developing world and the extent to which they differ from the developed world. We consider the extent to which urbanization in the developing world can be explained by conventional models of spatial equilibrium. Despite their relative poverty, developing world cities are relatively highly productive, and often provide good access to safe water, improved sanitation, schooling and inoculations. In some parts of the world, they are home to a surprisingly small number of factory workers and a surprisingly large number of farmers. Developing world cities seem to do less well at protecting their residents from lifestyle diseases and crime, their female residents from domestic violence and their children from illness. In thinking about these facts, we note that one strand of the literature focused on structural transformation has suggested that urbanization in the developing is occurring `too early’, while another strand argues that urbanization is occurring `too slow’ to be consistent with conventional models of spatial equilibrium. Despite many differences between developing and developed world cities, our new results combined with those in the literature suggest that models of spatial equilibrium can be adapted to be a useful guide to understanding the process of urbanization in the developing world.

中文摘要

我们描述了发展中国家的城市化模式及其与发达国家的差异程度。我们考虑了空间均衡的传统模型能在多大程度上解释发展中国家的城市化。尽管相对贫困，发展中国家城市的生产率相对较高，并且通常能提供良好的安全用水、改善的卫生设施、学校教育和疫苗接种。在世界某些地区，这些城市中工厂工人的数量出奇地少，而农民的数量出奇地多。发展中国家城市在保护居民免受生活方式疾病和犯罪侵害、保护女性居民免受家庭暴力以及保护儿童免受疾病侵害方面似乎做得较差。在思考这些事实时，我们注意到，专注于结构转型的一支文献认为发展中国家的城市化发生得“太早”，而另一支文献则认为城市化发生得“太慢”，与传统的空间均衡模型不一致。尽管发展中国家和发达国家城市之间存在许多差异，但我们结合文献得出的新结果表明，空间均衡模型可以经过调整，成为理解发展中国家城市化过程的有用指南。

No. 92论文详情NBER w27200

Can the World’s Poor Protect Themselves from the New Coronavirus?

世界上的穷人能保护自己免受新冠病毒侵害吗？

Caitlin S. Brown, Martin Ravallion, Dominique van de Walle

Abstract

We propose an index of the adequacy of home environments for protection (HEP) from COVID-19, and we compare our index across developing countries using data for one million sampled households from the latest Demographic and Health Surveys. We find that prevailing WHO recommendations for protection posit unrealistic home environments. 90% of households have inadequate HEP by one or more dimensions considered. 40% do not have a formal health-care facility within 5km. A strong wealth effect is indicated within and between countries. Only 6% of the poorest 40% have an adequate HEP, and the proportion is virtually zero in sub-Saharan Africa.

中文摘要

我们提出了一个家庭环境防护充分性指数，用于评估对新冠病毒的防护能力，并利用来自最新人口与健康调查的一百万抽样家庭数据，在发展中国家之间比较该指数。我们发现，世界卫生组织现行的防护建议设定了不切实际的家庭环境。90%的家庭在考虑的一个或多个维度上家庭环境防护不足。40%的家庭在5公里范围内没有正规的医疗保健设施。国家内部和国家之间显示出强烈的财富效应。在最贫困的40%人口中，只有6%拥有足够的家庭环境防护，而在撒哈拉以南非洲，这一比例几乎为零。

No. 93论文详情NBER w27199

Foreign Exchange Order Flow as a Risk Factor

外汇订单流作为风险因子

Craig Burnside, Mario Cerrato, Zhekai Zhang

Abstract

This paper proposes a set of novel pricing factors for currency returns that are motivated by microstructure models. In so doing, we bring two strands of the exchange rate literature, namely market-microstructure and risk-based models, closer together. Our novel factors use order flow data to provide direct measures of buying and selling pressure related to carry trading and momentum strategies. We find that they appear to be good proxies for currency crash risk. Additionally, we show that the association between our order-flow factors and currency returns differs according to the customer segment of the foreign exchange market. In particular, it appears that financial customers are risk takers in the market, while non-financial customers serve as liquidity providers.

中文摘要

本文提出了一组基于微观结构模型的新颖货币收益定价因子。通过这样做，我们将汇率文献的两个分支，即市场微观结构和基于风险的模型，更紧密地结合在一起。我们的新颖因子利用订单流数据，提供了与套利交易和动量策略相关的买卖压力的直接度量。我们发现它们似乎是货币崩盘风险的良好代理变量。此外，我们表明，我们的订单流因子与货币收益之间的关联因外汇市场的客户细分而不同。特别是，金融客户似乎是市场中的风险承担者，而非金融客户则充当流动性提供者。

Identification of Time-Inconsistent Models: The Case of Insecticide Treated Nets

时间不一致模型的识别：以杀虫剂处理蚊帐为例

Aprajit Mahajan, Christian Michel, Alessandro Tarozzi

Abstract

Time-inconsistency may play a central role in explaining inter-temporal behavior, particularly among poor households. However, little is known about the distribution of time-inconsistent agents, and time-preference parameters are typically not identified in standard dynamic choice models. We formulate a dynamic discrete choice model in an unobservedly heterogeneous population of possibly time-inconsistent agents. We provide conditions under which all population type probabilities and preferences for both time-consistent and sophisticated agents are point-identified and sharp set-identification results for naïve and partially sophisticated agents. Estimating the model using data from a health intervention providing insecticide treated nets (ITNs) in rural Odisha, India, we find that about two-thirds of our sample comprises time-inconsistent agents and that both sophisticated and naïve agents are considerably present-biased. Counterfactuals show that the under-investment in ITNs attributable to present-bias leads to substantial costs that are about four times the price of an ITN.

中文摘要

时间不一致性可能在解释跨期行为中发挥核心作用，尤其是在贫困家庭中。然而，关于时间不一致行为主体的分布知之甚少，且时间偏好参数在标准动态选择模型中通常无法识别。我们构建了一个动态离散选择模型，研究对象是可能具有时间不一致性的不可观测异质性人群。我们提供了条件，在这些条件下，所有人群类型概率以及时间一致和精明行为主体的偏好都可以点识别，而对于天真和部分精明行为主体则得到尖锐集识别结果。利用来自印度奥里萨邦农村一项提供杀虫剂处理蚊帐的健康干预措施的数据估计该模型，我们发现样本中约三分之二的人属于时间不一致行为主体，并且精明和天真行为主体都表现出显著的现时偏向。反事实分析表明，由现时偏向导致的杀虫剂处理蚊帐投资不足带来了巨大成本，约为杀虫剂处理蚊帐价格的四倍。

Correcting Estimates of Electric Vehicle Emissions Abatement: Implications for Climate Policy

修正电动汽车减排估算：对气候政策的启示

Erich Muehlegger, David S. Rapson

Abstract

Transportation electrification is viewed by many as a cornerstone for climate change mitigation, with the ultimate vision to phase out conventional vehicles entirely. In a world with only electric vehicles (EVs), transportation pollution would be primarily determined by the electricity grid composition. For the foreseeable future, however, environmental benefits of EVs must be measured relative to the (likely gasoline) car that would have been bought instead. This so-called “counterfactual” vehicle cannot be observed, but its fuel economy can be estimated. A quasi-experiment in California allows us to show that subsidized buyers of EVs would have, on average, purchased relatively fuel-efficient cars had they not gone electric. The actual incremental pollution abatement arising from EVs today is thus substantially smaller than one would predict using the fleet average as the counterfactual vehicle. We discuss implications for climate policy and how to accurately reflect EV choice in integrated assessment models.

中文摘要

交通电气化被许多人视为减缓气候变化的基石，其最终愿景是彻底淘汰传统车辆。在一个只有电动汽车的世界里，交通污染将主要由电网构成决定。然而，在可预见的未来，电动汽车的环境效益必须相对于原本可能购买的（很可能是汽油）汽车来衡量。这种所谓的“反事实”车辆无法被观测到，但其燃油经济性可以估算。加利福尼亚州的一项准实验使我们能够证明，获得补贴的电动汽车购买者如果未选择电动，平均而言会购买相对节能的汽车。因此，当前电动汽车带来的实际增量污染减排远小于使用车队平均值作为反事实车辆所预测的结果。我们讨论了这对气候政策的启示，以及如何在综合评估模型中准确反映电动汽车选择。

Males at the Tails: How Socioeconomic Status Shapes the Gender Gap

尾部的男性：社会经济地位如何塑造性别差距

David Autor, David N. Figlio, Krzysztof Karbownik, Jeffrey Roth, Melanie Wasserman

Abstract

Analyzing Florida birth certificates matched to school records, we document that the female advantage in childhood behavioral and academic outcomes is driven by gender gaps at the extremes of the outcome distribution. Using unconditional quantile regression, we investigate whether family socioeconomic status (SES) differentially affects the lower tail outcomes of boys. We find that the differential effects of family SES on boys’ outcomes are concentrated in the parts of the distribution where the gender gaps are most pronounced. Accounting for the disproportionate effects of family environment on boys at the tails substantially narrows the gender gap in high school dropout.

中文摘要

通过分析佛罗里达州的出生证明与学校记录匹配数据，我们记录了儿童时期行为和学业结果中女性优势是由结果分布极端处的性别差距驱动的。利用无条件分位数回归，我们研究了家庭社会经济地位是否对男孩的下尾结果产生差异化影响。我们发现，家庭社会经济地位对男孩结果的差异化影响集中在性别差距最为显著的那部分分布中。考虑家庭环境对尾部男孩的过度影响，显著缩小了高中辍学率中的性别差距。

No. 97论文详情NBER w27195

Interest Rates and the Design of Financial Contracts

利率与金融合约设计

Michael R. Roberts, Michael Schwert

Abstract

We show that the partial response of loan rates to interest rate changes, referred to in the bank lending literature as “stickiness,” is a feature of perfect capital markets. No-arbitrage models of credit risk are able to replicate empirical interest rate sensitivities. However, the widespread use of interest rate floors in the low-rate environment of the last decade is a result of risk-sharing and incentive considerations arising from market imperfections. Floors reallocate cash flows across states in a way that loan spreads cannot. They insure lenders against losses if rates fall, while mitigating borrower moral hazard if rates rise.

中文摘要

我们证明，贷款利率对利率变动的部分反应（在银行贷款文献中称为“粘性”）是完美资本市场的特征。信用风险的无套利模型能够复现经验性的利率敏感性。然而，过去十年低利率环境下利率下限的广泛使用，源于市场不完美所引发的风险分担和激励考量。利率下限以贷款利差无法实现的方式在各状态间重新分配现金流。它们在利率下降时为贷款人提供损失保障，同时在利率上升时减轻借款人的道德风险。

No. 98论文详情NBER w27194

Issue Salience and Political Stereotypes

议题显著性与政治刻板印象

Pedro Bordalo, Marco Tabellini, David Y. Yang

Abstract

US voters exaggerate the differences in attitudes held by Republicans and Democrats on a range of socioeconomic and political issues, and greater perceived polarization is associated with greater political engagement and affective polarization. In this paper, we examine the drivers of such perceived partisan differences. We find that a model of stereotypes, where distortions are stronger for issues that are more salient to voters, captures important features of the data. First, perceived partisan differences are predictable from the actual differences across parties, in particular from the relative prevalence of extreme attitudes. Second, perceived partisan differences are larger on issues that individuals consider more important. Third, issue salience increases the tendency to over-weigh extreme types. Exploiting nationally representative survey data, we show that the end of the Cold War in 1991, which shifted US voters’ attention away from external threats, increased perceived, relative to actual, partisan differences on domestic issues. The rise was stronger for issues with more stereotypical partisan differences. The reverse pattern occurred after the terrorist attacks in 2001, when attention swung back towards external threats. Consistent with the mechanism of salience-modulated stereotyping, beliefs about political groups can shift dramatically even when the underlying partisan differences change little.

中文摘要

美国选民夸大了共和党人和民主党人在一系列社会经济和政治议题上态度的差异，且更大的感知极化与更高的政治参与度和情感极化相关。本文考察了这种感知党派差异的驱动因素。我们发现，一个刻板印象模型（其中对选民更显著的议题扭曲更强）捕捉了数据的重要特征。首先，感知的党派差异可根据党派间的实际差异（特别是极端态度的相对普遍性）进行预测。其次，在个人认为更重要的议题上，感知的党派差异更大。第三，议题显著性增加了过度重视极端类型的倾向。利用具有全国代表性的调查数据，我们表明1991年冷战结束（将美国选民的注意力从外部威胁转移开）增加了国内议题上感知的（相对于实际的）党派差异。这种上升在具有更刻板党派差异的议题上更为强烈。2001年恐怖袭击后，当注意力重新转向外部威胁时，出现了相反的模式。与显著性调节刻板印象的机制一致，即使潜在的党派差异变化很小，对政治群体的信念也可能发生剧烈转变。

No. 99论文详情NBER w27193

The Declining Worker Power Hypothesis: An explanation for the recent evolution of the American economy

工人权力下降假说：对美国经济近期演变的解释

Anna Stansbury, Lawrence H. Summers

Abstract

Rising profitability and market valuations of US businesses, sluggish wage growth and a declining labor share of income, and reduced unemployment and inflation, have defined the macroeconomic environment of the last generation. This paper offers a unified explanation for these phenomena based on reduced worker power. Using individual, industry, and state-level data, we demonstrate that measures of reduced worker power are associated with lower wage levels, higher pr ofit shares, and reductions in measures of the NAIRU. We argue that the declining worker power hypothesis is more compelling as an explanation for observed changes than increases in firms’ market power, both because it can simultaneously explain a falling labor share and a reduced NAIRU, and because it is more directly supported by the data.

中文摘要

美国企业盈利能力和市场估值上升、工资增长乏力与劳动收入份额下降、以及失业率和通胀降低，定义了上一代的宏观经济环境。本文基于工人权力下降为这些现象提供了一个统一解释。利用个人、行业和州层面的数据，我们证明工人权力下降的衡量指标与较低的工资水平、较高的利润份额以及NAIRU衡量指标的降低相关。我们认为，工人权力下降假说作为观察到的变化的解释比企业市场势力增加更有说服力，因为它既能同时解释劳动份额下降和NAIRU降低，又更直接地得到数据支持。

Language Barriers, Technology Adoption and Productivity: Evidence from Agriculture in India

语言障碍、技术采用与生产率：来自印度农业的证据

Apoorv Gupta, Jacopo Ponticelli, Andrea Tesei

Abstract

We study the effect of language barriers on the ability of farmers to access information about agricultural technologies in rural areas of India. We use call- level data from a government-sponsored call center for agricultural advice offered in different languages across Indian states. Exploiting differences in the language spoken by farmers and call center advisors, we document that language barriers limit the adoption of modern agricultural technologies—such as high-yielding variety seeds. We find no impact of language barriers on agricultural productivity within five years from introduction of call centers, although small but significant differences arise in the longer run.

中文摘要

我们研究了语言障碍对印度农村地区农民获取农业技术信息能力的影响。我们使用了政府资助的农业咨询呼叫中心（以不同语言在印度各邦提供服务）的通话层面数据。利用农民与呼叫中心顾问所说语言的差异，我们证明语言障碍限制了现代农业技术（如高产品种种子）的采用。我们发现，在呼叫中心引入后的五年内，语言障碍对农业生产率没有影响，尽管在长期内出现了微小但显著的差异。

No. 101论文详情NBER w27191

COVID-19 and Emerging Markets: A SIR Model, Demand Shocks and Capital Flows

COVID-19与新兴市场：SIR模型、需求冲击与资本流动

Cem Çakmaklı, Selva Demiralp, Ṣebnem Kalemli-Özcan, Sevcan Yesiltas, Muhammed A. Yildirim

Abstract

We quantify the macroeconomic effects of COVID-19 for a small open economy. We use a two country framework combined with a sectoral-SIR model to estimate the effects of collapses in foreign demand and supply. The small open economy suffers from domestic demand and supply shocks due to its own pandemic. In addition, there are external shocks coming from rest of the world (country two). Aggregate exports of the small open economy go down when foreign demand goes down, and aggregate imports suffer from lockdowns in the rest of the world. We calibrate the model to Turkey. Our results show that the optimal policy, which yields the lowest output loss and saves the maximum number of lives, for the small open economy, is an early and globally coordinated full lockdown of 39 days.

中文摘要

我们量化了COVID-19对一个小型开放经济的宏观经济影响。我们使用一个两国框架结合部门SIR模型来估计外国需求和供给崩溃的影响。该小型开放经济因其自身疫情而遭受国内需求和供给冲击。此外，还有来自世界其他地区（国家二）的外部冲击。当外国需求下降时，小型开放经济的总出口下降，而总进口则因世界其他地区的封锁而受损。我们将模型校准到土耳其。我们的结果表明，对于小型开放经济，能产生最低产出损失并挽救最多生命的最优政策是早期且全球协调的39天全面封锁。

How Sticky is Retirement Behavior in the U.S.? Responses to Changes in the Full Retirement Age

美国退休行为有多粘性？对全额退休年龄变化的反应

Manasi Deshpande, Itzik Fadlon, Colin Gray

Abstract

We study how increases in the Social Security full retirement age (FRA) affect benefit claiming and retirement behavior, and specifically the interaction between these two choices. Using Social Security administrative data, we implement complementary research designs of a traditional cohort analysis and a regression-discontinuity design. We find that while increases in the FRA strongly and immediately shift claiming ages, retirement ages exhibit persistent "stickiness" at the old FRA of 65. We use several strategies to explore the likely mechanisms behind the stickiness in retirement, and we find suggestive evidence of a role for employers in individuals' responses to the FRA.

中文摘要

我们研究社会保障全额退休年龄（FRA）的提高如何影响福利申领和退休行为，特别是这两种选择之间的相互作用。利用社会保障行政数据，我们实施了传统队列分析和断点回归设计的互补研究设计。我们发现，虽然FRA的提高强烈且立即地改变了申领年龄，但退休年龄在旧的65岁FRA处表现出持续的“粘性”。我们使用多种策略来探索退休粘性背后的可能机制，并发现雇主在个人对FRA的反应中发挥作用的暗示性证据。

Trust and Insurance Contracts

信任与保险合同

Nicola Gennaioli, Rafael La Porta, Florencio Lopez-de-Silanes, Andrei Shleifer

Abstract

We assemble and analyze a new data set of homeowner insurance claims from 28 independently operated country subsidiaries of a multinational insurance company. A fundamental feature of the data is that such claims are often disputed, and lead to rejections or lower payments. We propose a new model of insurance, in which consumers can make invalid claims and firms can deny valid claims. In this environment, trust and honesty are critical factors that shape insurance contracts and the payment of claims, especially when the disputed amounts are too small for courts. We characterize equilibrium insurance contracts, and show how they depend on the quality of the legal system and the level of trust. We then investigate the incidence of claims, disputes and rejections of claims, and payment of claims in our data, as well as the cost and pricing of insurance. The evidence is consistent with the centrality of trust for insurance markets, as predicted by the model.

中文摘要

我们收集并分析了一家跨国保险公司28个独立运营的国家子公司的新房主保险索赔数据集。该数据的一个基本特征是，此类索赔经常引发争议，并导致拒赔或赔付减少。我们提出了一个新的保险模型，其中消费者可能提出无效索赔，而公司可能拒绝有效索赔。在这种环境下，信任和诚实是塑造保险合同和索赔支付的关键因素，尤其是在争议金额太小而无法诉诸法庭时。我们刻画了均衡保险合同，并展示了它们如何依赖于法律体系的质量和信任水平。然后，我们考察了数据中索赔、争议和拒赔的发生率以及赔付情况，以及保险的成本和定价。证据与模型预测的信任对保险市场的核心重要性一致。

No. 104论文详情NBER w27188

Public Procurement in Law and Practice

法律与实践中的公共采购

Erica Bosio, Simeon Djankov, Edward L. Glaeser, Andrei Shleifer

Abstract

We examine a new data set of laws and practices governing public procurement, as well as procurement outcomes, in 187 countries. We measure regulation as restrictions on discretion of the procuring agents. We find that laws and practices are highly correlated with each other across countries, better practices are correlated with better outcomes, but laws themselves are not correlated with outcomes. To shed light on this puzzle, we present a model of procurement in which both regulation and public sector capacity determine the efficiency of procurement. In the model, regulation is effective in countries with low public sector capacity, and detrimental in countries with high public sector capacity because it inhibits the socially optimal exercise of discretion. We find evidence broadly consistent with this prediction: regulation of procurement improves outcomes, but only in countries with low public sector capacity.

中文摘要

我们考察了187个国家关于公共采购的法律、实践以及采购结果的新数据集。我们将监管衡量为对采购代理人自由裁量权的限制。我们发现，各国的法律与实践高度相关，更好的实践与更好的结果相关，但法律本身与结果不相关。为阐明这一难题，我们提出了一个采购模型，其中监管和公共部门能力共同决定采购效率。在该模型中，监管在公共部门能力低的国家有效，而在公共部门能力高的国家则有害，因为它抑制了社会最优的自由裁量权行使。我们发现了与这一预测大致一致的证据：采购监管改善了结果，但仅限于公共部门能力低的国家。

The Relationship between In-Person Voting and COVID-19: Evidence from the Wisconsin Primary

现场投票与COVID-19之间的关系：来自威斯康星州初选的证据

Chad D. Cotti, Bryan Engelhardt, Joshua Foster, Erik T. Nesson, Paul S. Niekamp

Abstract

On April 7, 2020, Wisconsin held its presidential primary election, and news reports showed long lines of voters due to fewer polling locations. We use county-level variation in voting patterns and weekly county-level COVID test data to examine whether in-person voting increased COVID-19 cases. We ﬁnd a statistically signiﬁcant association between in-person voting density and the spread of COVID-19 two to three weeks after the election. In our main results, a 10% increase in in-person voters per polling location is associated with an 18.4% increase in the COVID-19 positive test rate two to three weeks later.\n

中文摘要

2020年4月7日，威斯康星州举行了总统初选，新闻报道显示由于投票点减少，选民排起了长队。我们利用县级投票模式的差异和每周县级COVID检测数据，考察现场投票是否增加了COVID-19病例。我们发现，现场投票密度与选举后两到三周COVID-19的传播之间存在统计上显著的关联。在我们的主要结果中，每个投票点的现场选民人数增加10%，与两到三周后COVID-19阳性检测率增加18.4%相关。

No. 106论文详情NBER w27186

Confidence Management in Tournaments

锦标赛中的信心管理

Shanglyu Deng, Hanming Fang, Qiang Fu, Zenan Wu

Abstract

An incumbent employee competes against a new hire for bonus or promotion. The incumbent’s ability is commonly known, while that of the new hire is private information. The incumbent is subject to a perceptional bias: His prior about the new hire’s type differs from the true underlying distribution. He can be either ex ante overconfident or underconfident. We first explore whether a firm that aims to maximize aggregate effort would benefit or suffer from the bias. It is shown that debiasing may not be productive in incentivizing efforts. We then study the optimal information disclosure policy. The firm is allowed to ex ante commit to whether an informative signal—which allows the incumbent to infer the new hire’s type—will be disclosed publicly. We fully characterize the conditions under which transparency or opacity will prevail. We further take a Bayesian persuasion approach to optimally design the firm’s evaluation and feedback structure. We also consider an alternative context in which the manager is concerned about the expected winner’s effort. We demonstrate that the insights obtained from the baseline setting remain intact. Our results shed light on the extensive discussion of confidence management in firms and the debate about organizational transparency.

中文摘要

一名在职员工与一名新员工竞争奖金或晋升。在职员工的能力是众所周知的，而新员工的能力是私人信息。在职员工存在认知偏差：他对新员工类型的先验信念与真实潜在分布不同。他可能事前过度自信或信心不足。我们首先探讨一个旨在最大化总努力水平的公司是否会从这种偏差中受益或受损。结果表明，去偏差可能不利于激励努力。然后我们研究最优信息披露政策。公司被允许事前承诺是否公开披露一个信息信号——该信号允许在职员工推断新员工的类型。我们完全刻画了透明或不透明政策占优的条件。我们进一步采用贝叶斯说服方法，最优地设计公司的评估和反馈结构。我们还考虑了一个替代情境，其中管理者关注预期获胜者的努力水平。我们证明，从基准设定中获得的见解仍然成立。我们的研究结果为关于公司信心管理和组织透明度的广泛讨论提供了启示。

No. 107论文详情NBER w27185

Accounting for Global COVID-19 Diffusion Patterns, January-April 2020

解释2020年1月至4月全球COVID-19传播模式

Yothin Jinjarak, Rashad Ahmed, Sameer Nair-Desai, Weining Xin, Joshua Aizenman

Abstract

Key factors in modeling a pandemic and guiding policy-making include mortality rates associated with infections; the ability of government policies, medical systems, and society to adapt to the changing dynamics of a pandemic; and institutional and demographic characteristics affecting citizens’ perceptions and behavioral responses to stringent policies. This paper traces the cross-country associations between COVID-19 mortality, policy interventions aimed at limiting social contact, and their interactions with institutional and demographic characteristics. We document that, with a lag, more stringent pandemic policies were associated with lower mortality growth rates. The association between stricter pandemic policies and lower future mortality growth is more pronounced in countries with a greater proportion of the elderly population and urban population, greater democratic freedoms, and larger international travel flows. Countries with greater policy stringency in place prior to the first death realized lower peak mortality rates and exhibited lower durations to the first mortality peak. In contrast, countries with higher initial mobility saw higher peak mortality rates in the first phase of the pandemic, and countries with a larger elderly population, a greater share of employees in vulnerable occupations, and a higher level of democracy took longer to reach their peak mortalities. Our results suggest that policy interventions are effective at slowing the geometric pattern of mortality growth, reducing the peak mortality, and shortening the duration to the first peak. We also shed light on the importance of institutional and demographic characteristics in guiding policy-making for future waves of the pandemic.

中文摘要

建模大流行病和指导政策制定的关键因素包括：与感染相关的死亡率；政府政策、医疗系统和社会适应大流行病动态变化的能力；以及影响公民对严格政策的认知和行为反应的制度和人口特征。本文追踪了COVID-19死亡率、旨在限制社交接触的政策干预措施及其与制度和人口特征相互作用的国家间关联。我们记录到，在滞后一段时间后，更严格的大流行病政策与较低的死亡率增长率相关。在老年人口和城市人口比例更高、民主自由程度更高以及国际旅行流量更大的国家，更严格的大流行病政策与未来死亡率增长降低之间的关联更为显著。在首例死亡发生前已实施更严格政策的国家，实现了更低的峰值死亡率，并且达到首次死亡率峰值的时间更短。相比之下，初始流动性较高的国家在大流行病第一阶段经历了更高的峰值死亡率；而老年人口比例较大、脆弱职业员工比例较高以及民主程度较高的国家，达到死亡率峰值所需时间更长。我们的结果表明，政策干预在减缓死亡率增长的几何模式、降低峰值死亡率以及缩短达到首次峰值的时间方面是有效的。我们还揭示了制度和人口特征在指导未来大流行病浪潮政策制定中的重要性。
