The Size and Life-cycle Growth of Plants: The Role of Productivity, Demand and Wedges

企业的规模与生命周期增长：生产率、需求和楔子的作用

Marcela Eslava, John C. Haltiwanger

Abstract

We develop a framework that uses price and quantity information on both establishments' outputs and inputs to assess the roles, on establishment dynamics and welfare, of technical efficiency, input prices, demand/quality, idiosyncratic markups, and residual wedges. Our strategy nests previous approaches limited by data availability. In our application, demand/quality is found to dominate the cross sectional variability of sales and sales growth, while quality-adjusted input prices and residual wedges play dampening roles, especially at birth. Markups play only a modest role for cross-sectional variability of sales and sales growth but are important in explaining welfare losses from revenue productivity dispersion.

No. 109论文详情NBER w27183

Launching with a Parachute: The Gig Economy and New Business Formation

带着降落伞创业：零工经济与新企业形成

John M. Barrios, Yael V. Hochberg, Hanyi Yi

Abstract

The introduction of the gig economy creates opportunities for would-be entrepreneurs to supplement their income in downside states of the world and provides insurance in the form of an income fallback in the event of failure. We present a conceptual framework supporting the notion that the gig economy may serve as an income supplement and as insurance against entrepreneurial-related income volatility, and utilize the arrival of the on-demand, platform-enabled gig economy in the form of the staggered rollout of ridehailing in U.S. cities to examine the effect of the arrival of the gig economy on new business formation. The introduction of gig opportunities is associated with an increase of ~5% in the number of new business registrations in the local area, and a correspondingly-sized increase in small business lending to newly registered businesses. Internet searches for entrepreneurship-related keywords increase ~7%, lending further credence to the predictions of our conceptual framework. Both the income supplement and insurance channels are empirically supported: the increase in entry is larger in regions with lower average income and higher credit constraints, as well as in locations with higher ex-ante economic uncertainty regarding future wage levels and wage growth.

中文摘要

零工经济的引入为潜在企业家创造了机会，使他们能够在世界状况不佳时补充收入，并在失败时以收入退路的形式提供保险。我们提出了一个概念框架，支持零工经济可以作为收入补充和针对创业相关收入波动的保险的观点，并利用按需、平台驱动的零工经济的到来——以美国城市网约车服务分阶段推出的形式——来考察零工经济的出现对新企业形成的影响。零工机会的引入与当地新企业注册数量增加约5%相关，同时向新注册企业的小企业贷款也相应增加。与创业相关的关键词的互联网搜索量增加了约7%，这进一步证实了我们概念框架的预测。收入补充和保险渠道都得到了实证支持：在平均收入较低和信贷约束较高的地区，以及在未来工资水平和工资增长的事前经济不确定性较高的地区，企业进入的增加幅度更大。

No. 110论文详情NBER w27182

Latent Dirichlet Analysis of Categorical Survey Expectations

分类调查预期的潜在狄利克雷分析

Evan M. Munro, Serena Ng

Abstract

Beliefs are important determinants of an individual's choices and economic outcomes, so understanding how they differ across individuals is of considerable interest. Researchers often rely on surveys that report individual expectations as qualitative data. We propose using a Bayesian hierarchical latent class model to summarize and interpret observed heterogeneity in categorical expectations data. We show that the statistical model corresponds to an economic structural model of information acquisition, which guides interpretation and estimation of the model parameters. An algorithm based on stochastic optimization is proposed to estimate a model for repeated surveys when beliefs follow a dynamic structure and conjugate priors are not appropriate. Guidance on selecting the number of belief types is also provided. Two examples are considered. The first shows that there is information in the Michigan survey responses beyond the consumer sentiment index that is officially published. The second shows that belief types constructed from survey responses can be used in a subsequent analysis to estimate heterogeneous returns to education.

中文摘要

信念是个人选择和经济结果的重要决定因素，因此理解信念在个体间的差异具有相当大的研究价值。研究人员通常依赖以定性数据形式报告个人预期的调查。我们提出使用贝叶斯分层潜在类别模型来总结和解释分类预期数据中观察到的异质性。我们表明，该统计模型对应于一个信息获取的经济结构模型，这指导了模型参数的解读和估计。当信念遵循动态结构且共轭先验不适用时，提出了一种基于随机优化的算法来估计重复调查的模型。还提供了选择信念类型数量的指导。考虑了三个例子。第一个例子表明，密歇根调查的回应中除了官方发布的消费者情绪指数外，还包含信息。第二个例子表明，从调查回应构建的信念类型可以在后续分析中用于估计教育回报的异质性。

No. 111论文详情NBER w27181

Innovation in the U.S. Government

美国政府的创新

Joshua R. Bruce, John M. de Figueiredo

Abstract

This paper examines the U.S. government’s intramural research and development efforts over a 40-year period, drawing together multiple human capital, government spending, and patent datasets. The U.S. Federal Government innovates along four dimensions: technological, organizational, regulatory, and policy. After discussing these dimensions, the paper focuses on the inputs to and outputs of government intramural technological innovation. We measure innovative effort and results by accounting for the government scientists and dollars committed to R&D and patents created with government involvement. Overall, we show that intramural innovations, measured by government-assigned patents, are slightly more original and general, but less cited, than patents awarded to private-sector companies and extramural organizations patenting in the same technology classes. The majority of the 200,000 federal government scientists work at the Department of Defense, the Department of Energy, and NASA, and are largely in physical science and engineering occupations; the scientific expertise of other agencies is heavily weighted toward mathematics, social sciences, and data analytics. As these latter disciplines’ innovative outputs are less readily catalogued with patents, measuring total government innovative output with government-assigned patents is likely to over-emphasize innovations in engineering and physical sciences while under-reporting intramural innovations in other disciplines. We discuss the implications of our findings for both public- and private-sector innovation efforts and pose questions for future research.

中文摘要

本文考察了美国政府在40年期间的内部研发努力，汇集了多个人力资本、政府支出和专利数据集。美国联邦政府在四个维度上进行创新：技术、组织、监管和政策。在讨论这些维度之后，本文聚焦于政府内部技术创新的投入和产出。我们通过统计投入研发的政府科学家和资金以及涉及政府参与的专利，来衡量创新努力和成果。总体而言，我们表明，与在同一技术类别中申请专利的私营企业和外部组织获得的专利相比，以政府授权专利衡量的内部创新在原创性和通用性上略高，但被引次数较少。20万名联邦政府科学家中的大多数在国防部、能源部和NASA工作，主要从事物理科学和工程职业；其他机构的科学专业知识则严重偏向数学、社会科学和数据分析。由于这些后一类学科的创新产出不易通过专利进行编目，因此用政府授权专利来衡量政府总创新产出可能会过度强调工程和物理科学的创新，而低估其他学科的内部创新。我们讨论了我们的发现对公共和私营部门创新努力的影响，并提出了未来研究的问题。

No. 112论文详情NBER w27180

The Incidence of Foreign Market Accessibility on Farmland Rental Rates

国外市场可及性对农田租金率的影响

Jisang Yu, Nelson B. Villoria, Nathan P. Hendricks

Abstract

We estimate the impact of the tariffs that U.S. export crops face on farmland rental rates. The estimation of the impact of the localized measure on the rents faces two aggregation problems that lead to identification challenges: a) aggregating tariffs across trading partners to obtain crop-specific tariffs, and b) aggregating the crop-specific tariffs across crops to obtain the localized measure. Utilizing shift-share style approaches, we find that a one percent increase in the localized tariff reduces the rents by about 2.6 - 5.3% point, which implies that the 2018 Chinese retaliatory tariffs would reduce the rents by about 2%.

中文摘要

我们估算了美国出口作物面临的关税对农田租金率的影响。估算本地化指标对租金的影响面临两个导致识别挑战的加总问题：a) 将各贸易伙伴的关税加总为作物特定关税，以及b) 将作物特定关税跨作物加总以获得本地化指标。利用份额转移类方法，我们发现本地化关税每增加1%，租金率下降约2.6至5.3个百分点，这意味着2018年中国报复性关税将使租金率下降约2%。

No. 113论文详情NBER w27179

Savings and Saving Rates: Up or Down?

储蓄与储蓄率：上升还是下降？

Guillermo Ordoñez, Facundo Piguillem

Abstract

It depends what we want to measure. Most literature has focused on observed flow of savings (per-period savings as fraction of GDP), which has declined persistently since 1980. Even though this decline means that fewer funds are available for investment in each period, it does not follow that the households’ actual savings (underlying, not observed, savings determined by dynamic optimization) also go down. We theoretically link these two concepts, discuss the conditions under which they move in opposite directions, and show that indeed the actual savings has sharply increased since 1980.

中文摘要

这取决于我们想要衡量什么。大多数文献关注的是观察到的储蓄流量（每期储蓄占GDP的比重），自1980年以来这一指标持续下降。尽管这种下降意味着每期可用于投资的资金减少，但这并不意味着家庭的实际储蓄（由动态优化决定的潜在储蓄，而非观察到的储蓄）也会下降。我们从理论上将这两个概念联系起来，讨论了它们朝相反方向变动的条件，并表明自1980年以来实际储蓄确实大幅增加。

No. 114论文详情NBER w27178

Deliberate Surrender? The Impact of Interwar Indian Protection

有意的牺牲？两次世界大战期间印度保护主义的影响

Vellore Arthi, Markus Lampe, Ashwin R Nair, Kevin Hjortshøj O'Rourke

Abstract

What is the role of trade policy in promoting intra-Empire trade? We address the question in the context of interwar India, whose trade policies have been accused of harming British export interests. We quantify the impact of trade policy on the value and composition of Indian imports, using novel disaggregated data on both trade policies and imports for 114 commodity categories coming from 42 countries. We find that even though Indian protection lowered total imports, it substantially boosted imports from the UK. Despite the rising tariff barriers facing British exporters, trade diversion from other countries ensured that Indian trade policy benefited them overall.

中文摘要

贸易政策在促进帝国内部贸易中扮演什么角色？我们在两次世界大战期间印度的背景下探讨这个问题，印度的贸易政策曾被指责损害了英国的出口利益。我们利用来自42个国家的114个商品类别的新颖细分数据，量化了贸易政策对印度进口价值和构成的影响。我们发现，尽管印度的保护主义降低了总进口，但它显著促进了从英国的进口。尽管英国出口商面临不断上升的关税壁垒，但从其他国家的贸易转移确保了印度的贸易政策总体上使英国受益。

No. 115论文详情NBER w27177

The Economic Impact of Access to Public Four-Year Colleges

进入公立四年制大学的经济影响

Jonathan Smith, Joshua Goodman, Michael Hurwitz

Abstract

We estimate the economic impacts of students’ access to an entire sector of U.S. public higher education. Approximately half of Georgia high school graduates who enroll in college do so in the state’s public four-year sector, which requires minimum SAT scores for admission. Regression discontinuity estimates show enrollment in public four-year institutions boosts students’ estimated household income around age 30 by about 17 percent and has even larger impacts for those from low-income high schools. Access to this sector has little clear impact on financial health or student loan balances. For the marginal student, and particularly for those from low-income high schools, enrollment in such institutions has large private returns in the short run and positive returns to state budgets in the long run.

中文摘要

我们估算了学生进入美国公立高等教育整个部门的经济影响。在佐治亚州，大约一半高中毕业生在进入大学时选择该州的公立四年制大学，这些大学要求最低SAT分数才能入学。断点回归估计显示，进入公立四年制大学可使学生在30岁左右的预估家庭收入提高约17%，对来自低收入高中的学生影响更大。进入这一部门对财务健康或学生贷款余额几乎没有明显影响。对于边缘学生，尤其是来自低收入高中的学生，进入这类大学在短期内具有较大的私人回报，长期内对州预算具有正向回报。

No. 116论文详情NBER w27176

Estimating Probabilities of Success of Vaccine and Other Anti-Infective Therapeutic Development Programs

估算疫苗及其他抗感染治疗开发项目的成功概率

Andrew W. Lo, Kien Wei Siah, Chi Heem Wong

Abstract

A key driver in biopharmaceutical investment decisions is the probability of success of a drug development program. We estimate the probabilities of success (PoSs) of clinical trials for vaccines and other anti-infective therapeutics using 43,414 unique triplets of clinical trial, drug, and disease between January 1, 2000, and January 7, 2020, yielding 2,544 vaccine programs and 6,829 nonvaccine programs targeting infectious diseases. The overall estimated PoS for an industry-sponsored vaccine program is 39.6%, and 16.3% for an industry-sponsored anti-infective therapeutic. Among industry-sponsored vaccines programs, only 12 out of 27 disease categories have seen at least one approval, with the most successful being against monkeypox (100%), rotavirus (78.7%), and Japanese encephalitis (67.6%). The three infectious diseases with the highest PoSs for industry-sponsored nonvaccine therapeutics are smallpox (100%), cytomegalovirus (CMV) infection (31.8%), and onychomycosis (29.8%). Non-industry-sponsored vaccine and nonvaccine development programs have lower overall PoSs: 6.8% and 8.2%, respectively. Viruses involved in recent outbreaks—Middle East respiratory syndrome (MERS), severe acute respiratory syndrome (SARS), Ebola, and Zika—have had a combined total of only 45 nonvaccine development programs initiated over the past two decades, and no approved therapy to date. These estimates offer guidance both to biopharma investors as well as to policymakers seeking to identify areas most likely to be underserved by private sector engagement and in need of public sector support.

中文摘要

生物制药投资决策的一个关键驱动因素是药物开发项目的成功概率。我们利用2000年1月1日至2020年1月7日期间43,414个独特的临床试验、药物和疾病三元组，估算了疫苗和其他抗感染治疗临床试验的成功概率，涉及2,544个疫苗项目和6,829个针对传染病的非疫苗项目。行业赞助的疫苗项目的总体估计成功概率为39.6%，行业赞助的抗感染治疗项目的成功概率为16.3%。在行业赞助的疫苗项目中，27个疾病类别中只有12个至少获得一次批准，最成功的项目针对猴痘（100%）、轮状病毒（78.7%）和日本脑炎（67.6%）。行业赞助的非疫苗治疗项目中成功概率最高的三种传染病是天花（100%）、巨细胞病毒感染（31.8%）和甲癣（29.8%）。非行业赞助的疫苗和非疫苗开发项目的总体成功概率较低，分别为6.8%和8.2%。涉及近期疫情暴发的病毒——中东呼吸综合征、严重急性呼吸综合征、埃博拉和寨卡——在过去二十年中总共只启动了45个非疫苗开发项目，且至今没有获批的治疗方法。这些估计为生物制药投资者以及寻求识别最可能缺乏私营部门参与并需要公共部门支持的领域的政策制定者提供了指导。

No. 117论文详情NBER w27175

Bayesian Adaptive Clinical Trials for Anti‐Infective Therapeutics during Epidemic Outbreaks

疫情暴发期间抗感染治疗的贝叶斯自适应临床试验

Shomesh Chaudhuri, Andrew W. Lo, Danying Xiao, Qingyang Xu

Abstract

In the midst of epidemics such as COVID-19, therapeutic candidates are unlikely to be able to complete the usual multiyear clinical trial and regulatory approval process within the course of an outbreak. We apply a Bayesian adaptive patient-centered model—which minimizes the expected harm of false positives and false negatives—to optimize the clinical trial development path during such outbreaks. When the epidemic is more infectious and fatal, the Bayesian-optimal sample size in the clinical trial is lower and the optimal statistical significance level is higher. For COVID-19 (assuming a static <i>R</i>₀ – 2 and initial infection percentage of 0.1%), the optimal significance level is 7.1% for a clinical trial of a nonvaccine anti-infective therapeutic and 13.6% for that of a vaccine. For a dynamic <i>R</i>₀ decreasing from 3 to 1.5, the corresponding values are 14.4% and 26.4%, respectively. Our results illustrate the importance of adapting the clinical trial design and the regulatory approval process to the specific parameters and stage of the epidemic.

中文摘要

在COVID-19等疫情中，治疗候选药物不太可能在疫情暴发期间完成通常需要多年的临床试验和监管审批流程。我们应用一种以患者为中心的贝叶斯自适应模型——该模型最小化假阳性和假阴性的预期危害——来优化此类疫情中的临床试验开发路径。当疫情更具传染性和致命性时，贝叶斯最优的临床试验样本量较低，而最优统计显著性水平较高。对于COVID-19（假设静态R₀为2，初始感染百分比为0.1%），非疫苗抗感染治疗临床试验的最优显著性水平为7.1%，疫苗临床试验为13.6%。对于动态R₀从3降至1.5的情况，相应值分别为14.4%和26.4%。我们的结果说明了根据疫情的具体参数和阶段调整临床试验设计和监管审批流程的重要性。

The Influence of Early Life Health Conditions on Life Course Health

早期健康状况对生命历程健康的影响

Manuel Flores Mallo, Barbara L. Wolfe

Abstract

We expand on earlier studies investigating the links between early health and later health by including different dimensions of early-life health and multiple life course outcomes consisting of the age of onset of serious cardiovascular diseases (CVDs) and multiple job-related health outcomes. The four dimensions of childhood health are mental, physical, self-rated general health and severe headaches or migraines. The data set we use includes 21 countries from the Survey of Health, Ageing and Retirement in Europe. We find that the different dimensions of childhood health have unique ties to later outcomes. For men, early mental health problems play a stronger role for life course job-related health outcomes, but early poor or fair general health is more strongly linked to the spike in onset of CVDs in their late 40s. For women, these links between childhood health dimensions and life course outcomes are less clear-cut than for men. The spike in onset of CVDs in their late 40s is driven by those with severe headaches or migraines while those with early physical health problems generally do better as captured by job-related outcomes. We also explore and control for possible mediating factors and assess the importance of omitted variables using a test proposed by Oster (2019).

中文摘要

我们扩展了早期健康与后期健康之间联系的研究，纳入了早期健康的不同维度以及多个生命历程结果，包括严重心血管疾病的发病年龄和多个与工作相关的健康结果。儿童期健康的四个维度是心理健康、身体健康、自评总体健康以及严重头痛或偏头痛。我们使用的数据集包括来自欧洲健康、老龄化和退休调查的21个国家。我们发现，儿童期健康的不同维度与后期结果有独特的联系。对于男性，早期心理健康问题对生命历程中与工作相关的健康结果影响更大，但早期总体健康较差或一般与他们在40多岁后期心血管疾病发病高峰的关联更强。对于女性，儿童期健康维度与生命历程结果之间的联系不如男性明确。40多岁后期心血管疾病发病高峰是由那些有严重头痛或偏头痛的人驱动的，而早期有身体健康问题的人在与工作相关的结果方面通常表现更好。我们还探索并控制了可能的调节因素，并使用Oster（2019）提出的检验评估了遗漏变量的重要性。

No. 119论文详情NBER w27173

Effects of the COVID-19 Pandemic on Outpatient Providers in the US

COVID-19疫情对美国门诊服务提供者的影响

Pinka Chatterji, Yue Li

Abstract

There is growing concern that the COVID-19 pandemic may have severe, adverse effects on the health care sector, a sector of the economy that historically has been somewhat shielded from the business cycle. In this paper, we study one aspect of this issue by estimating the magnitude of the COVID-19 pandemic on use of outpatient health services. We use 2010-2020 data from the Outpatient Influenza-like Illness Surveillance Network (ILINet). Our findings indicate that the COVID-19 pandemic is associated with about a 67 percent decline in the total number of outpatient visits per provider by the week of April 12-18th, 2020 relative to the same week in prior years. Effects become apparent earlier in the pandemic for outpatient visits for non-flu symptoms, but we find negative effects on outpatient visits for flu symptoms as well.

中文摘要

Optimal Contracting with Altruistic Agents: A Structural Model of Medicare Payments for Dialysis Drugs

与利他主义代理人的最优契约：透析药物医疗保险支付的结构模型

Martin Gaynor, Nirav Mehta, Seth Richards-Shubik

Abstract

We study physician agency and optimal payment policy in the context of an expensive medication used in dialysis care. Using Medicare claims data we estimate a structural model of treatment decisions, in which physicians differ in their altruism and marginal costs, and this heterogeneity is unobservable to the government. In a novel application of nonlinear pricing methods, we theoretically characterize the optimal unrestricted contract in this screening environment with multidimensional heterogeneity. We combine these results with the estimated model to construct the optimal contract and simulate counterfactual outcomes. The optimal contract is a flexible fee-for-service contract, which pays for reported treatments but uses variable marginal payments instead of constant reimbursement rates, resulting in substantial health improvements and reductions in costs. Our structural approach also yields important qualitative findings, such as rejecting the optimality of any linear contract, and may be employed more broadly to analyze a variety of applications.

中文摘要

我们研究了在透析护理中使用的一种昂贵药物背景下的医生代理问题和最优支付政策。利用医疗保险索赔数据，我们估计了一个治疗决策的结构模型，其中医生在利他主义和边际成本方面存在差异，且这种异质性对政府不可观测。在非线性定价方法的新应用中，我们从理论上刻画了在这种具有多维异质性的筛选环境中的最优无限制契约。我们将这些结果与估计模型相结合，构建了最优契约并模拟了反事实结果。最优契约是一种灵活的按服务收费契约，它为报告的治疗付费，但使用可变边际支付而非固定报销率，从而带来显著的健康改善和成本降低。我们的结构方法还产生了重要的定性发现，例如拒绝了任何线性契约的最优性，并且可以更广泛地用于分析各种应用。

No. 121论文详情NBER w27171

China's Model of Managing the Financial System

中国金融管理体系模式

Markus K. Brunnermeier, Michael Sockin, Wei Xiong

Abstract

China's economic model involves active government intervention in financial markets. We develop a theoretical framework in which interventions prevent a market breakdown and a volatility explosion caused by the reluctance of short-term investors to trade against noise traders. In the presence of information frictions, the government can alter market dynamics since the noise in its intervention program becomes an additional factor driving asset prices. More importantly, this may divert investor attention away from fundamentals and totally toward government interventions (as a result of complementarity in investors' information acquisition). A trade-off arises: government's objective to reduce asset price volatility may worsen, rather than improve, information efficiency of asset prices.

中文摘要

中国的经济模式涉及政府对金融市场的积极干预。我们构建了一个理论框架，在该框架中，干预措施防止了因短期投资者不愿与噪音交易者交易而导致的市场崩溃和波动性爆发。在存在信息摩擦的情况下，政府可以改变市场动态，因为其干预计划中的噪音成为驱动资产价格的额外因素。更重要的是，这可能会将投资者的注意力从基本面完全转移到政府干预上（这是投资者信息获取互补性的结果）。由此产生了一种权衡：政府降低资产价格波动的目标可能会恶化而非改善资产价格的信息效率。

No. 122论文详情NBER w27170

The Accumulation of Human and Market Capital in the United States: The Long View, 1948–2013

美国人力资本与市场资本的积累：长期视角，1948–2013

Barbara M. Fraumeni, Michael S. Christian, Jon D. Samuels

Abstract

Over the 1948–2013 period, many factors significantly impacted on human capital, which in turn affected economic growth in the United States. This chapter analyzes these factors within a complete national income accounting system which integrates Jorgenson-Fraumeni human capital into the accounts. By including human capital, a fresh perspective on economic growth across time and within specific subperiods is revealed, notably regarding the 1995–2000 and 2007–2009 periods. During the 1995–2000 period, the reduction in human capital investment significantly reduced apparent economic growth. In the 2007–2009 period, the increase in human capital investment tempered the negative impact of the Great Recession. Over the longer time period, first the post-World War baby boom and then the substantial increase in education led to higher economic growth than otherwise expected. As the pace of increase in education slowed and the workforce aged toward the end of the period, human capital induced growth was reduced.

中文摘要

在1948年至2013年期间，许多因素显著影响了人力资本，进而影响了美国的经济增长。本章在一个完整的国民收入核算体系中分析了这些因素，该体系将乔根森-弗劳梅尼人力资本纳入核算。通过纳入人力资本，揭示了经济增长在时间跨度和特定子时期内的新视角，特别是关于1995–2000年和2007–2009年期间。在1995–2000年期间，人力资本投资的减少显著降低了表观经济增长。在2007–2009年期间，人力资本投资的增加缓和了大衰退的负面影响。在更长的时期内，首先是二战后婴儿潮，然后是教育的大幅提升，导致经济增长高于预期。随着教育增速放缓以及劳动力在期末老龄化，人力资本驱动的增长有所减弱。

No. 123论文详情NBER w27169

The Contribution of Chinese Diaspora Researchers to Global Science and China's Catching Up in Scientific Research

华人散居研究人员对全球科学的贡献及中国在科研领域的追赶

Qingnan Xie, Richard B. Freeman

Abstract

This study examines the contribution of Chinese diaspora researchers – those born in China but working outside the country – to China's catching up in global science to become a world leader in research publications and citations. Using a novel name-based way to identify Chinese diaspora authors of scientific papers, we show that these researchers produce a large proportion of global scientific papers of high quality, gaining about twice as many citations as other papers of the same vintage. Our analysis also shows that diaspora researchers are a critical node in the co-authorship and citation networks that connect scientific discovery in China with the rest of the world. In co-authorship, diaspora researchers are over-represented on international collaborations with China-addressed authors. In citations, a paper with a diaspora author is more likely to cite China-addressed papers than a non-China addressed paper without a diaspora author; and, commensurately, China-addressed papers are more likely to cite a non-China addressed paper with a diaspora author than a non-China paper without a diaspora author. Through those pathways, diaspora research contributed to China’s 2000-2015 catch-up in science and to global science writ large, consistent with ethnic network models of knowledge transfer, and contrary to brain drain fears that the emigration of researchers harms the source country.

中文摘要

本研究考察了华人散居研究人员——即出生在中国但在国外工作的人——对中国在全球科学领域追赶并成为研究论文和引用量世界领先者的贡献。通过一种新颖的基于姓名的方法来识别科学论文的华人散居作者，我们表明这些研究人员产出了全球高质量科学论文的很大一部分，其引用量约为同期其他论文的两倍。我们的分析还表明，散居研究人员是将中国的科学发现与世界其他地区联系起来的合著和引用网络中的关键节点。在合著方面，散居研究人员在与有中国地址作者的跨国合作中占比过高。在引用方面，有散居作者的论文比没有散居作者的非中国地址论文更有可能引用中国地址论文；相应地，中国地址论文比没有散居作者的非中国论文更有可能引用有散居作者的非中国地址论文。通过这些途径，散居研究为2000-2015年中国在科学领域的追赶以及全球科学整体做出了贡献，这与知识转移的族群网络模型一致，并且与研究人员移民损害来源国的“人才流失”担忧相反。

No. 124论文详情NBER w27168

When Selling Becomes Viral: Disruptions in Debt Markets in the COVID-19 Crisis and the Fed’s Response

当抛售变得具有传染性：COVID-19危机中债务市场的混乱与美联储的应对

Valentin Haddad, Alan Moreira, Tyler Muir

Abstract

We study disruptions in debt markets during the COVID-19 crisis. The safer end of the credit spectrum experienced significant losses that are hard to fully reconcile with standard default or risk premium channels. Corporate bonds traded at a large discount to their corresponding CDS, and this basis widened most for safer bonds. Liquid bond ETFs traded at a large discount to their NAV, more so for Treasuries, municipal bonds, and investment-grade corporate than high-yield corporate. These facts suggest investors tried to sell safer, more liquid securities to raise cash. These disruptions disappeared nearly as fast as they appeared. We trace this recovery back to the unprecedented actions the Fed took to purchase corporate bonds rather than its interventions in extending credit. The March 23rd announcement to buy investment-grade debt boosted prices and lowered bond spreads (particularly at shorter maturities and the safer end of investment-grade) while having virtually no effect on high-yield debt. April 9th, in contrast, had a large effect on both investment-grade and high-yield, even for the riskier end of high yield which would only indirectly benefit from the policy. These facts highlight the importance of financial frictions early on in the crisis, but also challenge existing theories of these frictions.

中文摘要

我们研究了COVID-19危机期间债务市场的混乱。信用谱系中较安全的一端经历了重大损失，这很难完全用标准的违约或风险溢价渠道来解释。公司债券相对于其相应的CDS以大幅折价交易，且这种基差在更安全的债券中扩大得最多。流动性强的债券ETF相对于其资产净值以大幅折价交易，国债、市政债券和投资级公司债的折价幅度大于高收益公司债。这些事实表明，投资者试图出售更安全、流动性更强的证券以筹集现金。这些混乱几乎与出现时一样迅速地消失了。我们将这种复苏追溯到美联储为购买公司债券而采取的前所未有的行动，而非其在扩大信贷方面的干预。3月23日宣布购买投资级债务的公告推高了价格并降低了债券利差（尤其是在较短期限和投资级中较安全的一端），同时对高收益债务几乎没有影响。相比之下，4月9日的公告对投资级和高收益债券都有很大影响，甚至对高收益中风险较高的端也是如此，而后者只会从该政策中间接受益。这些事实突显了危机早期金融摩擦的重要性，但也对这些摩擦的现有理论提出了挑战。

Using Disasters to Estimate the Impact of Uncertainty

利用灾难估计不确定性的影响

Scott R. Baker, Nicholas Bloom, Stephen J. Terry

Abstract

Uncertainty rises in recessions and falls in booms. But what is the causal relationship? We construct cross-country panel data on stock market returns to proxy for first- and second-moment shocks and instrument these with natural disasters, terrorist attacks, and political shocks. Our IV regression results reveal a robust negative short-term impact of second moments (uncertainty) on growth. Employing multiple VAR estimation approaches, relying on a range of identifying assumptions, also reveals a negative impact of uncertainty on growth. Finally, we show that these results are reproducible in a conventional micro-macro business cycle model with time-varying uncertainty.

中文摘要

不确定性在经济衰退时上升，在经济繁荣时下降。但因果关系是什么？我们构建了股票市场回报的跨国面板数据，以代理一阶和二阶矩冲击，并用自然灾害、恐怖袭击和政治冲击作为这些冲击的工具变量。我们的IV回归结果揭示了二阶矩（不确定性）对增长的稳健的短期负面影响。采用多种VAR估计方法，并依赖一系列识别假设，也揭示了不确定性对增长的负面影响。最后，我们表明这些结果可以在一个具有时变不确定性的传统微观-宏观商业周期模型中得到复现。

No. 126论文详情NBER w27166

Reopening Under COVID-19: What to Watch For

COVID-19下的重新开放：应关注什么

Jeffrey E. Harris

Abstract

We critically analyze the currently available status indicators of the COVID-19 epidemic so that state governors will have the guideposts necessary to decide whether to further loosen or instead retighten controls on social and economic activity. Overreliance on aggregate, state-level data in Wisconsin, we find, confounds the effects of the spring primary elections and the outbreak among meat packers. Relaxed testing standards in Los Angeles may have upwardly biased the observed trend in new infection rates. Reanalysis of New Jersey data, based upon the date an ultimately fatal case first became ill rather than the date of death, reveals that deaths have already peaked in that state. Evidence from Cook County, Illinois shows that trends in the percentage of positive tests can be wholly misleading. Trends on emergency department visits for influenza-like illness, advocated by the White House Guidelines, are unlikely to be informative. Data on hospital census counts in Orange County, California suggest that healthcare system-based indicators are likely to be more reliable and informative. An analysis of cumulative infections in San Antonio, Texas, shows how mathematical models intended to guide decisions on relaxation of social distancing are severely limited by untested assumptions. Universal coronavirus testing may not on its own solve difficult problems of data interpretation and causal inference.

中文摘要

我们批判性地分析了目前可用的COVID-19疫情状态指标，以便州长们拥有必要的路标来决定是进一步放松还是重新收紧对社会和经济活动的控制。我们发现，过度依赖威斯康星州的总体州级数据混淆了春季初选和肉类加工厂疫情爆发的影响。洛杉矶放宽的检测标准可能使观察到的感染率新趋势产生向上偏差。基于最终致命病例首次发病日期而非死亡日期对新泽西州数据的重新分析显示，该州的死亡人数已经达到峰值。来自伊利诺伊州库克县的证据表明，阳性检测百分比趋势可能完全具有误导性。白宫指南所倡导的因流感样疾病就诊的急诊科趋势不太可能提供信息。加利福尼亚州奥兰治县的医院住院人数数据显示，基于医疗保健系统的指标可能更可靠、信息量更大。对德克萨斯州圣安东尼奥市累计感染人数的分析表明，旨在指导放松社交距离决策的数学模型受到未经检验假设的严重限制。普遍的新冠病毒检测本身可能无法解决数据解释和因果推断的难题。

No. 127论文详情NBER w27165

The Economics of Time-Limited Development Options: The Case of Oil and Gas Leases

限时开发选择权的经济学：以油气租约为例

Evan M. Herrnstadt, Ryan Kellogg, Eric Lewis

Abstract

Oil and gas leases between mineral owners and extraction firms ubiquitously include royalty and primary term clauses. The royalty denotes the share of revenue that is paid to the mineral owner, and the primary term specifies the date by which the firm must complete a well, lest it lose the lease. Using data from the Louisiana shale boom, we first show that wells' drilling timing is substantially bunched just before lease expiration, raising the question of why leases include development deadlines that distort drilling decisions. We then develop a contracting model in which mineral owners face firms with private information and have the ability to contract on both realized revenue and drilling timing. We show that primary terms can increase both the owner's expected revenue and total surplus because they counteract the delay incentives imposed by the royalty.

中文摘要

矿产所有者与开采公司之间的油气租约普遍包含权利金和初始期限条款。权利金表示支付给矿产所有者的收入份额，初始期限则规定了公司必须完成一口井的日期，否则将失去租约。利用路易斯安那州页岩繁荣期的数据，我们首先表明钻井时机大量集中在租约到期之前，这引发了为何租约包含扭曲钻井决策的开发截止日期的问题。然后，我们构建了一个契约模型，其中矿产所有者面对拥有私人信息的公司，并且能够就实现的收入和钻井时机进行签约。我们表明，初始期限可以提高所有者的预期收入和总剩余，因为它们抵消了权利金施加的延迟激励。

No. 128论文详情NBER w27164

The Marginal Net Taxation of Americans’ Labor Supply

美国人劳动供给的边际净税收

David Altig, Alan J. Auerbach, Laurence J. Kotlikoff, Elias Ilin, Victor Ye

Abstract

The U.S. has a plethora of federal and state tax and benefit programs, each with its own work incentives and disincentives. This paper uses the Fiscal Analyzer (TFA) to assess how these policies, in unison, impact work incentives. TFA is a life-cycle, consumption-smoothing program that incorporates cash-flow constraints, retirement hazards, all major federal and state fiscal policies, and welfare-program-specific takeup rates. We use TFA in conjunction with the 2019 Survey of Consumer Finances to calculate Americans’ remaining lifetime marginal net tax rates (LMTR). Our findings are striking. Over half of working-age Americans face LMTRs exceeding 40 percent. One in four households in the bottom lifetime resource quintile face LMTRs above 50 percent. One in ten face rates above 70 percent, effectively locking them out of the labor force and into poverty. The richest 1 percent also face extremely high LMTRs with a 57.9 percent median rate. We find remarkable dispersion in both LMTRs and current-year marginal tax rates, not only across, but within states, age cohorts, and resource quintiles. Among those in the bottom quintile, 5.1 percent face LMTRs exceeding 100 percent; 4.5 percent face negative rates. Based on simplified excess burden calculations, eliminating the dispersion in marginal lifetime net taxation would produce efficiency gains of up to 24.1 percent of labor income for households in the bottom quintile where MTR dispersion is greatest.

中文摘要

美国有大量的联邦和州税收及福利项目，每个项目都有其自身的工作激励和抑制因素。本文使用财政分析器（TFA）来评估这些政策如何共同影响工作激励。TFA是一个生命周期消费平滑程序，它纳入了现金流约束、退休风险、所有主要的联邦和州财政政策以及特定福利项目的参与率。我们结合2019年消费者金融调查使用TFA来计算美国人剩余生命周期的边际净税率（LMTR）。我们的发现令人震惊。超过一半的适龄劳动美国人面临超过40%的LMTR。在生命周期资源最低的五分之一家庭中，有四分之一面临超过50%的LMTR。十分之一面临超过70%的税率，这实际上将他们锁在劳动力市场之外并陷入贫困。最富有的1%也面临极高的LMTR，中位数为57.9%。我们发现LMTR和当前年度边际税率都存在显著的离散性，不仅在不同州之间，而且在同一州内、不同年龄组和资源五分位组之间也是如此。在最低五分位组中，5.1%的人面临超过100%的LMTR；4.5%的人面临负税率。基于简化的超额负担计算，消除边际生命周期净税收的离散性将为最低五分位组（MTR离散性最大）的家庭带来高达劳动收入24.1%的效率收益。

Robbing Peter to Pay Paul: Understanding How State Tax Credits Impact Charitable Giving

拆东墙补西墙：理解州税收抵免如何影响慈善捐赠

Chandrayee Chatterjee, James C. Cox, Michael K. Price, Florian Rundhammer

Abstract

Donations to charity are widely encouraged by policymakers through targeted tax incentives such as tax credits for contributions only to qualifying causes. We use a framed field experiment to test how the largest such program, Arizona’s state income tax credit for donations to qualifying charities, affects donation decisions in a modified dictator game. In the experiment, we randomize whether subjects receive detailed information about the tax credit program prior to selecting potential recipients and completing the allocation task. We also vary the number of charities that subjects can select as recipients along with the (tax-credit) qualifying vs. non-qualifying composition of the choice set. We find that average giving is unaffected by the information provision and composition of the choice set. However, subjects direct significantly more funds towards qualifying charities when provided information about the tax program; an effect that is enhanced when subjects select multiple recipients from lists that contain a mixture of qualifying and non-qualifying organizations. Our results underline the importance of including a portfolio of choices when studying the impact of targeted incentives because this makes it possible to identify a central feature of our data: participants “rob Peter” (non-qualifying charities) “to pay Paul” (qualifying charities).

中文摘要

政策制定者通过有针对性的税收激励措施（例如仅对符合条件的捐赠提供税收抵免）广泛鼓励向慈善机构捐款。我们使用一个框架性实地实验来测试最大的此类项目——亚利桑那州对符合条件慈善机构捐赠的州所得税抵免——如何在修改后的独裁者游戏中影响捐赠决策。在实验中，我们在受试者选择潜在受助方并完成分配任务之前，随机化他们是否收到关于税收抵免计划的详细信息。我们还改变了受试者可以选择作为受助方的慈善机构数量，以及选择集中（税收抵免）合格与非合格机构的构成。我们发现，平均捐赠不受信息提供和选择集构成的影响。然而，当受试者获得有关税收计划的信息时，他们会将显著更多的资金导向符合条件的慈善机构；当受试者从包含合格和非合格组织混合的列表中选择多个受助方时，这种效应会增强。我们的结果强调了在研究针对性激励措施的影响时纳入投资组合选择的重要性，因为这使得识别我们数据的一个核心特征成为可能：参与者“拆东墙”（非合格慈善机构）“补西墙”（合格慈善机构）。

College Achievement and Attainment Gaps: Evidence from West Point Cadets

大学成就与毕业差距：来自西点军校学员的证据

Dario Cestau, Dennis Epple, Richard Romano, Holger Sieg, Carl Wojtaszek

Abstract

Assessing the effectiveness of education by race and gender is as difficult as it is important. We investigate this question utilizing data for eleven cohorts at West Point, a distinguished military academy and highly ranked liberal arts college. Employing matching using entry scores on three comprehensive measures, we obtain exceptional matches of score distributions for black and matched white students. We find black students have lower graduating achievement scores than matched white students, but comparable rates of graduation, retention in the Army after graduation, and early promotion. Hispanic-white comparisons reveal no differences. Female-male comparisons reveal women have lower attainment and retention rates.

中文摘要

评估教育在种族和性别方面的有效性既困难又重要。我们利用西点军校（一所杰出的军事学院和排名靠前的文理学院）十一届学员的数据来研究这个问题。使用三项综合指标的入学分数进行匹配，我们获得了黑人学生与匹配白人学生分数分布的出色匹配。我们发现，黑人学生的毕业成绩低于匹配的白人学生，但他们的毕业率、毕业后在军队的留任率以及早期晋升率相当。西班牙裔与白人的比较显示没有差异。男女比较显示，女性的毕业率和留任率较低。

When Coercive Economies Fail: The Political Economy of the US South After the Boll Weevil

当强制经济失败时：棉铃虫灾后美国南部的政治经济学

James J. Feigenbaum, Soumyajit Mazumder, Cory B. Smith

Abstract

How do coercive societies respond to negative economic shocks? We explore this question in the early 20th-Century United States South. Since before the nation's founding, cotton cultivation formed the politics and institutions in the South, including the development of slavery, the lack of democratic institutions, and intergroup relations between whites and blacks. We leverage the natural experiment generated by the boll weevil infestation from 1892-1922, which disrupted cotton production in the region. Panel difference-in-differences results provide evidence that Southern society became less violent and repressive in response to this shock with fewer lynchings and less Confederate monument construction. Cross-sectional results leveraging spatial variation in the infestation and historical cotton specialization show that affected counties had less KKK activity, higher non-white voter registration, and were less likely to experience contentious politics in the form of protests during the 1960s. To assess mechanisms, we show that the reductions in coercion were responses to African American out-migration. Even in a context of antidemocratic institutions, ordinary people can retain political power through the ability to ``vote with their feet.''

中文摘要

强制社会如何应对负面经济冲击？我们在20世纪初的美国南部探讨这个问题。自建国之前，棉花种植就塑造了南方的政治和制度，包括奴隶制的发展、民主制度的缺失以及白人与黑人之间的群体关系。我们利用了1892年至1922年棉铃虫灾害这一自然实验，该灾害破坏了该地区的棉花生产。面板双重差分结果提供了证据，表明南方社会在应对这一冲击时变得不那么暴力和压制，私刑减少，邦联纪念碑建设减少。利用灾害的空间变化和历史棉花专业化进行的横截面结果显示，受影响的县三K党活动较少，非白人选民登记率较高，并且在1960年代以抗议形式经历争议性政治的可能性较低。为了评估机制，我们表明强制行为的减少是对非裔美国人向外迁移的回应。即使在反民主制度的背景下，普通人仍然可以通过“用脚投票”的能力保留政治权力。

No. 132论文详情NBER w27160

Earnings Expectations in the COVID Crisis

新冠疫情危机中的盈利预期

Augustin Landier, David Thesmar

Abstract

We analyze firm-level analyst forecasts during the COVID crisis. First, we describe expectations dynamics about future corporate earnings. Downward revisions have been sharp, mostly focused on 2020, 2021 and 2022, but much less drastic than the lower bound estimated by Gormsen and Koijen (2020). Analyst forecasts do not exhibit evidence of over-reaction: As of mid-May, forecasts over 2020 earnings have progressively been reduced by 16%. Longer-run forecasts, as well as expected “Long-Term Growth” have reacted much less than short-run forecasts, and feature less disagreement. Second, we ask how much discount rate changes explain market dynamics, in an exercise similar to Shiller (1981). Given forecast revisions and price movements, we estimate an implicit discount rate going from 10% in mid-February, to 13% at the end of March, back down to their initial level in mid-May. We then decompose discount rate changes into three factors: changes in unlevered asset risk premium (0%), increased leverage (+1%) and interest rate reduction (-1%). Overall, analyst forecast revisions explain all of the decrease in equity values between January 2020 and mid May 2020, but they do not explain shorter term movements.

中文摘要

我们分析了新冠疫情危机期间的企业层面分析师预测。首先，我们描述了关于未来企业盈利的预期动态。向下修正幅度很大，主要集中在2020年、2021年和2022年，但远没有Gormsen和Koijen（2020）估计的下限那么剧烈。分析师预测没有表现出过度反应的证据：截至5月中旬，对2020年盈利的预测已逐步下调了16%。长期预测以及预期的“长期增长”的反应远小于短期预测，并且分歧较小。其次，我们询问在类似于Shiller（1981）的练习中，贴现率变化在多大程度上解释了市场动态。根据预测修正和价格变动，我们估计隐含贴现率从2月中旬的10%上升到3月底的13%，然后在5月中旬回落到初始水平。然后，我们将贴现率变化分解为三个因素：无杠杆资产风险溢价的变化（0%）、杠杆率增加（+1%）和利率降低（-1%）。总体而言，分析师预测修正解释了2020年1月至2020年5月中旬期间股权价值的所有下降，但它们无法解释短期波动。

No. 133论文详情NBER w27159

The U.S. Labor Market during the Beginning of the Pandemic Recession

疫情衰退初期的美国劳动力市场

Tomaz Cajner, Leland D. Crane, Ryan A. Decker, John Grigsby, Adrian Hamins-Puertolas, Erik Hurst, Christopher Kurz, Ahu Yildirmaz

Abstract

Using weekly administrative payroll data from the largest U.S. payroll processing company, we measure the evolution of the U.S. labor market during the first four months of the global COVID-19 pandemic. After aggregate employment fell by 21 percent through late-April, employment rebounded somewhat through late-June. The re-opening of temporarily shuttered businesses contributed significantly to the employment rebound, particularly for smaller businesses. We show that worker recall has been an important component of recent employment gains for both re-opening and continuing businesses. Employment losses have been concentrated disproportionately among lower wage workers; as of late June employment for workers in the lowest wage quintile was still 20 percent lower relative to mid-February levels. As a result, average base wages increased between February and June, though this increase arose entirely through a composition effect. Finally, we document that businesses have cut nominal wages for almost 7 million workers while forgoing regularly scheduled wage increases for many others.

中文摘要

利用来自美国最大薪资处理公司的每周行政薪资数据，我们衡量了全球新冠疫情前四个月美国劳动力市场的演变。在总就业人数在4月下旬下降21%之后，就业人数在6月下旬有所回升。暂时关闭企业的重新开业对就业反弹做出了显著贡献，尤其是对小型企业而言。我们表明，对于重新开业和持续经营的企业来说，工人召回一直是近期就业增长的重要组成部分。就业损失不成比例地集中在低工资工人中；截至6月下旬，最低工资五分位工人的就业水平仍比2月中旬水平低20%。因此，平均基本工资在2月至6月间有所上升，尽管这种上升完全是通过构成效应产生的。最后，我们记录了企业削减了近700万工人的名义工资，同时放弃了对许多其他工人定期加薪。

No. 134论文详情NBER w27158

Zombie Credit and (Dis-)Inflation: Evidence from Europe

僵尸信贷与（通缩）通胀：来自欧洲的证据

Viral V. Acharya, Matteo Crosignani, Tim Eisert, Christian Eufinger

Abstract

We show that cheap credit to impaired firms has a disinflationary effect. By helping distressed firms to stay afloat, “zombie credit” can create excess production capacity, and in turn, put downward pressure on markups and prices. We test this mechanism exploiting granular inflation and firm-level data from twelve European countries. In the cross-section of industries and countries, we find that a rise of zombie credit is associated with a decrease in firm defaults and entries, firm markups and product prices; lower productivity; and, an increase in aggregate sales as well as material and labor cost. These results hold at the firm-level, where we document spillover effects to healthy firms in markets with high zombie credit. Our partial equilibrium estimates suggest that without a rise in zombie credit post 2012, annual inflation in Europe during 2012-2016 would have been 0.45 percentage points higher.

中文摘要

我们表明，向受损企业提供廉价信贷具有通缩效应。通过帮助陷入困境的企业维持运营，“僵尸信贷”可以创造过剩的生产能力，进而对加价和价格产生下行压力。我们利用来自十二个欧洲国家的细粒度通胀和企业层面数据来检验这一机制。在行业和国家的横截面上，我们发现僵尸信贷的增加与以下因素相关：企业违约和进入减少、企业加价和产品价格下降、生产率降低；以及总销售额以及材料和劳动力成本增加。这些结果在企业层面成立，我们记录了在僵尸信贷高的市场中向健康企业的溢出效应。我们的局部均衡估计表明，如果2012年后僵尸信贷没有增加，2012-2016年期间欧洲的年通胀率将高出0.45个百分点。

No. 135论文详情NBER w27157

Poverty, Depression, and Anxiety: Causal Evidence and Mechanisms

贫困、抑郁与焦虑：因果证据与机制

Matthew W. Ridley, Gautam Rao, Frank Schilbach, Vikram H. Patel

Abstract

Why are people living in poverty disproportionately affected by mental illness? We review the interdisciplinary evidence of the bi-directional causal relationship between poverty and common mental illnesses – depression and anxiety – and the underlying mechanisms. Research shows that mental illness reduces employment and therefore income and that psychological interventions generate economic gains. Similarly, negative economic shocks cause mental illness, and anti-poverty programs, such as cash transfers, improve mental health. A crucial step toward the design of effective policies is to better understand the mechanisms underlying these causal effects.

中文摘要

为什么生活在贫困中的人不成比例地受到精神疾病的影响？我们回顾了贫困与常见精神疾病——抑郁和焦虑——之间双向因果关系的跨学科证据及其潜在机制。研究表明，精神疾病会减少就业，从而降低收入，而心理干预会产生经济收益。同样，负面经济冲击会导致精神疾病，而反贫困计划（如现金转移）可以改善心理健康。设计有效政策的关键一步是更好地理解这些因果效应背后的机制。

No. 136论文详情NBER w27156

The Winners and Losers of Immigration: Evidence from Linked Historical Data

移民的赢家与输家：来自关联历史数据的证据

Joseph Price, Christian vom Lehn, Riley Wilson

Abstract

Using recent innovations in linking historical U.S. Census data, we study the economic impacts of immigration on natives, including their geographic migration response. We find that the arrival of foreign immigrants significantly increases both native out-migration and in-migration. Accounting for this selective geographic migration, we find smaller economic impacts of immigration for native workers than previous work, including no positive impact on worker incomes. We present evidence of significant “losers” from increased immigration, namely workers who appear to be displaced by immigrant labor and move out of their local labor market, whereas the workers who remain see significant benefits. We also find that younger and lowerskilled workers are “losers” from increased immigration, whereas older and higher-skilled workers are “winners.”

中文摘要

利用关联历史美国人口普查数据的最新创新，我们研究了移民对本地人的经济影响，包括他们的地理迁移反应。我们发现，外国移民的到来显著增加了本地人的向外迁移和向内迁移。考虑到这种选择性的地理迁移，我们发现移民对本地工人的经济影响比以往研究更小，包括对工人收入没有积极影响。我们提供了证据表明，移民增加存在显著的“输家”，即那些似乎被移民劳动力取代并迁出本地劳动力市场的工人，而留下的工人则看到了显著的好处。我们还发现，年轻和低技能工人是移民增加的“输家”，而年长和高技能工人是“赢家”。

No. 137论文详情NBER w27155

Prospect Theory and Stock Market Anomalies

前景理论与股市异象

Nicholas C. Barberis, Lawrence J. Jin, Baolian Wang

Abstract

We present a new model of asset prices in which investors evaluate risk according to prospect theory and examine its ability to explain 23 prominent stock market anomalies. The model incorporates all the elements of prospect theory, takes account of investors’ prior gains and losses, and makes quantitative predictions about an asset’s average return based on empirical estimates of its volatility, skewness, and past capital gain. We ﬁnd that the model is helpful for thinking about a majority of the 23 anomalies.

中文摘要

我们提出了一个新的资产价格模型，在该模型中，投资者根据前景理论评估风险，并检验了该模型解释23个著名股市异象的能力。该模型包含了前景理论的所有要素，考虑了投资者先前的收益和损失，并根据对资产波动性、偏度和过去资本收益的实证估计，对资产的平均回报做出了定量预测。我们发现，该模型有助于理解这23个异象中的大多数。

The Gender Gap in Tech & Competitive Work Environments? Field Experimental Evidence from an Internet-of-Things Product Development Platform

科技与竞争性工作环境中的性别差距？来自物联网产品开发平台的实地实验证据

Kevin Boudreau, Nilam Kaushik

Abstract

Many technology companies struggle to fill all their positions and to achieve gender parity in their ranks. One explanation for gender disparities is the possibility that men and women differ in their willingness to work under competitive organizational environments of tech firms. To investigate this question, this paper reports on a large platform-based field experiment in which 97,696 U.S. university-educated individuals were given the opportunity to join a tech-related product development activity. Individuals were randomly assigned to treatments emphasizing either competitive or collaborative interactions with other participants. We find that (1) in non-STEM fields, the competition treatment leads to a 27% drop in participation for females in comparison to males. However, in our main finding, (2) in STEM fields, we find no statistical differences in men and women’s responses to competition. The patterns are consistent with (3) men in non-STEM fields exhibiting overconfidence in their likelihood of succeeding under competition. We also find that, while participation in highest in STEM fields, (4) the ratio of female to male participation in a field is better predicted by whether the field is male- or female-dominated, than it is by whether it is a STEM field or not. We discuss theoretical interpretations and implications for organizations.

中文摘要

许多科技公司难以填补所有职位空缺，并难以在其员工队伍中实现性别平等。性别差异的一种解释是，男性和女性在科技公司竞争性组织环境下工作的意愿可能存在差异。为了研究这个问题，本文报告了一项基于大型平台的实地实验，其中97,696名受过大学教育的美国人有机会参加一项与科技相关的产品开发活动。个体被随机分配到强调与其他参与者竞争或协作互动的处理组。我们发现：（1）在非STEM领域，与男性相比，竞争处理导致女性参与率下降27%。然而，在我们的主要发现中，（2）在STEM领域，我们发现男性和女性对竞争的反应没有统计上的差异。这些模式与（3）非STEM领域的男性在竞争中对成功可能性表现出过度自信是一致的。我们还发现，虽然STEM领域的参与率最高，但（4）一个领域的女性与男性参与比例，更能由该领域是男性主导还是女性主导来预测，而不是由它是否是STEM领域来预测。我们讨论了理论解释及其对组织的启示。

No. 139论文详情NBER w27153

Leader Value Added: Assessing the Growth Contribution of Individual National Leaders

领导者的增加值：评估国家领导人的个体增长贡献

William Easterly, Steven Pennings

Abstract

Previous literature suggests that leaders matter for growth in general. This paper asks which leaders matter and develops a methodology to estimate the growth contribution of individual leaders and calculate its precision. The findings show that few leaders have statistically significant contributions; it is difficult to know who is good for growth and who is not. The paper also finds that the most intuitive estimate of a leader’s contribution—the average growth rate during tenure—is largely useless for measuring his or her true contribution. Consequently, many leaders with statistically significant growth effects are surprises. Moreover, leaders in non-democratic countries are no more likely to be statistically significant than leaders in democratic ones.

中文摘要

以往的文献表明，领导者总体上对增长很重要。本文探讨哪些领导者重要，并开发了一种方法来估计个体领导者的增长贡献并计算其精确度。研究结果表明，很少有领导者具有统计上显著的贡献；很难知道谁对增长有利，谁不利。本文还发现，对领导者贡献最直观的估计——任期内的平均增长率——在很大程度上无法衡量其真实贡献。因此，许多具有统计上显著增长效应的领导者是令人意外的。此外，非民主国家的领导者并不比民主国家的领导者更可能具有统计显著性。

No. 140论文详情NBER w27152

Supply and Demand in Disaggregated Keynesian Economies with an Application to the Covid-19 Crisis

分解的凯恩斯主义经济中的供给与需求——兼论新冠疫情危机中的应用

David Baqaee, Emmanuel Farhi

Abstract

We study supply and demand shocks in a disaggregated model with multiple sectors, multiple factors, input-output linkages, downward nominal wage rigidities, credit-constraints, and a zero lower bound. We use the model to understand how the Covid-19 crisis, an omnibus supply and demand shock, affects output, unemployment, and inflation, and leads to the coexistence of tight and slack labor markets. We show that negative sectoral supply shocks are stagflationary, whereas negative demand shocks are deflationary, even though both can cause Keynesian unemployment. Furthermore, complementarities in production amplify Keynesian spillovers from supply shocks but mitigate them for demand shocks. This means that complementarities reduce the effectiveness of aggregate demand stimulus. In a stylized quantitative model of the US, we find supply and demand shocks each explain about half the reduction in real GDP from February to May, 2020. Although there was as much as 7% Keynesian unemployment, this was concentrated in certain markets. Hence, aggregate demand stimulus is one quarter as effective as in a typical recession where all labor markets are slack.

中文摘要

我们研究了一个分解模型中的供给和需求冲击，该模型包含多个部门、多种要素、投入产出关联、向下名义工资刚性、信贷约束和零下限。我们使用该模型来理解新冠疫情危机——一种综合性的供给和需求冲击——如何影响产出、失业和通胀，并导致紧张和松弛的劳动力市场并存。我们表明，负面的部门供给冲击是滞胀性的，而负面的需求冲击是通缩性的，尽管两者都可能导致凯恩斯式失业。此外，生产中的互补性放大了供给冲击的凯恩斯式溢出效应，但缓解了需求冲击的溢出效应。这意味着互补性降低了总需求刺激的有效性。在一个针对美国的简约定量模型中，我们发现供给和需求冲击各解释了2020年2月至5月实际GDP减少量的大约一半。尽管存在高达7%的凯恩斯式失业，但这集中在某些市场。因此，总需求刺激的效果仅为所有劳动力市场都松弛的典型衰退时期的四分之一。

Machine Learning in Gravity Models: An Application to Agricultural Trade

引力模型中的机器学习：在农产品贸易中的应用

Munisamy Gopinath, Feras A. Batarseh, Jayson Beckman

Abstract

Predicting agricultural trade patterns is critical to decision making in the public and private domains, especially in the current context of trade disputes among major economies. Focusing on seven major agricultural commodities with a long history of trade, this study employed data-driven and deep-learning processes: supervised and unsupervised machine learning (ML) techniques – to decipher patterns of trade. The supervised (unsupervised) ML techniques were trained on data until 2010 (2014), and projections were made for 2011-2016 (2014-2020). Results show the high relevance of ML models to predicting trade patterns in near- and long-term relative to traditional approaches, which are often subjective assessments or time-series projections. While supervised ML techniques quantified key economic factors underlying agricultural trade flows, unsupervised approaches provide better fits over the long-term.

How Resilient is Venture-Backed Innovation? Evidence from Four Decades of U.S. Patenting

风险投资支持的创新有多强的韧性？来自美国四十年专利数据的证据

Sabrina T. Howell, Josh Lerner, Ramana Nanda, Richard R. Townsend

Abstract

Despite theoretical predictions to the contrary, corporate innovation is strongly pro-cyclical. In this paper, we compare innovation in the economy as a whole to that of firms backed by venture capital (VC), a source of capital associated with the most impactful young firms. We show that (1) patents filed by VC-backed firms are of significantly higher quality and economic importance than those in the broader economy, (2) venture-backed innovation is even more procyclical than innovation in general, and (3) that the deterioration of venture innovation in downturns appears driven by shifts in the types of startups that these investors finance. Our findings suggest that during recessions, venture capitalists perceive a need to conserve capital both due to demand for financing from struggling companies already in their portfolios and due to a more challenging fundraising environment. Therefore, they shift funding to less innovative firms that are closer to profitability. Rather than countering the pro-cyclicality of innovation in the broader economy, VC finance appears instead to amplify this pattern.

中文摘要

尽管有相反的理论预测，企业创新具有强烈的顺周期性。在本文中，我们将整体经济中的创新与风险投资支持的企业（一种与最具影响力的年轻企业相关的资本来源）的创新进行了比较。我们表明：（1）风险投资支持企业申请的专利在质量和经济重要性上显著高于更广泛经济中的专利；（2）风险投资支持的创新比一般创新更具顺周期性；（3）经济衰退期间风险创新质量的下降似乎是由这些投资者所资助的初创企业类型的变化驱动的。我们的研究结果表明，在经济衰退期间，风险投资家认为需要节约资本，这既是因为其投资组合中陷入困境的公司有融资需求，也是因为融资环境更具挑战性。因此，他们将资金转向更接近盈利、创新性较低的企业。风险投资非但没有抵消更广泛经济中创新的顺周期性，反而似乎放大了这种模式。

Systemic Credit Freezes in Financial Lending Networks

金融借贷网络中的系统性信贷冻结

Daron Acemoglu, Asuman Ozdaglar, James Siderius, Alireza Tahbaz-Salehi

Abstract

This paper develops a network model of interbank lending, in which banks decide to extend credit to their potential borrowers. Borrowers are subject to shocks that may force them to default on their loans. In contrast to much of the previous literature on financial networks, we focus on how anticipation of future defaults may result in ex ante “credit freezes,” whereby banks refuse to extend credit to one another. We first characterize the terms of the interbank contracts and the patterns of interbank lending that emerge in equilibrium. We then study how shifts in the distribution of shocks can result in complex credit freezes that travel throughout the network. We use this framework to analyze the effects of various policy interventions on systemic credit freezes.

中文摘要

本文构建了一个银行间借贷的网络模型，其中银行决定是否向其潜在借款人提供信贷。借款人可能遭受冲击，迫使其贷款违约。与以往许多关于金融网络的文献不同，我们关注的是对未来违约的预期如何可能导致事前的“信贷冻结”，即银行拒绝相互提供信贷。我们首先刻画了均衡中出现的银行间合约条款和银行间借贷模式。然后，我们研究了冲击分布的变化如何导致复杂的信贷冻结，并在整个网络中传播。我们利用这一框架分析了各种政策干预对系统性信贷冻结的影响。

No. 144论文详情NBER w27148

Trade in Technology: A Potential Solution to the Food Security Challenges of the 21st Century

技术贸易：解决21世纪粮食安全挑战的潜在方案

Thomas W. Hertel, Uris L.C. Baldos, Keith O. Fuglie

Abstract

The recent rise in caloric undernutrition in Sub-Saharan Africa (SSA) demonstrates the continued relevance of the Malthusian footrace between food availability and population. Sluggish growth in farm productivity in SSA has brought to the fore the key role of agricultural technology in alleviating future food insecurity. We develop a model of technology, food security and international trade with three distinct channels for technology reduce food insecurity in SSA. The first is via greater domestic R&D investment. An alternative is to import technologies from other countries with significant knowledge capital. The third role for technology to resolve the Malthusian dilemma in SSA is that of ‘virtual technology trade’, i.e., importing technological investments undertaken elsewhere through cheaper imported food. To assess the relative contribution of each channel to food security in Africa, we employ a partial equilibrium, quantitative trade model, augmented by a temporal relationship between R&D investments, knowledge capital and agricultural productivity. Over the historical period: 1991-2011 we find that direct R&D investments in SSA have been the dominant vehicle for lowering food prices in Africa. Looking forward to 2050, we find that virtual technology trade will be the most important vehicle for reducing non-farm undernutrition in Africa.

中文摘要

撒哈拉以南非洲地区近期热量摄入不足问题的加剧，表明马尔萨斯关于食物供给与人口增长之间的竞赛仍然具有现实意义。撒哈拉以南非洲地区农业生产力增长缓慢，凸显了农业技术在缓解未来粮食不安全中的关键作用。我们构建了一个包含技术、粮食安全和国际贸易的模型，其中技术通过三种不同渠道减少撒哈拉以南非洲地区的粮食不安全。第一种是通过增加国内研发投资。另一种是从拥有大量知识资本的其他国家进口技术。技术解决撒哈拉以南非洲地区马尔萨斯困境的第三种角色是“虚拟技术贸易”，即通过进口更便宜的食物来进口其他地方进行的技术投资。为了评估每种渠道对非洲粮食安全的相对贡献，我们采用了一个部分均衡的定量贸易模型，并加入了研发投资、知识资本和农业生产力之间的时间关系。在历史时期（1991-2011年），我们发现撒哈拉以南非洲地区的直接研发投资是降低非洲粮食价格的主要途径。展望2050年，我们发现虚拟技术贸易将成为减少非洲非农业人口营养不足的最重要途径。

No. 145论文详情NBER w27147

The Impact of Retaliatory Tariffs on Agricultural and Food Trade

报复性关税对农产品和食品贸易的影响

Colin A. Carter, Sandro Steinbach

Abstract

This paper analyzes the short-run trade effects of retaliatory tariffs against agriculture and food exports from the United States. The results indicate that these tariffs caused a substantial decline in U.S. agriculture and food exports and induced a reorientation of international trade patterns. We find that losses in foreign trade with retaliatory countries outweigh the gains from trade with non-retaliatory countries by more than USD 14.4 billion. Our results also indicate that non-retaliatory countries accommodated the increased demand from retaliatory countries by reorienting their trade relationships. We find that countries in South America and Europe benefited the most from these adjustments gaining more than USD 13.5 billion in additional foreign sales. The effects of retaliatory tariff increases across products vary substantially, with soybeans and meat products experiencing the most considerable redistribution effects.

中文摘要

本文分析了针对美国农产品和食品出口的报复性关税在短期内的贸易效应。结果表明，这些关税导致美国农产品和食品出口大幅下降，并引发了国际贸易格局的重新调整。我们发现，与报复性国家的对外贸易损失超过了与非报复性国家贸易带来的收益，差额超过144亿美元。我们的结果还表明，非报复性国家通过重新调整其贸易关系来满足报复性国家增加的需求。我们发现，南美和欧洲的国家从这些调整中获益最多，获得了超过135亿美元的额外海外销售额。报复性关税上调对不同产品的影响差异很大，其中大豆和肉类产品经历了最显著的重新分配效应。

No. 146论文详情NBER w27146

Kill Zone

杀伐地带

Sai Krishna Kamepalli, Raghuram Rajan, Luigi Zingales

Abstract

Venture capitalists suggest that incumbent internet platforms create a kill zone around themselves, where any competing entrant is acquired quickly. Consequently, financing new startups becomes unprofitable. We construct a simple model that rationalizes the existence of a kill zone. The price at which an acquisition is done depends on the number of customers the entrant platform can attract if it remains independent, which in turn depends on the number of apps that have adapted to the platform. The prospect of a quick acquisition by the incumbent platform, however, reduces the app designers’ benefits from adaptation, making it harder for a technological superior entrant to acquire customers. This reduces the stand-alone price of the new entrant, decreasing the price at which they will be acquired, and thus reducing the incentives of VCs to finance their entry. We discuss the policy implications of this model.

中文摘要

风险投资家认为，现有互联网平台会在自身周围创造一个“杀伐地带”，任何竞争性进入者都会被迅速收购。因此，为新创企业融资变得无利可图。我们构建了一个简单的模型，使“杀伐地带”的存在合理化。收购价格取决于进入平台若保持独立所能吸引的客户数量，而这又取决于已适配该平台的应用数量。然而，被现有平台快速收购的前景降低了应用设计者从适配中获得的收益，使得技术更优的进入者更难获取客户。这降低了新进入者的独立估值，从而压低了其被收购的价格，进而削弱了风险投资为其进入提供资金的激励。我们讨论了该模型的政策含义。

No. 147论文详情NBER w27145

Innovation and Entrepreneurship in the Energy Sector

能源领域的创新与创业

David Popp, Jacquelyn Pless, Ivan Haščič, Nick Johnstone

Abstract

Historically, innovation in the energy sector proceeded slowly and entrepreneurial start-up firms played a relatively minor role. We argue that this may be changing. Energy markets are going through a period of profound structural change. The rise of hydrofracturing lowered fossil fuel prices so much that natural gas is now the primary fuel for electricity generation in the US. Renewable energy technologies also experienced significant cost and performance improvements. However, integrating intermittent resources creates additional grid management challenges, requiring further innovation. This chapter documents the evolving roles of innovation and entrepreneurship in the energy sector. First, we provide an overview of the energy industry, highlighting that many new energy technologies are smaller, modular, and increasingly rely on innovation in other fast-moving high-tech sectors. We then conduct two descriptive data analyses that document a sharp decline in both clean energy patenting and start-up activity from about 2010 onwards. We discuss potential explanations and provide some evidence that while innovation in existing technologies may simply have been successful, continued innovation will be needed in enabling technologies that are more likely to depend on progress in other sectors.

中文摘要

历史上，能源领域的创新进展缓慢，创业型初创企业扮演的角色相对次要。我们认为这种情况可能正在改变。能源市场正经历一场深刻的结构性变革。水力压裂技术的兴起大幅降低了化石燃料价格，以至于天然气现已成为美国发电的主要燃料。可再生能源技术也经历了显著的成本降低和性能提升。然而，整合间歇性资源带来了额外的电网管理挑战，需要进一步的创新。本章记录了能源领域创新与创业角色的演变。首先，我们概述了能源行业，强调许多新能源技术更小型化、模块化，并且日益依赖于其他快速发展的高科技领域的创新。随后，我们进行了两项描述性数据分析，记录了从2010年左右开始，清洁能源专利活动和初创企业活动均急剧下降。我们讨论了潜在的解释，并提供了一些证据表明，虽然现有技术的创新可能只是取得了成功，但在使能技术方面仍需持续创新，而这些技术更可能依赖于其他领域的进步。

No. 148论文详情NBER w27144

Measuring Real Consumption and CPI Bias under Lockdown Conditions

封锁条件下衡量实际消费与CPI偏差

W. Erwin Diewert, Kevin J. Fox

Abstract

Millions of goods and services are now unavailable in many countries due to the current coronavirus pandemic, dramatically impacting on the construction of key economic statistics used for informing policy. This situation is unprecedented; hence methods to address it have not previously been developed. Current advice to national statistical offices from the IMF, Eurostat and the UN is shown to result in downward bias in the CPI and upward bias in real consumption. We conclude that the only way to produce a meaningful CPI within the lockdown period is through establishing a continuous consumer expenditure survey.

中文摘要

由于当前的新冠疫情，许多国家数以百万计的商品和服务现已无法获得，这极大地影响了用于制定政策的关键经济统计数据的编制。这种情况是前所未有的，因此此前尚未开发出应对方法。本文表明，目前国际货币基金组织、欧盟统计局和联合国向各国统计机构提供的建议会导致消费者价格指数（CPI）出现向下偏差，而实际消费出现向上偏差。我们得出结论，在封锁期内编制有意义的CPI的唯一方法是建立持续的消费者支出调查。
