Paying It Backward and Forward: Expanding Access to Convalescent Plasma Therapy Through Market Design

向后支付与向前支付：通过市场设计扩大恢复期血浆疗法的可及性

Scott Duke Kominers, Parag A. Pathak, Tayfun Sönmez, M. Utku Ünver

Abstract

COVID-19 convalescent plasma (CCP) therapy is currently a leading treatment for COVID-19. At present, there is a shortage of CCP relative to demand. We develop and analyze a model of centralized CCP allocation that incorporates both donation and distribution. In order to increase CCP supply, we introduce a mechanism that utilizes two incentive schemes, respectively based on principles of “paying it backward” and “paying it forward.” Under the first scheme, CCP donors obtain treatment vouchers that can be transferred to patients of their choosing. Under the latter scheme, patients obtain priority for CCP therapy in exchange for a future pledge to donate CCP if possible. We show that in steady-state, both principles generally increase overall treatment rates for all patients—not just those who are voucher-prioritized or pledged to donate. Our results also hold under certain conditions if a fraction of CCP is reserved for patients who participate in clinical trials. Finally, we examine the implications of pooling blood types on the efficiency and equity of CCP distribution.

中文摘要

COVID-19恢复期血浆疗法是目前治疗COVID-19的主要方法之一。目前，恢复期血浆相对于需求存在短缺。我们开发并分析了一个集中化恢复期血浆分配的模型，该模型同时考虑了捐赠和分配。为了增加恢复期血浆的供应，我们引入了一种机制，该机制利用两种激励方案，分别基于“向后支付”和“向前支付”原则。在第一种方案下，恢复期血浆捐赠者获得治疗凭证，这些凭证可以转让给他们选择的患者。在后一种方案下，患者通过承诺未来在可能的情况下捐赠恢复期血浆，来获得恢复期血浆治疗的优先权。我们表明，在稳态下，这两种原则通常都会提高所有患者的总体治疗率——而不仅仅是那些拥有凭证优先权或承诺捐赠的患者。如果一部分恢复期血浆被预留给参与临床试验的患者，我们的结果在特定条件下仍然成立。最后，我们研究了混合血型对恢复期血浆分配效率和公平性的影响。

No. 150论文详情NBER w27142

The Use of Group-Level Approaches to Environmental and Natural Resource Policy

环境与自然资源政策中群体层面方法的应用

Matthew Kotchen, Kathleen Segerson

Abstract

Policies to address environmental and natural resource management are often implemented at the group level. The defining feature of such policies is that penalties or rewards are based on group rather than individual performance, or rights are allocated to a group rather than to individuals. This article discusses how group-level policies have been applied and studied across a variety of contexts in the literature on environmental and natural resource management. The aim is to identify common theoretical and empirical insights and lessons learned about the design and implementation of these instruments. A general finding is that group-level policies are most likely to be effective when rewards and/or penalties are designed to provide strong incentives for groups to meet targets in a cost-effective way. Moreover, to the extent that this requires coordination within the group, the effectiveness of policies will depend on whether the group has or can create its own institutions or mechanisms to facilitate and enforce that coordination.

中文摘要

解决环境和自然资源管理问题的政策通常是在群体层面实施的。这类政策的定义性特征是，惩罚或奖励基于群体而非个人表现，或者权利被分配给群体而非个人。本文讨论了群体层面政策如何在环境和自然资源管理文献中的各种背景下被应用和研究。目的是识别关于这些工具设计和实施的共同理论和实证见解及经验教训。一个总体发现是，当奖励和/或惩罚旨在为群体以成本有效的方式实现目标提供强有力的激励时，群体层面政策最有可能有效。此外，就这需要群体内部协调而言，政策的有效性将取决于该群体是否拥有或能够创建自己的机构或机制来促进和执行这种协调。

No. 151论文详情NBER w27141

The Cost of the Covid-19 Crisis: Lockdowns, Macroeconomic Expectations, and Consumer Spending

新冠疫情危机的代价：封锁、宏观经济预期与消费者支出

Olivier Coibion, Yuriy Gorodnichenko, Michael Weber

Abstract

We study how the differential timing of local lockdowns due to COVID-19 causally affects households’ spending and macroeconomic expectations at the local level using several waves of a customized survey with more than 10,000 respondents. About 50% of survey participants report income and wealth losses due to the corona virus, with the average losses being $\$5,293$ and $\$33,482$ respectively. Aggregate consumer spending dropped by 31 log percentage points with the largest drops in travel and clothing. We find that households living in counties that went into lockdown earlier expect the unemployment rate over the next twelve months to be 13 percentage points higher and continue to expect higher unemployment at horizons of three to five years. They also expect lower future inflation, report higher uncertainty, expect lower mortgage rates for up to 10 years, and have moved out of foreign stocks into liquid forms of savings. The imposition of lockdowns can account for much of the decline in employment in recent months as well as declines in consumer spending. While lockdowns have pronounced effects on local economic conditions and households’ expectations, they have little impact on approval ratings of Congress, the Fed, or the Treasury but lead to declines in the approval of the President.

中文摘要

我们利用一项包含超过10,000名受访者的多轮定制调查，研究了因新冠疫情导致的各地封锁时间差异如何因果性地影响地方层面的家庭支出和宏观经济预期。约50%的调查参与者报告因新冠病毒遭受了收入和财富损失，平均损失分别为5,293美元和33,482美元。总消费者支出下降了31个对数百分点，其中旅行和服装支出降幅最大。我们发现，居住在较早进入封锁状态的县的家庭，预计未来十二个月的失业率会高出13个百分点，并且在三到五年的更长时期内仍预期失业率更高。他们还预期未来通胀率更低，报告了更高的不确定性，预期未来长达十年的抵押贷款利率更低，并且已将资金从外国股票转向流动性储蓄形式。封锁的实施可以解释近几个月就业以及消费者支出的大部分下降。虽然封锁对地方经济状况和家庭预期有显著影响，但对国会、美联储或财政部的支持率影响甚微，但会导致总统支持率下降。

No. 152论文详情NBER w27140

Entry vs. Rents: Aggregation with Economies of Scale

进入与租金：具有规模经济的加总

David Baqaee, Emmanuel Farhi

Abstract

We characterize the response of aggregate output to micro shocks in disaggregated economies with entry, non-constant returns to scale, input-output linkages, and distortions. We decompose output changes into technical and allocative eﬃciency components, and show that the latter depends on changes in rents and quasi-rents across markets. We use this to characterize the social costs of distortions and show the importance of accounting for entry both qualitatively and quantitatively. As an example, we show that the eﬃciency losses caused by markups in the US rise from around 20% of GDP to around 40% once we account for the entry margin. Our base-line is sensitive not only to the presence of entry, but also to the specifics of how entry is modeled, in ways that our social-costs-of-distortions formulas clarify. Entry can substantively alter the economy’s response to shocks even if variable profits and fixed costs are small as a share of GDP.

中文摘要

我们刻画了在存在进入、非恒定规模报酬、投入产出关联和扭曲的分散化经济中，总产出对微观冲击的响应。我们将产出变化分解为技术效率和配置效率组成部分，并表明后者取决于跨市场的租金和准租金变化。我们利用这一点来刻画扭曲的社会成本，并表明在定性和定量上考虑进入因素的重要性。例如，我们表明，一旦我们考虑进入边际，美国由加价造成的效率损失从约占GDP的20%上升到约40%。我们的基准结果不仅对是否存在进入敏感，而且对进入建模的具体方式也敏感，我们的社会成本扭曲公式阐明了这一点。即使可变利润和固定成本占GDP的份额很小，进入也能实质性地改变经济对冲击的响应。

No. 153论文详情NBER w27139

The Darwinian Returns to Scale

达尔文式的规模回报

David Baqaee, Emmanuel Farhi, Kunal Sangani

Abstract

How does an increase in market size, say due to globalization, affect welfare? We study this question using a model with monopolistic competition, heterogeneous markups, and fixed costs. We characterize changes in welfare and decompose changes in allocative efficiency into three different effects: (1) reallocations across firms with heterogeneous price elasticities due to intensifying competition, (2) reallocations due to the exit of marginally profitable firms, and (3) reallocations due to changes in firms’ markups. Whereas the second and third effects have ambiguous implications for welfare, the first effect, which we call the Darwinian effect, always increases welfare regardless of the shape of demand curves. We non-parametrically calibrate demand curves with data from Belgian manufacturing firms and quantify our results. We find that mild increasing returns at the micro level can catalyze large increasing returns at the macro level. Between 70–90% of increasing returns to scale come from improvements in how a larger market allocates resources. The lion’s share of these gains are due to the Darwinian effect, which increases the aggregate markup and concentrates sales and employment in high-markup firms. This has implications for policy: an entry subsidy, which harnesses Darwinian reallocations, can improve welfare even when there is more entry than in the first-best.

中文摘要

市场规模的扩大（例如由全球化引起）如何影响福利？我们使用一个包含垄断竞争、异质性加成和固定成本的模型来研究这一问题。我们刻画了福利的变化，并将配置效率的变化分解为三种不同的效应：（1）由于竞争加剧，在具有不同价格弹性的企业之间进行的重新配置；（2）由于边际利润企业退出而导致的重新配置；（3）由于企业加成变化而导致的重新配置。第二和第三种效应对福利的影响是模糊的，而第一种效应（我们称之为达尔文效应）无论需求曲线的形状如何，总是能提高福利。我们利用比利时制造业企业的数据，以非参数方式校准了需求曲线，并量化了我们的结果。我们发现，微观层面温和的规模报酬递增可以催化宏观层面巨大的规模报酬递增。规模报酬递增的70%至90%来自于更大市场如何改善资源配置。这些收益的绝大部分归因于达尔文效应，该效应提高了总体加成，并将销售和就业集中在高加成企业。这对政策有启示：即使存在比最优状态更多的进入，利用达尔文式重新配置的进入补贴也能改善福利。

No. 154论文详情NBER w27138

Paid sick-leave and physical mobility: Evidence from the United States during a pandemic

带薪病假与身体流动性：来自美国大流行期间的证据

Martin Andersen, Johanna Catherine Maclean, Michael F. Pesko, Kosali I. Simon

Abstract

We study the effects of a massive temporary U.S. paid sick leave (PSL) mandate that became effective April 1st, 2020 on self-quarantining, proxied by physical mobility behaviors gleaned from cellular devices. Such behaviors are critical for containment of infectious diseases. The national PSL policy was implemented in response to the COVID-19 global pandemic and mandated two weeks of fully compensated paid leave. We study the impact of this policy using difference-in-differences methods, leveraging pre-policy county-level differences in the share of ‘nonessential’ workers likely eligible for paid sick leave benefits. We find robust evidence that the policy increased the average number of hours at home and reduced the share of the individuals likely at work. Comparing the county with the lowest to highest policy exposure, we find that the average hours per day not at home, and at work decreased by 8.9% and 6.9% post-policy.

中文摘要

我们研究了美国一项大规模临时带薪病假（PSL）强制令（于2020年4月1日生效）对自我隔离的影响，以从蜂窝设备获取的身体流动性行为作为代理指标。这种行为对于传染病的控制至关重要。这项全国性的带薪病假政策是为了应对COVID-19全球大流行而实施的，规定了两周的全薪带薪休假。我们使用双重差分方法研究该政策的影响，利用政策实施前县级层面可能符合带薪病假福利资格的“非必要”工人比例的差异。我们发现强有力的证据表明，该政策增加了平均居家小时数，并减少了可能在工作中的个体比例。比较政策暴露程度最低和最高的县，我们发现政策实施后，平均每天不在家和工作的小时数分别下降了8.9%和6.9%。

No. 155论文详情NBER w27137

COVID-19 Is Also a Reallocation Shock

COVID-19也是一次重新配置冲击

Jose Maria Barrero, Nicholas Bloom, Steven J. Davis

Abstract

Drawing on firm-level expectations at a one-year forecast horizon in the Survey of Business Uncertainty (SBU), we construct novel, forward-looking reallocation measures for jobs and sales. These measures rise sharply after February 2020, reaching rates in April that are 2.4 (3.9) times the pre-COVID average for jobs (sales). We also draw on special questions in the April SBU to quantify the near-term impact of the COVID-19 shock on business staffing. We find 3 new hires for every 10 layoffs caused by the shock and estimate that 42 percent of recent layoffs will result in permanent job loss. Our survey evidence aligns well with anecdotal evidence of large pandemic-induced demand increases at some firms, with contemporaneous evidence on gross business formation, and with a sharp pandemic-induced rise in equity return dispersion across firms. After developing the evidence, we consider implications of our evidence for the economic outlook and for policy responses to the pandemic. Unemployment benefit levels that exceed worker earnings, policies that subsidize employee retention, occupational licensing restrictions, and regulatory barriers to business formation will impede reallocation responses to the COVID-19 shock.

中文摘要

利用商业不确定性调查（SBU）中一年预测期内的企业层面预期，我们构建了关于就业和销售的新型前瞻性重新配置指标。这些指标在2020年2月后急剧上升，到4月份，就业和销售的重新配置率分别达到COVID-19前平均水平的2.4倍和3.9倍。我们还利用4月份SBU中的特殊问题来量化COVID-19冲击对商业人员配置的近期影响。我们发现，冲击导致的每10次裁员对应3次新招聘，并估计42%的近期裁员将导致永久性失业。我们的调查证据与关于大流行导致某些企业需求大幅增加的轶事证据、关于企业成立总量的同期证据以及大流行导致的企业间股票收益离散度急剧上升的证据高度吻合。在提出证据后，我们考虑了这些证据对经济前景和政策应对大流行的启示。超过工人收入的失业救济金水平、补贴员工留任的政策、职业许可限制以及企业成立的监管障碍，都将阻碍对COVID-19冲击的重新配置反应。

No. 156论文详情NBER w27136

What Keeps Stablecoins Stable?

是什么让稳定币保持稳定？

Richard K. Lyons, Ganesh Viswanath-Natraj

Abstract

We take this question to be isomorphic to, "What Keeps Fixed Exchange Rates Fixed?" and address it with analysis familiar in exchange-rate economics. Stablecoins solve the volatility problem by pegging to a national currency, typically the US dollar, and are used as vehicles for exchanging national currencies into non-stable cryptocurrencies, with some stablecoins having a ratio of trading volume to outstanding supply exceeding one daily. Using a rich dataset of signed trades and order books on multiple exchanges, we examine how peg-sustaining arbitrage stabilizes the price of the largest stablecoin, Tether. We find that stablecoin issuance, the closest analogue to central-bank intervention, plays only a limited role in stabilization, pointing instead to stabilizing forces on the demand side. Following Tether's introduction to the Ethereum blockchain in 2019, we find increased investor access to arbitrage trades, and a decline in arbitrage spreads from 70 to 30 basis points. We also pin down which fundamentals drive the two-sided distribution of peg-price deviations: Premiums are due to stablecoins' role as a safe haven, exhibiting, for example, premiums greater than 100 basis points during the COVID-19 crisis of March 2020; discounts derive from liquidity effects and collateral concerns.

中文摘要

我们认为这个问题与“是什么让固定汇率保持固定？”是同构的，并用汇率经济学中熟悉的分析来回答它。稳定币通过锚定一种国家货币（通常是美元）来解决波动性问题，并被用作将国家货币兑换成非稳定加密货币的工具，一些稳定币的交易量与流通供应量之比每天超过1。利用多个交易所的已签署交易和订单簿的丰富数据集，我们研究了维持锚定的套利如何稳定最大稳定币Tether的价格。我们发现，稳定币发行（最接近央行干预的类比）在稳定中只起有限作用，反而指出了需求侧的稳定力量。在2019年Tether引入以太坊区块链后，我们发现投资者进行套利交易的机会增加，套利价差从70个基点下降到30个基点。我们还确定了哪些基本面因素驱动了锚定价格偏差的双侧分布：溢价源于稳定币作为避险资产的作用，例如在2020年3月的COVID-19危机期间溢价超过100个基点；折价则源于流动性效应和抵押品担忧。

No. 157论文详情NBER w27135

Expected Health Effects of Reduced Air Pollution from COVID-19 Social Distancing

COVID-19社交距离措施减少空气污染的预期健康影响

Steve Cicala, Stephen P. Holland, Erin T. Mansur, Nicholas Z. Muller, Andrew J. Yates

Abstract

The COVID-19 pandemic resulted in stay-at-home policies and other social distancing behaviors in the United States in spring of 2020. This paper examines the impact that these actions had on emissions and expected health effects through reduced personal vehicle travel and electricity consumption. Using daily cell phone mobility data for each U.S. county, we find that vehicle travel dropped about 40% by mid-April across the nation. States that imposed stay-at-home policies before March 28 decreased travel slightly more than other states, but travel in all states decreased significantly. Using data on hourly electricity consumption by electricity region (e.g., balancing authority), we find that electricity consumption fell about six percent on average by mid-April with substantial heterogeneity. Given these decreases in travel and electricity use, we estimate the county-level expected improvements in air quality, and therefore expected declines in mortality. Overall, we estimate that, for a month of social distancing, the expected premature deaths due to air pollution from personal vehicle travel and electricity consumption declined by approximately 360 deaths, or about 25% of the baseline 1500 deaths. In addition, we estimate that CO2 emissions from these sources fell by 46 million metric tons (a reduction of approximately 19%) over the same time frame.

中文摘要

COVID-19大流行导致美国在2020年春季实施了居家政策和其他社交距离行为。本文研究了这些行动通过减少个人车辆出行和电力消耗对排放和预期健康影响产生的影响。利用美国每个县的每日手机流动性数据，我们发现到4月中旬，全国范围内的车辆出行下降了约40%。在3月28日之前实施居家政策的州，其出行减少幅度略大于其他州，但所有州的出行都显著减少。利用电力区域（例如平衡机构）的每小时电力消耗数据，我们发现到4月中旬，平均电力消耗下降了约6%，且存在显著的异质性。鉴于出行和电力使用的这些减少，我们估算了县级预期的空气质量改善，从而预期死亡率下降。总体而言，我们估计，在一个月的社交距离期间，因个人车辆出行和电力消耗导致的空气污染预期过早死亡人数减少了约360人，约占基线1500人死亡人数的25%。此外，我们估计，在同一时期内，这些来源的二氧化碳排放量减少了4600万公吨（减少了约19%）。

No. 158论文详情NBER w27134

Social Interactions in Pandemics: Fear, Altruism, and Reciprocity

大流行中的社会互动：恐惧、利他主义和互惠

Laura Alfaro, Ester Faia, Nora Lamersdorf, Farzad Saidi

Abstract

Social interactions and social preferences play a central role in public health domains. In the face of a pandemic, individuals adjust their behavior, whereas in SIR models infection rates are typically exogenous. City-level data across countries suggest that mobility falls in response to fear, proxied by Google searches. Incorporating experimentally validated measures of social preferences at the regional level, we find that stringency measures matter less when individuals are more patient, altruistic, or exhibit less negative reciprocity. To account for these findings, we extend homogeneous and networked SIR models by endogenizing agents' social-activity intensity and incorporating social preferences. Our quantitative predictions markedly differ from those of the naïve SIR network model. We derive the planner's problem, and show that neglecting agents' endogenous response leads to misguided policy decisions of various non-pharmaceutical interventions. Any further mobility restrictions, beyond agents' restraint, result from aggregate externalities which are curtailed by social preferences.

中文摘要

社会互动和社会偏好在公共卫生领域发挥着核心作用。面对大流行，个体会调整其行为，而在SIR模型中，感染率通常是外生的。跨国城市层面的数据表明，流动性会因恐惧（以谷歌搜索为代理指标）而下降。结合在区域层面经过实验验证的社会偏好指标，我们发现当个体更有耐心、更利他或表现出较少的消极互惠时，严格措施的重要性会降低。为了解释这些发现，我们通过内生化个体的社会活动强度并纳入社会偏好，扩展了同质和网络化的SIR模型。我们的定量预测与朴素SIR网络模型的预测显著不同。我们推导了规划者的问题，并表明忽视个体的内生反应会导致对各种非药物干预措施的政策决策产生误导。任何超出个体自我约束的进一步流动性限制，都是由社会偏好所抑制的总体外部性造成的。

No. 159论文详情NBER w27133

Trade and Welfare (Across Local Labor Markets)

贸易与福利（跨地方劳动力市场）

Ryan Kim, Jonathan Vogel, Moises Yi

Abstract

What are the welfare implications of trade shocks? Theoretically, we provide a sufficient statistic that measures changes in welfare (to a first-order approximation) for the set of workers who start within a region, taking into account adjustment in frictional unemployment, labor force participation, the sectors to which workers apply for jobs, and the regions in which workers choose to live. Our theory is flexible; for instance, it allows for arbitrary heterogeneity in worker productivity and non-pecuniary returns (amenities) across unemployment, labor force non-participation, sectors, and regions. Empirically, we apply these insights to measure changes in welfare between 2000-2007 across workers who start in different commuting zones (CZs) in the U.S. in the year 2000. Finally, we identify the differential impact across CZs of a particular trade shock: granting China permanent normal trade relations.

中文摘要

贸易冲击的福利含义是什么？在理论上，我们提供了一个充分统计量，用于衡量从一个地区开始的工人群体的福利变化（一阶近似），同时考虑了摩擦性失业、劳动力参与率、工人申请工作的部门以及工人选择居住的地区的调整。我们的理论是灵活的；例如，它允许在失业、劳动力非参与、部门和地区之间，工人生产率和非金钱回报（便利设施）存在任意异质性。在实证上，我们应用这些见解来衡量2000年至2007年间，从2000年美国不同通勤区（CZ）开始的工人之间的福利变化。最后，我们识别了一个特定贸易冲击（给予中国永久正常贸易关系地位）在不同通勤区之间的差异化影响。

No. 160论文详情NBER w27132

Determinants of Disparities in Covid-19 Job Losses

Covid-19失业差异的决定因素

Laura Montenovo, Xuan Jiang, Felipe Lozano Rojas, Ian M. Schmutte, Kosali I. Simon, Bruce A. Weinberg, Coady Wing

Abstract

We make several contributions to understanding the socio-demographic divide in early labor market responses to the U.S. COVID-19 epidemic and its policies, benchmarked against two previous recessions. First, monthly Current Population Survey (CPS) data show greater declines in employment in April and May 2020 (relative to February) for Hispanics, younger workers, and those with high school degrees and some college. Between April and May, all the demographic subgroups considered regained some employment. Re-employment in May was broadly proportional to the employment drop that occurred through April, except for Blacks who experienced a smaller rebound. Further, we show that compared to the 2001 recession and the Great Recession, employment losses in the early COVID-19 recession were smaller for groups with very low or very high (vs. medium) education. Second, we show that job loss was larger in occupations that require more interpersonal contact and that cannot be performed remotely. Third, we find pre-COVID-19 sorting of workers into occupations and industries along demographic lines can explain a sizeable portion of the gender, race, and ethnic gaps in new unemployment. For example, while women did suffer more job losses than men, their disproportionate pre-epidemic sorting into remote work compatible occupations shielded women from what would have been even larger employment losses during the epidemic. However, there remain substantial gaps in employment losses across groups that cannot be explained by socio-economic differences. We find some larger gaps in labor market impacts when we consider the “employed but absent from work” measure present in the CPS, in addition to the more traditional employment and unemployment measures. We conclude with a discussion of policy lessons and future research needs implied by the disparities in early labor market losses from the COVID-19 crisis.

中文摘要

我们对理解美国COVID-19疫情及其政策在早期劳动力市场反应中的社会人口学差异做出了若干贡献，并以两次之前的衰退作为基准。首先，月度当前人口调查（CPS）数据显示，2020年4月和5月（相对于2月），西班牙裔、年轻工人以及拥有高中学历和部分大学学历的工人就业下降幅度更大。在4月至5月期间，所有考虑的人口亚组都恢复了一些就业。5月份的再就业与截至4月份的就业下降幅度大致成比例，但黑人除外，他们的反弹较小。此外，我们表明，与2001年衰退和大衰退相比，早期COVID-19衰退中，教育水平极低或极高（相对于中等）的群体的就业损失较小。其次，我们表明，在需要更多人际接触且无法远程完成的职业中，失业更大。第三，我们发现，COVID-19之前工人按人口特征在职业和行业中的分类，可以解释新失业中性别、种族和民族差距的相当大一部分。例如，虽然女性确实比男性遭受更多的失业，但她们在疫情前不成比例地分类到可远程工作的职业中，这保护了女性，使其免于在疫情期间遭受更大的就业损失。然而，不同群体之间仍然存在无法用社会经济差异解释的就业损失差距。当我们考虑CPS中存在的“有工作但缺勤”指标以及更传统的就业和失业指标时，我们发现劳动力市场影响的一些更大差距。最后，我们讨论了COVID-19危机早期劳动力市场损失差异所暗示的政策教训和未来研究需求。

The First Weeks of the Coronavirus Crisis: Who Got Hit, When and Why? Evidence from Norway

新冠疫情危机的最初几周：谁受到了冲击、何时以及为何？来自挪威的证据

Annette Alstadsæter, Bernt Bratsberg, Gaute Eielsen, Wojciech Kopczuk, Simen Markussen, Oddbjorn Raaum, Knut Røed

Abstract

Using real-time register data we document the magnitude, dynamics and socio-economic characteristics of the crisis-induced temporary and permanent layoffs in Norway. We find evidence that the effects of social distancing measures quickly spread to industries that were not directly affected by policy. Close to 90% of layoffs are temporary, although this classification may change as the crisis progresses. Still, there is suggestive evidence of immediate stress on a subset of firms that manifests itself in permanent rather than temporary layoffs. We find that the shock had a strong socio-economic gradient, hit a financially vulnerable population, and parents with younger children, and was driven by layoffs in smaller, less productive, and financially weaker firms. Consequently though, the rise in unemployment likely overstates the loss of output associated with the layoffs by about a third.

中文摘要

利用实时登记数据，我们记录了挪威由危机引发的临时性和永久性裁员的范围、动态及社会经济特征。我们发现证据表明，社交距离措施的影响迅速蔓延至未受政策直接影响的行业。近90%的裁员是临时性的，尽管随着危机的发展，这一分类可能会发生变化。然而，有迹象表明，部分企业立即面临压力，表现为永久性而非临时性裁员。我们发现，此次冲击具有强烈的社会经济梯度，冲击了财务脆弱的群体以及有年幼子女的父母，并且是由规模较小、生产率较低且财务实力较弱的企业裁员所驱动。因此，失业率的上升可能高估了与裁员相关的产出损失约三分之一。

Does Biology Drive Child Penalties? Evidence from Biological and Adoptive Families

生物学因素是否驱动了育儿惩罚？来自亲生家庭和收养家庭的证据

Henrik Kleven, Camille Landais, Jakob Egholt Søgaard

Abstract

This paper investigates if the impact of children on the labor market outcomes of women relative to men — child penalties — can be explained by the biological links between mother and child. We estimate child penalties in biological and adoptive families using event studies around the arrival of children and almost forty years of adoption data from Denmark. Short-run child penalties are slightly larger for biological mothers than for adoptive mothers, but their long-run child penalties are virtually identical and precisely estimated. This suggests that biology is not a key driver of child-related gender gaps.

中文摘要

本文研究子女对女性相对于男性劳动力市场结果的影响——即育儿惩罚——是否可以通过母亲与子女之间的生物学联系来解释。我们利用丹麦近四十年的收养数据，围绕子女出生进行事件研究，估计了亲生家庭和收养家庭中的育儿惩罚。短期育儿惩罚在亲生母亲中略大于收养母亲，但她们的长期育儿惩罚几乎相同且估计精确。这表明生物学因素并非与子女相关的性别差距的关键驱动因素。

International Equity and Debt Flows: Composition, Crisis, and Controls

国际股权与债务流动：构成、危机与管制

Chang Ma, Shang-Jin Wei

Abstract

Standard models of capital flows to emerging market economies focus on debt flows and a pecuniary externality. However, by offering better risk sharing, international equity flows can render such externality unimportant, yet many economies fail to attract equity investment in a large quantity. We propose a theory of endogenous composition of capital flows that highlights two asymmetries. In our model, poor institutional quality leads to an inefficiently low share of equity financing as well as an inefficiently high volume of total inflows. Somewhat surprisingly, a social planner would often impose taxes on both equity and debt inflows. Our story differs in important ways from an alternative narrative focusing on collateral constraint.

中文摘要

关于新兴市场经济体资本流动的标准模型侧重于债务流动和货币外部性。然而，通过提供更好的风险分担，国际股权流动可能使这种外部性变得不重要，但许多经济体未能吸引大量股权投资。我们提出了一种资本流动内生构成的理论，强调了两种不对称性。在我们的模型中，制度质量低下导致股权融资份额过低且总流入量过高。有些出人意料的是，社会规划者通常会对股权和债务流入都征税。我们的故事与侧重于抵押品约束的另一种叙事在重要方面有所不同。

Estimating and Simulating a SIRD Model of COVID-19 for Many Countries, States, and Cities

估计和模拟多个国家、州和城市的COVID-19 SIRD模型

Jesús Fernández-Villaverde, Charles I. Jones

Abstract

We use data on deaths in New York City, Madrid, Stockholm, and other world cities as well as in various U.S. states and various countries and regions to estimate a standard epidemiological model of COVID-19. We allow for a time-varying contact rate in order to capture behavioral and policy-induced changes associated with social distancing. We simulate the model forward to consider possible futures for various countries, states, and cities, including the potential impact of herd immunity on re-opening. Our current baselinemortality rate (IFR) is assumed to be 1.0% but we recognize there is substantial uncertainty about this number. Our model fits the death data equally well with alternative mortality rates of 0.5% or 1.2%, so this parameter is unidentified in our data. However, its value matters enormously for the extent to which various places can relax social distancing without spurring a resurgence of deaths.

中文摘要

我们利用纽约市、马德里、斯德哥尔摩及其他世界城市以及美国各州和多个国家及地区的死亡数据，估计了一个标准的COVID-19流行病学模型。我们允许接触率随时间变化，以捕捉与社交距离相关的行为和政策诱导变化。我们向前模拟模型，以考虑各个国家、州和城市的可能未来，包括群体免疫对重新开放的潜在影响。我们当前的基线死亡率（IFR）假设为1.0%，但我们认识到这个数字存在很大的不确定性。我们的模型在替代死亡率0.5%或1.2%的情况下同样能很好地拟合死亡数据，因此该参数在我们的数据中无法识别。然而，其值对于各地在多大程度上可以放松社交距离而不引发死亡病例反弹至关重要。

Is the Cure Worse than the Problem Itself? Immediate Labor Market Effects of COVID-19 Case Rates and School Closures in the U.S.

治疗比问题本身更糟糕吗？美国COVID-19病例率和学校关闭的即时劳动力市场效应

Felipe Lozano Rojas, Xuan Jiang, Laura Montenovo, Kosali I. Simon, Bruce A. Weinberg, Coady Wing

Abstract

The relationship between population health and measures of economic well-being and economic activity is a long standing topic in health economics (Preston, 1975; Cutler, Deaton, and Lleras-Muney, 2006; Ruhm, 2000). The conceptual issues in analyzing the complicated link between health and economic well-being are central to understanding the implications of the COVID-19 epidemic in the United States The public health shock of the epidemic has direct economic impacts, but the mitigation policies governments are using to control the spread of the virus may also damage economic activity. We estimate how state job market conditions respond to state COVID-19 infections and school closures, which are the earliest of the major mitigation policies. Mitigation policies and local epidemiological conditions explain some of the variation in unemployment patterns. However, the historically unprecedented increase in new UI claims during the weeks of March 15-21 and March 22-28 was largely across-the-board and occurred in all states. This suggests most of the economic disruption was driven by the health shock itself. Put differently, it appears that the labor market slowdown was due primarily to a nationwide response to evolving epidemiological conditions and that individual state policies and own epidemiologic situations have had a comparatively modest effect.

中文摘要

人口健康与经济福祉和经济活动衡量指标之间的关系是健康经济学中的一个长期主题（Preston, 1975; Cutler, Deaton, and Lleras-Muney, 2006; Ruhm, 2000）。分析健康与经济福祉之间复杂联系的概念性问题，对于理解美国COVID-19疫情的影响至关重要。疫情带来的公共卫生冲击具有直接的经济影响，但政府为控制病毒传播而采取的缓解政策也可能损害经济活动。我们估计各州就业市场状况如何响应各州的COVID-19感染和学校关闭——这是最早的主要缓解政策之一。缓解政策和地方流行病学状况解释了失业模式的部分变化。然而，在3月15日至21日和3月22日至28日这两周内，新增失业保险申请出现了历史性的普遍增长，且发生在所有州。这表明大部分经济混乱是由健康冲击本身驱动的。换句话说，劳动力市场放缓似乎主要是由于全国范围内对不断变化的流行病学状况的反应，而各州的具体政策和自身的流行病学状况影响相对较小。

No. 166论文详情NBER w27126

Does Information Disclosure Improve Consumer Knowledge? Evidence from a Randomized Experiment of Restaurant Menu Calorie Labels

信息披露能改善消费者知识吗？来自餐厅菜单卡路里标签随机实验的证据

John Cawley, Alex M. Susskind, Barton Willage

Abstract

The United States, in 2018, implemented a nationwide requirement that chain restaurants disclose calorie information on their menus and menu boards. This law was motivated by concern that consumers underestimate the number of calories in restaurant food, but it remains unclear the extent to which this information disclosure affects consumer knowledge. This paper fills that gap by estimating the impact of information disclosure on consumer knowledge through a randomized controlled field experiment of calorie labels on the menus of a full-service restaurant. The results indicate that information disclosure significantly reduces the extent to which consumers underestimate the number of calories in restaurant food; the labels improve the accuracy of consumers’ post-meal estimates of the number of calories they ordered by 4.0 percent and reduces by 28.9% the probability of underestimating the calories in one’s meal by 50% or more, both of which are statistically significant. However, even after information disclosure, there remains considerable error in consumer beliefs about the calorie content of the restaurant food they ordered. Even among the treatment group who received calorie labels, the average absolute value of percent error in their report is 34.2%.

中文摘要

美国于2018年实施了一项全国性要求，规定连锁餐厅在其菜单和菜单板上披露卡路里信息。这项法律是出于对消费者低估餐厅食品卡路里数量的担忧，但尚不清楚这种信息披露在多大程度上影响消费者的知识。本文通过在一家全方位服务餐厅的菜单上进行卡路里标签的随机对照现场实验，填补了这一空白，估计了信息披露对消费者知识的影响。结果表明，信息披露显著降低了消费者低估餐厅食品卡路里数量的程度；标签使消费者餐后对订购卡路里数量的估计准确度提高了4.0%，并将低估餐食卡路里50%或以上的概率降低了28.9%，两者均具有统计显著性。然而，即使在信息披露之后，消费者对其订购的餐厅食品卡路里含量的认知仍然存在相当大的误差。即使在收到卡路里标签的处理组中，其报告的平均绝对百分比误差为34.2%。

No. 167论文详情NBER w27125

The Effects of Need-Based Financial Aid on Employment and Earnings: Experimental Evidence from the Fund for Wisconsin Scholars

基于需求的财政援助对就业和收入的影响：来自威斯康星学者基金的实验证据

Deven E. Carlson, Alex Schmidt, Sarah Souders, Barbara L. Wolfe

Abstract

In this paper, we leverage the random assignment of a need-based financial aid grant offer—the Fund for Wisconsin Scholars (FFWS) grant—and several sets of administrative records to provide experimental evidence on the effects of the grant offer on students’ in-state employment and earnings. For students in four-year universities, our results demonstrate significant employment reductions in the two years immediately following the aid offer as well as in the sixth, seventh, and eighth after receiving the randomized grant offer. We also find the aid offer to reduce these students’ in-state earnings throughout the full eight-year period we study. However, we show that the aid offer increases student grade point average, suggesting that the employment and earnings reductions during students’ in-college years are attributable to a reallocation of time and effort away from employment and toward coursework. For students’ post-college years, we provide suggestive evidence that the reductions are attributable to a combination of two mechanisms: 1) Reduced loan debt offering greater financial flexibility when selecting among employment options, and 2) Offer-induced outstate migration. We find little evidence that the FFWS grant offer affects the labor market outcomes of students in two-year institutions, although the effects for students in technical colleges are significantly more positive than the effects for students in two-year colleges in the University of Wisconsin System.

中文摘要

在本文中，我们利用基于需求的财政援助助学金——威斯康星学者基金（FFWS）助学金——的随机分配以及多套行政记录，提供了关于助学金提供对学生州内就业和收入影响的实验证据。对于四年制大学的学生，我们的结果显示，在获得助学金后的最初两年以及获得随机助学金后的第六、第七和第八年，就业显著减少。我们还发现，助学金提供在我们研究的整个八年期间减少了这些学生的州内收入。然而，我们表明助学金提供提高了学生的平均绩点，这表明学生在大学期间的就业和收入减少可归因于时间和精力从就业向课程学习的重新分配。对于学生毕业后的年份，我们提供了暗示性证据，表明这些减少归因于两种机制的结合：1）减少的贷款债务提供了在选择就业选项时更大的财务灵活性，以及2）助学金引发的州外迁移。我们几乎没有发现FFWS助学金提供影响两年制院校学生劳动力市场结果的证据，尽管对技术学院学生的影响显著比对威斯康星大学系统内两年制学院学生的影响更为积极。

No. 168论文详情NBER w27124

Covid-19, Shelter-In Place Strategies and Tipping

COVID-19、居家策略与临界点

Zhihan Cui, Geoffrey Heal, Howard Kunreuther

Abstract

Social distancing via shelter-in-place strategies has emerged as the most effective way to combat Covid-19. In the United States, choices about such policies are made by individual states. Here we show that the policy choice made by one state influences the incentives that other states face to adopt similar policies: they can be viewed as strategic complements in a supermodular game. If they satisfy the condition of uniform strict increasing differences then following Heal and Kunreuther ([6]) we show that if enough states engage in social distancing, they will tip others to do the same and thus shift the Nash equilibrium with respect to the number of states engaging in social distancing.

中文摘要

通过居家策略进行社交距离已成为对抗COVID-19最有效的方式。在美国，此类政策的选择由各州自行决定。在此我们表明，一个州做出的政策选择会影响其他州采取类似政策的激励：它们可以被视为超模博弈中的战略互补品。如果它们满足严格递增差异的一致条件，那么按照Heal和Kunreuther（[6]）的研究，我们证明，如果有足够多的州采取社交距离措施，它们将促使其他州也这样做，从而改变关于采取社交距离措施州数量的纳什均衡。

No. 169论文详情NBER w27123

The Wealth of Generations, With Special Attention to the Millennials

代际财富：聚焦千禧一代

William G. Gale, Hilary Gelfond, Jason J. Fichtner, Benjamin H. Harris

Abstract

We examine household wealth across birth cohorts and over time using data from the Survey of Consumer Finances. We show that although the Great Recession reduced wealth in every age group, longer-term trends indicate that the wealth of older age groups has increased while the wealth of younger age groups has declined. A substantial share of these changes, in both directions, can be explained by changes in household demographic and economic characteristics. As for the millennial generation, their median wealth in 2016 was lower than the wealth of any similarly aged cohort between 1989 and 2007. Millennials will have several advantages in wealth accumulation relative to previous generations, such as more education and longer working lives, but also several disadvantages, including weak prospects for economic growth and delays in home purchase and marriage. The millennial generation contains a significantly higher percentage of minorities than previous generations. We estimate that minority households have tended to accumulate less wealth than whites in the past, controlling for household characteristics, and the difference appears to be growing over time for Blacks relative to whites. These results apply to the period before the COVID-19 pandemic and are best interpreted as addressing generational wealth patterns through 2016 and providing a pre-COVID benchmark against which future studies can be compared.

中文摘要

我们利用消费者金融调查数据，考察了不同出生队列和随时间变化的家庭财富状况。研究表明，尽管大衰退减少了每个年龄组的财富，但长期趋势显示，老年组的财富有所增加，而年轻组的财富则有所下降。这些变化（无论是增加还是减少）中，有很大一部分可以通过家庭人口统计和经济特征的变化来解释。至于千禧一代，他们2016年的财富中位数低于1989年至2007年间任何同龄队列的财富水平。与前几代人相比，千禧一代在财富积累方面将拥有若干优势，例如更高的教育水平和更长的工作年限，但也面临若干劣势，包括经济增长前景疲软以及购房和结婚的延迟。千禧一代中少数族裔的比例显著高于前几代人。我们估计，过去少数族裔家庭的财富积累往往少于白人家庭，在控制家庭特征后，这种差异对于黑人相对于白人而言似乎随着时间的推移而扩大。这些结果适用于COVID-19大流行之前的时期，最好将其理解为探讨截至2016年的代际财富模式，并提供一个COVID前的基准，以便未来研究进行比较。

No. 170论文详情NBER w27122

The Macroeconomics of Automation: Data, Theory, and Policy Analysis

自动化的宏观经济学：数据、理论与政策分析

Nir Jaimovich, Itay Saporta-Eksten, Henry E. Siu, Yaniv Yedid-Levi

Abstract

During the last four decades, the U.S. has experienced a fall in the employment in middle-wage, "routine-task-intensive," occupations. We analyze the characteristics of those who used to be employed in such occupations and show that this type of individual is nowadays more likely to be out of the labor force or working in low-paying occupations. Based on these findings, we develop a quantitative, general equilibrium model, with heterogeneous agents, labor force participation, occupational choice, and investment in physical and automation capital. We first use the model to evaluate the distributional consequences of automation. We find heterogeneity in its impact across different occupations, leading to a significant polarization in welfare. We then use this framework as a laboratory to evaluate various public policies such as retraining, and explicitly redistributive policies that transfer resources from those who benefit from automation to those who bear the brunt of its costs. We assess the tradeoffs between the aggregate impact and welfare distributional consequences of such policies.

中文摘要

在过去四十年中，美国中等工资、“常规任务密集型”职业的就业率有所下降。我们分析了曾受雇于此类职业的个体的特征，并表明这类个体如今更有可能退出劳动力市场或从事低薪职业。基于这些发现，我们构建了一个包含异质性主体、劳动力参与、职业选择以及实物资本和自动化资本投资的定量一般均衡模型。我们首先利用该模型评估自动化的分配效应。我们发现其影响在不同职业之间存在异质性，导致福利显著极化。然后，我们将该框架用作实验室，评估各种公共政策，例如再培训政策，以及明确的再分配政策（即将资源从自动化受益者转移给承担其成本主要冲击的人群）。我们评估了这些政策在总体影响和福利分配后果之间的权衡。

No. 171论文详情NBER w27121

COVID-19 and the Welfare Effects of Reducing Contagion

COVID-19与降低传染的福利效应

Robert S. Pindyck

Abstract

I use a simple SIR model, augmented to include deaths, to elucidate how pandemic progression is affected by the control of contagion, and examine the key trade-offs that underlie policy design. I illustrate how the cost of reducing the "reproduction number" R0 depends on how it changes the infection rate, the total and incremental number of deaths, the duration of the pandemic, and the possibility and impact of a second wave. Reducing R0 reduces the number of deaths, but extends the duration (and hence economic cost) of the pandemic, and it increases the fraction of the population still susceptible at the end, raising the possibility of a second wave. The benefit of reducing R0 is largely lives saved, and the incremental number of lives saved rises as R0 is reduced. But using a VSL estimate to value those lives is problematic.

中文摘要

我使用一个简单的SIR模型（并扩展纳入死亡因素），阐明大流行的进程如何受到传染控制的影响，并审视政策设计背后的关键权衡。我阐述了降低“基本再生数”R0的成本如何取决于它如何改变感染率、总死亡人数和增量死亡人数、大流行的持续时间，以及第二波疫情的可能性和影响。降低R0会减少死亡人数，但会延长疫情持续时间（从而增加经济成本），并且会增加疫情结束时仍易感的人口比例，从而提高了第二波疫情的可能性。降低R0的收益主要是挽救生命，并且随着R0的降低，挽救的增量生命数量会增加。但使用统计生命价值（VSL）估算来评估这些生命价值是有问题的。

No. 172论文详情NBER w27120

The Value of Health Insurance during a Crisis: Effects of Medicaid Implementation on Pandemic Influenza Mortality

危机期间健康保险的价值：医疗补助实施对大流行流感死亡率的影响

Karen Clay, Joshua A. Lewis, Edson R. Severnini, Xiao Wang

Abstract

This paper studies how better access to public health insurance affects infant mortality during pandemics. Our analysis combines cross-state variation in mandated eligibility for Medicaid with two influenza pandemics – the 1957-58 “Asian Flu” Pandemic and the 1968-69 “Hong Kong Flu” Pandemic – that arrived shortly before and after the program's introduction. Exploiting heterogeneity in the underlying severity of these two shocks across counties, we find no relationship between Medicaid eligibility and pandemic infant mortality during the 1957-58 outbreak. In contrast during the 1968-1969 pandemic, which occurred after Medicaid implementation, we find that better access to insurance in high-eligibility states substantially reduced infant mortality. The reductions in pandemic infant mortality are too large to be attributable solely to new Medicaid recipients, suggesting that the expansion in health insurance coverage mitigated disease transmission among the broader population.

中文摘要

本文研究了在大流行期间，改善公共健康保险的可及性如何影响婴儿死亡率。我们的分析结合了各州在医疗补助强制资格方面的差异，以及两次流感大流行——即在该计划引入前后不久发生的1957-58年“亚洲流感”大流行和1968-69年“香港流感”大流行。利用这两个冲击在各县潜在严重程度的异质性，我们发现，在1957-58年疫情爆发期间，医疗补助资格与大流行婴儿死亡率之间没有关系。相比之下，在1968-69年大流行期间（发生在医疗补助实施之后），我们发现，在资格较高的州，更好的保险可及性显著降低了婴儿死亡率。大流行婴儿死亡率的降低幅度太大，不能仅仅归因于新的医疗补助受助人，这表明健康保险覆盖范围的扩大减轻了疾病在更广泛人群中的传播。

No. 173论文详情NBER w27119

A Note on Long-Run Persistence of Public Health Outcomes in Pandemics

关于大流行中公共卫生结果长期持续性的注记

Peter Zhixian Lin, Christopher M. Meissner

Abstract

Covid-19 is the single largest threat to global public health since the Spanish Influenza pandemic of 1918-20. Was the world better prepared in 2020 than it was in 1918? After a century of public health and basic science research, pandemic response and mortality outcomes should be better than in 1918-20. We ask whether mortality from historical pandemics has any predictive content for mortality in the ongoing Covid-19 pandemic. We find a strong persistence in public health performance in the early days of the Covid-19 pandemic. Places that performed poorly in terms of mortality in 1918 were more likely to have higher mortality today. This is true across countries and across a sample of US cities. Experience with SARS is associated with lower mortality today. Distrust of expert advice, lack of cooperation at many levels, over-confidence, and health care supply shortages have likely promoted higher mortality today as in the past.

中文摘要

Covid-19是自1918-20年西班牙流感大流行以来对全球公共卫生的最大单一威胁。2020年的世界是否比1918年准备得更充分？经过一个世纪的公共卫生和基础科学研究，大流行应对和死亡率结果应该比1918-20年更好。我们询问历史大流行的死亡率是否对正在进行的Covid-19大流行的死亡率具有任何预测能力。我们发现，在Covid-19大流行初期，公共卫生表现存在很强的持续性。那些在1918年死亡率表现不佳的地方，如今更有可能出现更高的死亡率。这一结论在跨国样本和美国城市样本中均成立。经历过SARS疫情的地方，如今的死亡率较低。对专家建议的不信任、多个层面的合作缺失、过度自信以及医疗保健供应短缺，很可能像过去一样导致了如今更高的死亡率。

No. 174论文详情NBER w27118

Transfers vs Credit Policy: Macroeconomic Policy Trade-offs during Covid-19

转移支付与信贷政策：Covid-19期间的宏观经济政策权衡

Saki Bigio, Mengbo Zhang, Eduardo Zilberman

Abstract

The Covid-19 crisis has lead to a reduction in the demand and supply of sectors that produce goods that need social interaction to be produced or consumed. We interpret the Covid-19 shock as a shock that reduces utility stemming from “social” goods in a two-sector economy with incomplete markets. We compare the advantages of lump-sum transfers versus a credit policy. For the same path of government debt, transfers are preferable when debt limits are tight, whereas credit policy is preferable when they are slack. A credit policy has the advantage of targeting fiscal resources toward agents that matter most for stabilizing demand. We illustrate this result with a calibrated model. We discuss various shortcomings and possible extensions to the model.

中文摘要

Covid-19危机导致那些生产或消费需要社交互动的商品的部门的需求和供给减少。我们将Covid-19冲击解释为在一个具有不完全市场的两部门经济中，降低来自“社交”商品效用的冲击。我们比较了一次性转移支付与信贷政策的优势。在相同的政府债务路径下，当债务限额紧张时，转移支付更优；而当债务限额宽松时，信贷政策更优。信贷政策的优势在于能够将财政资源有针对性地分配给对稳定需求最为重要的主体。我们通过一个校准模型说明了这一结果。我们讨论了该模型的各种缺陷和可能的扩展方向。

No. 175论文详情NBER w27117

The Effect of Changes in Alcohol Tax Differentials on Alcohol Consumption

酒精税差异变化对酒精消费的影响

Markus Gehrsitz, Henry Saffer, Michael Grossman

Abstract

We show that tax-induced increases in alcohol prices can lead to substantial substitution and avoidance behavior that limits reductions in alcohol consumption. Causal estimates are derived from a natural experiment in Illinois where spirits and wine taxes were raised sharply and unexpectedly in 2009. Beer taxes were increased by only a trivial amount. We construct representative and consistent measures of alcohol prices and sales from scanner data collected for hundreds of products in several thousand stores across the US. Using several differences-in-differences models, we show that alcohol excise taxes are instantly over-shifted by a factor of up to 1.5. Consumers react by switching to less expensive products and increase purchases of low-tax alcoholic beverages, thus all but offsetting any moderate, tax-induced reductions in total ethanol consumption. Our study highlights the importance of tax-induced substitution, the implications of differential tax increases by beverage group and the impacts on public health of alternative types of tax hikes whose main aims are to increase revenue.

中文摘要

我们表明，税收引起的酒精价格上涨可能导致大量的替代和规避行为，从而限制了酒精消费的减少。因果估计源自伊利诺伊州的一项自然实验，该州在2009年突然且大幅提高了烈酒和葡萄酒的税收。啤酒税仅增加了微不足道的数额。我们利用从美国数千家商店收集的数百种产品的扫描数据，构建了具有代表性且一致的酒精价格和销售量指标。通过使用多种双重差分模型，我们表明酒精消费税会立即被过度转嫁，转嫁系数高达1.5。消费者的反应是转向更便宜的产品，并增加对低税酒精饮料的购买，从而几乎完全抵消了税收引起的适度总乙醇消费减少。我们的研究强调了税收引致替代的重要性、按饮料类别实施差异化增税的影响，以及以增加收入为主要目标的其他类型增税对公共健康的影响。

No. 176论文详情NBER w27116

The Fiscal Theory of Price Level with a Bubble

包含泡沫的价格水平财政理论

Markus K. Brunnermeier, Sebastian A. Merkel, Yuliy Sannikov

Abstract

This paper incorporates a bubble term in the standard Fiscal Theory of the Price Level equation to explain why countries with persistently negative primary surpluses can have a positively valued currency and low inflation. It also provides two illustrative models with closed-form solutions in which the return on government bonds is below the economy’s growth rate. The government can “mine” the bubble by perpetually rolling over its debt. Despite the bubble, the price level remains determined provided government policy credibly promises primary surpluses off-equilibrium. Sufficient “fiscal space” ensures that the bubble term is attached to government bonds rather than other assets, like crypto assets. The analysis provides a new perspective on debt sustainability analysis.

中文摘要

本文将泡沫项纳入标准的价格水平财政理论方程中，以解释为何持续存在负基本盈余的国家可以拥有正值的货币价值和低通胀。本文还提供了两个具有闭式解的说明性模型，其中政府债券的回报率低于经济的增长率。政府可以通过永久性地滚动其债务来“开采”泡沫。尽管存在泡沫，但只要政府政策可信地承诺在非均衡状态下实现基本盈余，价格水平仍然是确定的。足够的“财政空间”确保泡沫项附着于政府债券而非其他资产（如加密资产）。该分析为债务可持续性分析提供了一个新的视角。

No. 177论文详情NBER w27115

Debt and Taxes in Eight U.S. Wars and Two Insurrections

美国八场战争与两次叛乱中的债务与税收

George J. Hall, Thomas J. Sargent

Abstract

From decompositions of U.S. federal fiscal accounts from 1790 to 1988, we describe differences and patterns in how expenditure surges were financed during 8 wars between 1812 and 1975. We also study two insurrections. We use two benchmark theories of optimal taxation and borrowing to frame a narrative of how government decision makers reasoned and learned about how to manage a common set of forces that bedeviled them during all of the wars, forces that included interest rate risks, unknown durations of expenditure surges, government creditors' debt dilution fears, and temptations to use changes in units of account and inflation to restructure debts. Ex post real rates of return on government securities are a big part of our story.

中文摘要

通过对1790年至1988年美国联邦财政账户的分解，我们描述了1812年至1975年间八场战争中支出激增融资方式的差异与模式。我们还研究了两场叛乱。我们运用最优税收与借贷的两种基准理论，构建了一个叙事框架，阐述政府决策者如何推理并学习管理一系列在所有战争中都困扰他们的共同因素，这些因素包括利率风险、支出激增的未知持续时间、政府债权人对于债务稀释的担忧，以及利用记账单位变更和通货膨胀来重组债务的诱惑。政府证券的事后实际回报率是我们故事的重要组成部分。

No. 178论文详情NBER w27114

The Effect of the U.S.-China Trade War on U.S. Investment

中美贸易战对美国投资的影响

Mary Amiti, Sang Hoon Kong, David Weinstein

Abstract

We develop a new method of quantifying the impact of policy announcements on investment rates that makes use of stock market data. By estimating the effect of U.S.-China tariff announcements on aggregate returns and the differential returns of firms exposed to China, we identify their effect on treated and untreated firms. We show theoretically and empirically that estimates of policy-induced stock-market declines imply lower returns to capital, which lowers investment rates. We estimate that the tariff actions through 2018 and 2019 will lower the investment growth rate of listed U.S. companies by 1.9 percentage points by the end of 2020.

中文摘要

我们开发了一种新方法，利用股票市场数据量化政策公告对投资率的影响。通过估计中美关税公告对总体回报率以及受中国影响企业差异化回报率的影响，我们识别了这些公告对受处理企业和未受处理企业的作用。我们从理论和实证上表明，政策引发的股市下跌估计值意味着资本回报率下降，从而降低了投资率。我们估计，截至2018年和2019年的关税行动将使美国上市公司的投资增长率在2020年底前下降1.9个百分点。

No. 179论文详情NBER w27113

The Macroprudential Role of Stock Markets

股票市场的宏观审慎作用

Kyriakos T. Chousakos, Gary B. Gorton, Guillermo Ordoñez

Abstract

A financial crisis is an event of sudden information acquisition about the collateral backing short-term debt in credit markets. When investors see a financial crisis coming, however, they react by more intensively acquiring information about firms in stock markets, revealing those that are weaker, which as a consequence end up cut off from credit. This cleansing effect of stock markets’ information on credit markets’ composition discourage information acquisition about the collateral of the firms remaining in credit markets, slowing down credit growth and potentially preventing a crisis. Production of information in stock markets, then, acts as a macroprudential tool in the economy.

中文摘要

金融危机是信贷市场中关于短期债务抵押品的信息突然获取事件。然而，当投资者预见到金融危机来临时，他们的反应是在股票市场中更密集地获取企业信息，从而揭示出那些较弱的企业，这些企业最终因此被切断信贷来源。股票市场信息对信贷市场构成的这种“净化效应”，会抑制对仍留在信贷市场中的企业抵押品的信息获取，从而减缓信贷增长，并可能阻止危机的发生。因此，股票市场中的信息生产在经济中起到了宏观审慎工具的作用。

No. 180论文详情NBER w27112

Monetary and Fiscal Policies in Times of Large Debt: Unity is Strength

高债务时期的货币与财政政策：团结就是力量

Francesco Bianchi, Renato Faccini, Leonardo Melosi

Abstract

The COVID pandemic found policymakers facing constraints on their ability to react to an exceptionally large negative shock. The current low interest rate environment limits the tools the central bank can use to stabilize the economy, while the large public debt curtails the efficacy of fiscal interventions by inducing expectations of costly fiscal adjustments. Against this background, we study the implications of a coordinated fiscal and monetary strategy aiming at creating a controlled rise of inflation to wear away a targeted fraction of debt. Under this coordinated strategy, the fiscal authority introduces an emergency budget with no provisions on how it will be balanced, while the monetary authority tolerates a temporary increase in inflation to accommodate the emergency budget. In our model the coordinated strategy enhances the efficacy of the fiscal stimulus planned in response to the COVID pandemic and allows the Federal Reserve to correct a prolonged period of below-target inflation. The strategy results in only moderate levels of inflation by separating long-run fiscal sustainability from a short-run policy intervention.

中文摘要

新冠疫情使政策制定者面临应对异常巨大负面冲击的能力限制。当前的低利率环境限制了央行可用于稳定经济的工具，而庞大的公共债务则通过引发对昂贵财政调整的预期，削弱了财政干预的效果。在此背景下，我们研究了一种协调的财政与货币策略的含义，该策略旨在制造可控的通胀上升，以侵蚀目标比例的债务。在这种协调策略下，财政当局引入一项紧急预算，但不规定如何平衡该预算，而货币当局则容忍通胀暂时上升以适应紧急预算。在我们的模型中，这种协调策略增强了为应对新冠疫情而计划的财政刺激的有效性，并允许美联储纠正长期低于目标的通胀。通过将长期财政可持续性与短期政策干预分开，该策略仅导致温和的通胀水平。

No. 181论文详情NBER w27111

An Economic Approach to Regulating Algorithms

监管算法的经济学方法

Ashesh Rambachan, Jon Kleinberg, Sendhil Mullainathan, Jens Ludwig

Abstract

There is growing concern about "algorithmic bias" - that predictive algorithms used in decision-making might bake in or exacerbate discrimination in society. We argue that such concerns are naturally addressed using the tools of welfare economics. This approach overturns prevailing wisdom about the remedies for algorithmic bias. First, when a social planner builds the algorithm herself, her equity preference has no effect on the training procedure. So long as the data, however biased, contain signal, they will be used and the learning algorithm will be the same. Equity preferences alone provide no reason to alter how information is extracted from data - only how that information enters decision-making. Second, when private (possibly discriminatory) actors are the ones building algorithms, optimal regulation involves algorithmic disclosure but otherwise no restriction on training procedures. Under such disclosure, the use of algorithms strictly reduces the extent of discrimination relative to a world in which humans make all the decisions.

中文摘要

人们日益担忧“算法偏见”——即决策中使用的预测算法可能固化或加剧社会中的歧视。我们认为，这种担忧自然可以通过福利经济学的工具来解决。这种方法推翻了关于算法偏见补救措施的普遍看法。首先，当社会规划者自己构建算法时，她的公平偏好对训练过程没有影响。只要数据（无论多么有偏见）包含信号，它们就会被使用，学习算法也将相同。仅凭公平偏好并不能提供改变信息提取方式的理由——只能改变信息如何进入决策过程。其次，当私人（可能是歧视性的）行为者是算法的构建者时，最优监管涉及算法披露，但除此之外不对训练过程施加限制。在这种披露下，与人类做出所有决策的世界相比，使用算法严格减少了歧视的程度。

No. 182论文详情NBER w27110

Social Security Wealth, Inequality, and Lifecycle Saving

社会保障财富、不平等与生命周期储蓄

John Sabelhaus, Alice Henriques Volz

Abstract

Wealth inequality in the US is high and rising, but Social Security is generally not considered in those wealth measures. Social Security Wealth (SSW) is the present value of future benefits that an individual will receive less the present value of future taxes they will pay. When an individual enters the labor force, they generally face a lifetime of taxes to pay before they will receive any benefits, and thus their initial SSW is generally low or negative. As an individual works and pays into the system their SSW grows and generally peaks somewhere around typical Social Security benefit claim ages. The accrual of SSW over the working life is most important for lower-income workers because the progressive Social Security benefit formula means that taxes paid while working are associated with proportionally higher benefits in retirement. We estimate SSW for individuals in the Survey of Consumer Finances (SCF) for 1995 through 2016 and use a pseudo-panel approach to empirically demonstrate those lifecycle patterns. We also show that including SSW in a comprehensive wealth measure generally reduces estimated levels of wealth inequality but does not reverse the upward trend in top wealth shares.

中文摘要

美国的财富不平等程度很高且仍在上升，但社会保障通常不被纳入这些财富衡量指标中。社会保障财富（SSW）是指个人未来将获得的福利现值减去其未来将支付的税收现值。当个人进入劳动力市场时，他们通常面临在获得任何福利之前需要缴纳一生的税收，因此其初始SSW通常较低或为负。随着个人工作并向系统缴款，其SSW增长，并通常在典型的社会保障福利申领年龄附近达到峰值。工作生涯中SSW的累积对低收入工人最为重要，因为累进的社会保障福利公式意味着工作期间缴纳的税款与退休后按比例获得的更高福利相关联。我们利用1995年至2016年消费者金融调查（SCF）中个人的数据估算SSW，并采用伪面板方法实证展示了这些生命周期模式。我们还表明，将SSW纳入综合财富衡量指标通常会降低财富不平等的估计水平，但不会逆转顶层财富份额的上升趋势。

No. 183论文详情NBER w27109

Taxation and Innovation: What Do We Know?

税收与创新：我们知道什么？

Ufuk Akcigit, Stefanie Stantcheva

Abstract

Tax policies are a wide array of tools, commonly used by governments to influence the economy. In this paper, we review the many margins through which tax policies can affect innovation, the main driver of economic growth in the long-run. These margins include the impact of tax policy on i) the quantity and quality of innovation; ii) the geographic mobility of innovation and inventors across U.S. states and countries; iii) the declining business dynamism in the U.S., firm entry, and productivity; iv) the quality composition of firms, inventors, and teams; and v) the direction of research effort, e.g., toward applied versus basic research, or toward dirty versus clean technologies. We give ideas drawn from research on how the design of policy can allow policy makers to foster the most productive firms without wasting public funds on less productive ones.

中文摘要

税收政策是政府用来影响经济的广泛工具。在本文中，我们回顾了税收政策影响创新（长期经济增长的主要驱动力）的多个渠道。这些渠道包括税收政策对以下方面的影响：i) 创新的数量和质量；ii) 创新和发明者在美国各州和国家之间的地理流动性；iii) 美国商业活力下降、企业进入和生产率；iv) 企业、发明者和团队的质量构成；以及v) 研究努力的方向，例如应用研究与基础研究，或污染技术与清洁技术。我们根据研究提出了一些政策设计思路，这些思路可以帮助政策制定者扶持最具生产力的企业，同时避免将公共资金浪费在生产力较低的企业上。

No. 184论文详情NBER w27108

The Variance Risk Premium in Equilibrium Models

均衡模型中的方差风险溢价

Geert Bekaert, Eric Engstrom, Andrey Ermolov

Abstract

The equity variance risk premium is the expected compensation earned for selling variance risk in equity markets. The variance risk premium is positive and shows moderate persistence. High variance risk premiums coincide with the left tail of the consumption growth distribution shifting down. These facts, together with a positive, yet moderate, difference between the risk-neutral entropy and variance of the aggregate market return, refute the bulk of the extant consumption-based asset pricing models. We introduce a tractable habit model that does fit the data. In the model, the variance risk premium depends positively (negatively) on “bad” (“good”) consumption growth uncertainty.

中文摘要

股票方差风险溢价是出售股票市场方差风险所获得的预期补偿。方差风险溢价为正且表现出适度的持续性。高方差风险溢价与消费增长分布左尾的下移同时发生。这些事实，加上总体市场回报的风险中性熵与方差之间存在正向但适度的差异，反驳了大多数现有的基于消费的资产定价模型。我们引入了一个符合数据的可处理习惯模型。在该模型中，方差风险溢价正向（负向）依赖于“坏”（“好”）消费增长的不确定性。

No. 185论文详情NBER w27107

Education and Innovation: The Long Shadow of the Cultural Revolution

教育与创新：文化大革命的长期阴影

Zhangkai Huang, Gordon M. Phillips, Jialun Yang, Yi Zhang

Abstract

The Cultural Revolution deprived Chinese students of the opportunity to receive higher education for 10 years when colleges and universities were closed from 1966-1976. We examine the human capital cost of this loss of education on subsequent innovation by firms, and ask if it impacted firms more than 30 years later. We examine the innovation of firms with CEOs who turned 18 during the Cultural Revolution, which sharply reduced their chances of attending college. Using multiple approaches to control for selection and endogeneity, including an instrument based on whether the CEO turned 18 during the Cultural Revolution and a regression discontinuity approach, we show that Chinese firms led by CEOs without a college degree spend less on R&D, generate fewer patents, and receive fewer citations to these patents.

中文摘要

文化大革命期间（1966-1976年），中国高等院校关闭长达10年，剥夺了学生接受高等教育的机会。本文考察了这种教育缺失对企业后续创新造成的人力资本成本，并探究其是否在30多年后仍对企业产生影响。我们研究了那些首席执行官在文化大革命期间年满18岁的企业的创新情况——这一年龄节点显著降低了他们上大学的机会。通过采用多种方法来控制选择性和内生性问题，包括基于首席执行官是否在文化大革命期间年满18岁的工具变量法以及断点回归方法，我们发现，由没有大学学位的首席执行官领导的中国企业在研发上的投入更少，产生的专利数量更少，这些专利获得的引用次数也更少。

No. 186论文详情NBER w27106

How Valuable is Financial Flexibility when Revenue Stops? Evidence from the COVID-19 Crisis

当收入停止时，财务灵活性有多大价值？来自COVID-19危机的证据

Rüdiger Fahlenbrach, Kevin Rageth, René M. Stulz

Abstract

Firms with greater financial flexibility should be better able to fund a revenue shortfall resulting from the COVID-19 shock and benefit less from policy responses. We find that firms with high financial flexibility experience a stock price drop lower by 26% or 9.7 percentage points than those with low financial flexibility accounting for a firm’s industry. This differential return persists as stock prices rebound. Similar results hold for CDS spreads. The stock price of a firm with an average payout over assets ratio would have dropped 2 percentage points less with no payouts for the last three years.

中文摘要

财务灵活性更强的企业应能更好地应对COVID-19冲击导致的收入短缺，并且从政策应对中获益更少。我们发现，在考虑企业所在行业的情况下，财务灵活性高的企业股价跌幅比财务灵活性低的企业低26%或9.7个百分点。这种差异化的回报在股价反弹时持续存在。信用违约互换利差也出现了类似的结果。一家过去三年没有派息、平均派息与资产比率的企业，其股价跌幅本可减少2个百分点。

No. 187论文详情NBER w27105

Pandemic Recession: L or V-Shaped?

大流行衰退：L型还是V型？

Victoria Gregory, Guido Menzio, David G. Wiczer

Abstract

We develop and calibrate a search-theoretic model of the labor market in order to forecast the evolution of the aggregate US labor market during and after the coronavirus pandemic. The model is designed to capture the heterogeneity of the transitions of individual workers across states of unemployment, employment and across different employers. The model is also designed to capture the trade-offs in the choice between temporary and permanent layoffs. Under reasonable parametrizations of the model, the lockdown instituted to prevent the spread of the novel coronavirus is shown to have long-lasting negative effects on unemployment. This is so because the lockdown disproportionately disrupts the employment of workers who need years to find stable jobs.

中文摘要

我们开发并校准了一个劳动力市场的搜索理论模型，以预测冠状病毒大流行期间及之后美国劳动力市场的总体演变。该模型旨在捕捉个体工人在失业、就业以及不同雇主之间状态转换的异质性。该模型还旨在捕捉临时裁员和永久裁员之间选择的权衡。在模型的合理参数化下，为阻止新型冠状病毒传播而实施的封锁被证明会对失业产生持久的负面影响。这是因为封锁不成比例地扰乱了那些需要多年才能找到稳定工作的工人的就业。

No. 188论文详情NBER w27104

The Macroeconomics of Testing and Quarantining

检测与隔离的宏观经济学

Martin S. Eichenbaum, Sergio Rebelo, Mathias Trabandt

Abstract

We develop a SIR-based macroeconomic model to study the impact of testing/quarantining and social distancing/mask use on health and economic outcomes. These policies can dramatically reduce the costs of an epidemic. Absent testing/quarantining, the main effect of social distancing and mask use on health outcomes is to delay, rather than reduce, epidemic-related deaths. Social distancing and mask use reduce the severity of the epidemic-related recession but prolong its duration. There is an important synergy between social distancing and mask use and testing/quarantining. Social distancing and mask use buy time for testing and quarantining to come to the rescue. The benefits of testing/quarantining are even larger when people can get reinfected, either because the virus mutates or immunity is temporary.

中文摘要

我们开发了一个基于SIR的宏观经济模型，以研究检测/隔离以及社交距离/口罩使用对健康和经济结果的影响。这些政策可以显著降低流行病的成本。在没有检测/隔离的情况下，社交距离和口罩使用对健康结果的主要影响是延迟而非减少与流行病相关的死亡。社交距离和口罩使用减轻了流行病相关衰退的严重程度，但延长了其持续时间。社交距离和口罩使用与检测/隔离之间存在重要的协同效应。社交距离和口罩使用为检测和隔离争取了时间来挽救局面。当人们可能再次感染时——无论是由于病毒变异还是免疫力暂时——检测/隔离的益处甚至更大。

No. 189论文详情NBER w27102

Optimal Targeted Lockdowns in a Multi-Group SIR Model

多群体SIR模型中的最优针对性封锁

Daron Acemoglu, Victor Chernozhukov, Iván Werning, Michael D. Whinston

Abstract

We study targeted lockdowns in a multi-group SIR model where infection, hospitalization and fatality rates vary between groups—in particular between the “young”, “the middle-aged” and the “old”. Our model enables a tractable quantitative analysis of optimal policy. For baseline parameter values for the COVID-19 pandemic applied to the US, we find that optimal policies differentially targeting risk/age groups significantly outperform optimal uniform policies and most of the gains can be realized by having stricter lockdown policies on the oldest group. Intuitively, a strict and long lockdown for the most vulnerable group both reduces infections and enables less strict lockdowns for the lower-risk groups. We also study the impacts of group distancing, testing and contract tracing, the matching technology and the expected arrival time of a vaccine on optimal policies. Overall, targeted policies that are combined with measures that reduce interactions between groups and increase testing and isolation of the infected can minimize both economic losses and deaths in our model.

中文摘要

我们在一个多群体SIR模型中研究针对性封锁，其中感染率、住院率和死亡率在不同群体之间存在差异——特别是在“年轻人”、“中年人”和“老年人”之间。我们的模型能够对最优政策进行易于处理的定量分析。对于应用于美国的COVID-19大流行的基准参数值，我们发现，针对风险/年龄组进行差异化处理的最优政策显著优于统一的政策，并且大部分收益可以通过对最年长群体实施更严格的封锁政策来实现。直观地说，对最脆弱群体实施严格且长期的封锁既能减少感染，也能对低风险群体实施不那么严格的封锁。我们还研究了群体隔离、检测和接触者追踪、匹配技术以及疫苗预期到达时间对最优政策的影响。总体而言，在我们的模型中，结合减少群体间互动措施以及加强检测和隔离感染者的针对性政策，可以最大限度地减少经济损失和死亡。

No. 190论文详情NBER w27101

Early Life Shocks, Market Adjustments, and Black-White Inequality

早期生活冲击、市场调整与黑人与白人之间的不平等

Karen Clay, Ethan J. Schmick

Abstract

This paper investigates the long run impacts of an early life agricultural shock on Black and White sons in the U.S. South. The boll weevil, one of the most destructive agricultural pests in American history, decreased cotton production and resulted in substantial changes to the Southern economy. The impact of this shock on children who were born before and after its arrival is not a priori obvious; it could be positive or negative depending on whether children born after the shock experienced better or worse early life conditions. To examine the empirical effects of this shock on Black and White fathers and sons, the analysis makes use of cross-census links from the Census Tree (Buckles et al., 2023) and race-specific difference-in-differences and triple difference empirical strategies. We find the arrival of the boll weevil benefited Black sons in the long run, as reflected in two 1940 measures of income – wages and imputed income – and did not harm White sons. These differential gains decreased inequality. We provide empirical and historical evidence on a range of mechanisms through which early life conditions may have improved for Black sons relative to White sons.

中文摘要

本文研究了美国南部早期农业冲击对黑人和白人儿子的长期影响。棉铃象甲是美国历史上最具破坏性的农业害虫之一，它的出现减少了棉花产量，并导致南方经济发生重大变化。这种冲击对冲击到来前后出生的儿童的影响并非先验明确；它可能是积极的，也可能是消极的，取决于冲击后出生的儿童是否经历了更好或更差的早期生活条件。为了考察这种冲击对黑人和白人父亲及儿子的实证影响，分析利用了来自Census Tree的跨人口普查链接以及针对种族的双重差分和三重差分实证策略。我们发现，棉铃象甲的到来在长期内使黑人儿子受益，这反映在1940年的两项收入指标——工资和推算收入——上，并且没有伤害白人儿子。这些差异化的收益减少了不平等。我们提供了一系列机制的经验和历史证据，通过这些机制，黑人儿子的早期生活条件相对于白人儿子可能得到了改善。

No. 191论文详情NBER w27100

Inequality of Fear and Self-Quarantine: Is There a Trade-off between GDP and Public Health?

恐惧与自我隔离的不平等：GDP与公共卫生之间存在权衡吗？

Sangmin Aum, Sang Yoon (Tim) Lee, Yongseok Shin

Abstract

We construct a quantitative model of an economy hit by an epidemic. People differ by age and skill, and choose occupations and whether to commute to work or work from home, to maximize their income and minimize their fear of infection. Occupations differ by wage, infection risk, and the productivity loss when working from home. By setting the model parameters to replicate the progression of COVID-19 in South Korea and the United Kingdom, we obtain three key results. First, government-imposed lock-downs may not present a clear trade-off between GDP and public health, as commonly believed, even though its immediate effect is to reduce GDP and infections by forcing people to work from home. A premature lifting of the lock-down raises GDP temporarily, but infections rise over the next months to a level at which many people choose to work from home, where they are less productive, driven by the fear of infection. A longer lock-down eventually mitigates the GDP loss as well as flattens the infection curve. Second, if the UK had adopted South Korean policies, its GDP loss and infections would have been substantially smaller both in the short and the long run. This is not because Korea implemented policies sooner, but because aggressive testing and tracking more effectively reduce infections and disrupt the economy less than a blanket lock-down. Finally, low-skill workers and self-employed lose the most from the epidemic and also from the government policies. However, the policy of issuing “visas” to those who have antibodies will disproportionately benefit the low-skilled, by relieving them of the fear of infection and also by allowing them to get back to work.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个受流行病冲击的经济体的定量模型。人们按年龄和技能划分，选择职业以及是否通勤上班或在家工作，以最大化他们的收入并最小化他们对感染的恐惧。不同职业的工资、感染风险以及在家工作时的生产力损失各不相同。通过设定模型参数以复制COVID-19在韩国和英国的传播过程，我们得到了三个关键结果。首先，政府实施的封锁可能并不像普遍认为的那样，在GDP和公共卫生之间存在明确的权衡，尽管其直接效果是通过迫使人们在家工作来减少GDP和感染。过早解除封锁会暂时提高GDP，但在接下来的几个月里，感染会上升到这样一个水平：出于对感染的恐惧，许多人选择在家工作，而他们在家的生产力较低。更长时间的封锁最终会减轻GDP损失，同时也能拉平感染曲线。其次，如果英国采用了韩国的政策，其GDP损失和感染在短期和长期内都会小得多。这不是因为韩国更早实施政策，而是因为积极的检测和追踪比全面封锁更有效地减少感染，并且对经济的破坏更小。最后，低技能工人和个体经营者从流行病以及政府政策中损失最大。然而，向拥有抗体的人发放“签证”的政策将不成比例地使低技能者受益，既减轻了他们对感染的恐惧，也允许他们重返工作岗位。

No. 192论文详情NBER w27099

Health vs. Wealth? Public Health Policies and the Economy During Covid-19

健康还是财富？COVID-19期间的公共卫生政策与经济

Zhixian Lin, Christopher M. Meissner

Abstract

We study the impact of non-pharmaceutical policy interventions (NPIs) like “stay-at-home” orders on the spread of infectious disease. Local policies have little impact on the economy nor on local public health. Stay-at-home is only weakly associated with slower growth of Covid-19 cases. Reductions in observed “mobility” are not associated with slower growth of Covid-19 cases. Stay-at-home is associated with lower workplace and more residential activity, but common shocks matter much more. Moreover, job losses have been no higher in US states that implemented stay-at-home during the Covid-19 pandemic than in states that did not have stay-at-home. All of these results demonstrate that the Covid-19 pandemic is a common economic and public health shock. They also show that policy spillovers and behavioral responses are important. The tradeoff between the economy and public health in a pandemic depends strongly on what is happening elsewhere. This underscores the importance of coordinated economic and public health responses.

中文摘要

我们研究了非药物政策干预措施（如“居家令”）对传染病传播的影响。地方政策对经济或当地公共卫生几乎没有影响。居家令与COVID-19病例增长放缓之间仅存在微弱关联。观察到的“流动性”减少与COVID-19病例增长放缓无关。居家令与工作场所活动减少和住宅活动增加相关，但共同冲击的影响要大得多。此外，在COVID-19大流行期间实施居家令的美国各州，其失业率并不高于未实施居家令的州。所有这些结果表明，COVID-19大流行是一种共同的经济和公共卫生冲击。它们也表明，政策溢出效应和行为反应很重要。在大流行中，经济与公共卫生之间的权衡在很大程度上取决于其他地方的情况。这凸显了协调经济和公共卫生应对措施的重要性。

No. 193论文详情NBER w27098

Office Visits Preventing Emergency Room Visits: Evidence From the Flint Water Switch

门诊就诊预防急诊就诊：来自弗林特水源切换的证据

Shooshan Danagoulian, Daniel S. Grossman, David Slusky

Abstract

Emergency department visits are costly to providers and to patients. We use the Flint water crisis to test if an increase in office visits reduced avoidable emergency room visits. In September 2015, the city of Flint issued a lead advisory to its residents, alerting them of increased lead levels in their drinking water, resulting from the switch in water source from Lake Huron to the Flint River. Using Medicaid claims for 2013-2016, we find that this information shock increased the share of enrollees who had lead tests performed by 1.7 percentage points. Additionally, it increased office visits immediately following the information shock and led to a reduction of 4.9 preventable, non-emergent, and primary-care-treatable emergency room visits per 1000 eligible children (8.2%). This decrease is present in shifts from emergency room visits to office visits across several common conditions. Our analysis suggest that children were more likely to receive care from the same clinic following lead tests and that establishing care reduced the likelihood parents would take their children to emergency rooms for conditions treatable in an office setting. Our results are potentially applicable to any situation in which individuals are induced to seek more care in an office visit setting.

中文摘要

急诊就诊对医疗服务提供者和患者而言成本高昂。我们利用弗林特水危机来检验门诊就诊的增加是否减少了可避免的急诊就诊。2015年9月，弗林特市向其居民发布了铅警告，提醒他们饮用水中的铅含量升高，这是由于水源从休伦湖切换到弗林特河所致。利用2013-2016年的医疗补助索赔数据，我们发现这一信息冲击使接受铅检测的参保者比例增加了1.7个百分点。此外，信息冲击后门诊就诊立即增加，并导致每1000名符合条件的儿童中可预防、非紧急且初级保健可治疗的急诊就诊减少了4.9次（8.2%）。这种减少体现在几种常见疾病从急诊就诊向门诊就诊的转变中。我们的分析表明，儿童在铅检测后更有可能从同一诊所获得护理，而建立护理关系降低了家长因可在门诊治疗的疾病而带孩子去急诊的可能性。我们的结果可能适用于任何促使个人在门诊环境中寻求更多护理的情况。

No. 194论文详情NBER w27097

Income, Liquidity, and the Consumption Response to the 2020 Economic Stimulus Payments

收入、流动性与2020年经济刺激支付的消费反应

Scott R. Baker, R. A. Farrokhnia, Steffen Meyer, Michaela Pagel, Constantine Yannelis

Abstract

The 2020 CARES Act directed large cash payments to households. We analyze house-holds’ spending responses using high-frequency transaction data from a Fintech non-profit, exploring heterogeneity by income levels, recent income declines, and liquidity as well as linked survey responses about economic expectations. Households respond rapidly to the re-ceipt of stimulus payments, with spending increasing by $\$0.25$-$\$0.40$ per dollar of stimulus during the first weeks. Households with lower incomes, greater income drops, and lower lev-els of liquidity display stronger responses highlighting the importance of targeting. Liquidity plays the most important role, with no significant spending response for households with large checking account balances. Households that expect employment losses and benefit cuts dis-play weaker responses to the stimulus. Relative to the effects of previous economic stimulus programs in 2001 and 2008, we see faster effects, smaller increases in durables spending, larger increases in spending on food, and substantial increases in payments like rents, mortgages, and credit cards reflecting a short-term debt overhang. We formally show that these differences can make direct payments less effective in stimulating aggregate consumption.

中文摘要

2020年《CARES法案》向家庭发放了大额现金支付。我们利用一家金融科技非营利组织的高频交易数据分析家庭的支出反应，探讨了按收入水平、近期收入下降和流动性划分的异质性，以及关于经济预期的关联调查回应。家庭在收到刺激支付后迅速做出反应，最初几周内每美元刺激支出增加0.25-0.40美元。收入较低、收入下降幅度较大和流动性水平较低的家庭表现出更强的反应，凸显了精准施策的重要性。流动性起着最重要的作用，对于支票账户余额较高的家庭，没有显著的支出反应。预期失业和福利削减的家庭对刺激的反应较弱。与2001年和2008年之前经济刺激计划的效果相比，我们看到效果更快，耐用品支出增长较小，食品支出增长较大，以及租金、抵押贷款和信用卡等支付大幅增加，反映了短期债务积压。我们正式表明，这些差异可能使直接支付在刺激总消费方面效果较差。

No. 195论文详情NBER w27096

Employer Policies and the Immigrant-Native Earnings Gap

雇主政策与移民-本地人收入差距

Benoit Dostie, Jiang Li, David Card, Daniel Parent

Abstract

We use longitudinal data from the income tax system to study the impacts of firms’ employment and wage-setting policies on the level and change in immigrant-native wage differences in Canada. We focus on immigrants who arrived in the early 2000s, distinguishing between those with and without a college degree from two broad groups of countries – the U.S., the U.K. and Northern Europe, and the rest of the world. Consistent with a growing literature based on the two-way fixed effects model of Abowd, Kramarz, and Margolis (1999), we find that firm-specific wage premiums explain a significant share of earnings inequality in Canada and contribute to the average earnings gap between immigrants and natives. In the decade after receiving permanent status, earnings of immigrants rise relative to those of natives. Compositional effects due to selective outmigration and changing participation play no role in this gain. About one-sixth is attributable to movements up the job ladder to employers that offer higher pay premiums for all groups, with particularly large gains for immigrants from the “rest of the world” countries.

中文摘要

我们利用所得税系统的纵向数据研究企业的就业和工资制定政策对加拿大移民与本地人工资差异水平和变化的影响。我们关注21世纪初抵达的移民，区分了来自两大国家群体（美国、英国和北欧，以及世界其他地区）的拥有和未拥有大学学位的移民。与基于Abowd、Kramarz和Margolis（1999）双向固定效应模型的日益增长的文献一致，我们发现企业特定的工资溢价解释了加拿大收入不平等的重要部分，并导致了移民与本地人之间的平均收入差距。在获得永久身份后的十年里，移民的收入相对于本地人有所上升。选择性向外迁移和参与率变化带来的构成效应在这一增长中没有作用。大约六分之一的增长归因于向提供更高工资溢价（对所有群体）的雇主晋升，其中来自“世界其他地区”国家的移民收益尤其大。

No. 196论文详情NBER w27095

Did the Paycheck Protection Program Hit the Target?

薪资保护计划是否命中目标？

João Granja, Christos Makridis, Constantine Yannelis, Eric Zwick

Abstract

This paper provides a comprehensive assessment of financial intermediation and the economic effects of the Paycheck Protection Program (PPP), a large and novel small business support program that was part of the initial policy response to the COVID-19 pandemic in the US. We use loan-level microdata for all PPP loans and high-frequency administrative employment data to present three main findings. First, banks played an important role in mediating program targeting, which helps explain why some funds initially flowed to regions that were less adversely affected by the pandemic. Second, we exploit regional heterogeneity in lending relationships and individual firm-loan matched data to study the role of banks in explaining the employment effects of the PPP. We find the short- and medium-term employment effects of the program were small compared to the program’s size. Third, many firms used the loans to make non-payroll fixed payments and build up savings buffers, which can account for small employment effects and likely reflects precautionary motives in the face of heightened uncertainty. Limited targeting in terms of who was eligible likely also led to many inframarginal firms receiving funds and to a low correlation between regional PPP funding and shock severity. Our findings illustrate how business liquidity support programs affect firm behavior and local economic activity, and how policy trans-mission depends on the agents delegated to deploy it.

中文摘要

本文对薪资保护计划（PPP）的金融中介和经济效应进行了全面评估，该计划是美国应对COVID-19大流行初期政策中一项大规模且新颖的小企业支持计划。我们利用所有PPP贷款的贷款级微观数据和高频行政就业数据，提出了三个主要发现。首先，银行在调节计划目标方面发挥了重要作用，这有助于解释为何部分资金最初流向了受大流行影响较小的地区。其次，我们利用借贷关系的区域异质性和个体企业-贷款匹配数据，研究银行在解释PPP就业效应中的作用。我们发现，与计划规模相比，该计划的短期和中期就业效应较小。第三，许多企业利用贷款进行非工资的固定支付并建立储蓄缓冲，这可以解释较小的就业效应，并可能反映了面对高度不确定性时的预防性动机。在资格方面的有限针对性也可能导致许多边际内企业获得资金，并导致区域PPP资金与冲击严重性之间的低相关性。我们的发现说明了企业流动性支持计划如何影响企业行为和当地经济活动，以及政策传导如何取决于被授权部署它的代理人。

No. 197论文详情NBER w27094

A New Method for Estimating Teacher Value-Added

一种估计教师增值的新方法

Michael Gilraine, Jiaying Gu, Robert McMillan

Abstract

This paper proposes a new methodology for estimating teacher value-added. Rather than imposing a normality assumption on unobserved teacher quality (as in the standard empirical Bayes approach), our nonparametric estimator permits the underlying distribution to be estimated directly and in a computationally feasible way. The resulting estimates fit the unobserved distribution very well regardless of the form it takes, as we show in Monte Carlo simulations. Implementing the nonparametric approach in practice using two separate large-scale administrative data sets, we find the estimated teacher value-added distributions depart from normality and differ from each other. To draw out the policy implications of our method, we first consider a widely-discussed policy to release teachers at the bottom of the value-added distribution, comparing predicted test score gains under our nonparametric approach with those using parametric empirical Bayes. Here the parametric method predicts similar policy gains in one data set while overestimating those in the other by a substantial margin. We also show the predicted gains from teacher retention policies can be underestimated significantly based on the parametric method. In general, the results highlight the benefit of our nonparametric empirical Bayes approach, given that the unobserved distribution of value-added is likely to be context-specific.

中文摘要

本文提出了一种估计教师增值的新方法。我们的非参数估计量不假设未观测到的教师质量服从正态分布（如标准经验贝叶斯方法那样），而是允许直接以计算上可行的方式估计潜在分布。正如我们在蒙特卡洛模拟中所示，无论分布形式如何，由此产生的估计都能很好地拟合未观测到的分布。使用两个独立的大规模行政数据集实际应用非参数方法，我们发现估计的教师增值分布偏离正态分布，并且彼此不同。为了阐明我们方法的政策含义，我们首先考虑一项广泛讨论的政策——解雇增值分布底部的教师，比较了非参数方法与参数经验贝叶斯方法下预测的考试成绩增益。在这里，参数方法在一个数据集中预测了类似的政策增益，但在另一个数据集中则大幅高估了这些增益。我们还表明，基于参数方法，教师留任政策的预测增益可能被显著低估。总体而言，结果凸显了我们非参数经验贝叶斯方法的优势，因为未观测到的增值分布很可能是情境特定的。

No. 198论文详情NBER w27093

Expected Profits and The Scientific Novelty of Innovation

预期利润与创新的科学新颖性

David Dranove, Craig Garthwaite, Manuel I. Hermosilla

Abstract

Innovation policy involves trading off monopoly output and pricing in the short run in exchange for incentives for firms to develop new products in the future. While existing research demonstrates that expected profits fuel R&D investments, little is known about the novelty of the projects funded by these investments. Relying on data that describe the scientific approaches used by a large sample of experimental drug projects, we expand on this literature by examining the scientific novelty of pharmaceutical R&D investments following the creation of the Medicare Part D program. We find little evidence that the positive demand shock implied by this program prompted firms to undertake scientifically novel R&D activity, as measured by whether the specific scientific approach had been used before. However, we find some evidence that firms invested in products involving novel combinations of scientific approaches. These estimates can inform economists and policymakers assessing the tradeoffs associated with marginal changes in commercial returns from newly developed pharmaceutical products.

中文摘要

创新政策涉及在短期内权衡垄断产出和定价，以换取激励企业未来开发新产品的动力。虽然现有研究表明预期利润推动了研发投资，但对于这些投资资助的项目的新颖性知之甚少。利用描述大量实验性药物项目所使用科学方法的数据，我们通过考察医疗保险D部分计划创建后制药研发投资的科学新颖性，扩展了这一文献。我们发现，几乎没有证据表明该计划带来的正向需求冲击促使企业从事科学新颖的研发活动，这是根据特定科学方法是否曾被使用来衡量的。然而，我们确实发现一些证据表明，企业投资于涉及科学方法新颖组合的产品。这些估计可以为评估新开发药品商业回报边际变化相关权衡的经济学家和政策制定者提供信息。

No. 199论文详情NBER w27092

Measuring the Perceived Liquidity of the Corporate Bond Market

衡量公司债券市场的感知流动性

Sergey Chernenko, Adi Sunderam

Abstract

We propose a novel measure of bond market liquidity that does not depend on transaction data: the strength of the cross-sectional relationship between mutual fund cash holdings and fund flow volatility. Our measure captures how liquid funds perceive their portfolio holdings to be at a given point in time. The perceived liquidity of speculative grade and Rule 144A bonds is significantly lower than investment grade bonds in the cross section and deteriorated significantly following the 2008-9 financial crisis. Our measure can be applied in settings where either transaction data are not available or transactions are rare, including the markets for asset-backed securities, syndicated loans, and municipal bonds.

中文摘要

我们提出了一种不依赖交易数据的债券市场流动性新衡量指标：共同基金现金持有量与基金流量波动性之间的横截面关系强度。我们的指标捕捉了基金在特定时间点对其投资组合持有量的感知流动性。在横截面上，投机级和144A规则债券的感知流动性显著低于投资级债券，并在2008-9年金融危机后显著恶化。我们的指标可应用于交易数据不可用或交易稀少的环境，包括资产支持证券、银团贷款和市政债券市场。
