When Do Shelter-in-Place Orders Fight COVID-19 Best? Policy Heterogeneity Across States and Adoption Time

居家令何时能最好地抗击COVID-19？各州政策异质性与采纳时间

Dhaval M. Dave, Andrew I. Friedson, Kyutaro Matsuzawa, Joseph J. Sabia

Abstract

Shelter in place orders (SIPOs) require residents to remain home for all but essential activities such as purchasing food or medicine, caring for others, exercise, or traveling for employment deemed essential. Between March 19 and April 20, 2020, 40 states and the District of Columbia adopted SIPOs. This study explores the impact of SIPOs on health, with particular attention to heterogeneity in their impacts. First, using daily state-level social distancing data from SafeGraph and a difference-in-differences approach, we document that adoption of a SIPO was associated with a 5 to 10 percent increase in the rate at which state residents remained in their homes full-time. Then, using daily state-level coronavirus case data collected by the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention, we find that approximately three weeks following the adoption of a SIPO, cumulative COVID-19 cases fell by 44 percent. Event-study analyses confirm common COVID-19 case trends in the week prior to SIPO adoption and show that SIPO-induced case reductions grew larger over time. However, this average effect masks important heterogeneity across states — early adopters and high population density states appear to reap larger benefits from their SIPOs. Finally, we find that statewide SIPOs were associated with a reduction in coronavirus-related deaths, but estimated mortality effects were imprecisely estimated.

中文摘要

居家令要求居民除购买食品或药品、照顾他人、锻炼或从事被视为必要的就业等基本活动外，留在家中。2020年3月19日至4月20日期间，40个州和哥伦比亚特区采纳了居家令。本研究探讨了居家令对健康的影响，特别关注其影响的异质性。首先，利用SafeGraph的每日州级社交距离数据和双重差分方法，我们记录了采纳居家令与州居民全天候留在家中比例增加5%至10%相关。然后，利用疾病控制与预防中心收集的每日州级冠状病毒病例数据，我们发现采纳居家令约三周后，累计COVID-19病例下降了44%。事件研究分析证实了在采纳居家令前一周COVID-19病例趋势相似，并显示居家令导致的病例减少随时间推移而增大。然而，这一平均效应掩盖了各州之间的重要异质性——早期采纳者和人口密度高的州似乎从其居家令中获益更大。最后，我们发现全州范围的居家令与冠状病毒相关死亡减少相关，但估计的死亡率效应并不精确。

Dropouts Need Not Apply? The Minimum Wage and Skill Upgrading

辍学者不予录用？最低工资与技能升级

Jeffrey Clemens, Lisa B. Kahn, Jonathan Meer

Abstract

We explore whether minimum wage increases result in substitution from lower-skilled to slightly higher-skilled labor. Using 2011-2016 American Community Survey data (ACS), we show that workers employed in low-wage occupations are older and more likely to have a high school diploma following recent statutory minimum wage increases. To better understand the role of firms, we examine the Burning Glass vacancy data. We find increases in a high school diploma requirement following minimum wage hikes, consistent with our ACS evidence on stocks of employed workers. We see substantial adjustments to requirements both within and across firms.

中文摘要

Do Differences in School Quality Generate Heterogeneity in the Causal Returns to Education?

学校质量差异是否会导致教育因果回报的异质性？

Philip DeCicca, Harry Krashinsky

Abstract

Estimating the returns to education remains an active area of research amongst applied economists. Most studies that estimate the causal return to education exploit changes in schooling and/or labor laws to generate exogenous differences in education. An implicit assumption is that more time in school may translate into greater earnings potential. None of these studies, however, explicitly consider the quality of schooling to which impacted students are exposed. To extend this literature, we examine the interaction between school quality and policy-induced returns to schooling, using temporally-available school quality measures from Card and Krueger (1992). We find that additional compulsory schooling, via either schooling or labor laws, increases earnings only if educational inputs are of sufficiently high quality. In particular, we find a consistent role for teacher quality, as measured by relative teacher pay across states, in generating consistently positive returns to compulsory schooling.

中文摘要

估算教育回报率仍是应用经济学家活跃的研究领域。大多数估算教育因果回报的研究利用学校法和/或劳动法的变化来产生教育的外生差异。一个隐含的假设是，更多的在校时间可能会转化为更高的收入潜力。然而，这些研究都没有明确考虑受影响学生所接受的学校教育质量。为了扩展这一文献，我们利用Card和Krueger（1992）中按时间可得的学校质量指标，考察了学校质量与政策诱导的教育回报之间的相互作用。我们发现，只有当教育投入质量足够高时，额外的义务教育（通过学校法或劳动法）才能提高收入。具体而言，我们发现教师质量（以各州相对教师薪酬衡量）在产生持续正向的义务教育回报方面具有一致的作用。

No. 203论文详情NBER w27088

Dissecting Mechanisms of Financial Crises: Intermediation and Sentiment

解析金融危机的机制：中介与情绪

Arvind Krishnamurthy, Wenhao Li

Abstract

We develop a model of financial crises with both a financial amplification mechanism, via frictional intermediation, and a role for sentiment, via time-varying beliefs about an illiquidity state. The model accounts for the entire crisis cycle, matching data on the frothy pre-crisis behavior of asset markets and credit, the sharp transition to a crisis where asset values fall, disintermediation occurs and output falls, and the slow post-crisis recovery in output. Both the intermediation and belief mechanism are essential to match the crisis cycle. However, modeling the belief variation via either a Bayesian or diagnostic model can match the broad patterns.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个金融危机模型，该模型既包含通过摩擦性中介实现的金融放大机制，也包含通过关于非流动性状态时变信念的情绪作用。该模型解释了整个危机周期，与资产市场和信贷在危机前的泡沫行为、资产价值下跌、去中介化和产出下降的危机急剧转变，以及危机后产出的缓慢复苏等数据相匹配。中介机制和信念机制对于匹配危机周期都至关重要。然而，通过贝叶斯模型或诊断模型对信念变化进行建模，都可以匹配总体模式。

No. 204论文详情NBER w27087

Personalized Pricing and the Value of Time: Evidence from Auctioned Cab Rides

个性化定价与时间价值：来自拍卖网约车行程的证据

Nicholas Buchholz, Laura Doval, Jakub Kastl, Filip Matějka, Tobias Salz

Abstract

We recover valuations of time using detailed data from a large ride-hail platform, where drivers bid on trips and consumers choose between a set of rides with different prices and wait times. Leveraging a consumer panel, we estimate demand as a function of both prices and wait times and use the resulting estimates to recover heterogeneity in the value of time across consumers. We study the welfare implications of personalized pricing and its effect on the platform, drivers, and consumers. Taking into account drivers’ optimal reaction to the platform’s pricing policy, personalized pricing lowers consumer surplus by 2.5% and increases overall surplus by 5.2%. Like the platform, drivers benefit from personalized pricing. ETA-based pricing– where different prices are set for various wait times and where extensive use of consumer data is not required–can capture a significant portion of the profits garnered from personalized pricing, while simultaneously benefiting consumers.

中文摘要

我们利用来自大型网约车平台的详细数据恢复了时间估值，在该平台上，司机对行程进行竞标，消费者在具有不同价格和等待时间的一组行程中进行选择。利用消费者面板数据，我们估计了作为价格和等待时间函数的需求，并利用所得估计值恢复了消费者之间时间价值的异质性。我们研究了个性化定价的福利影响及其对平台、司机和消费者的效应。考虑到司机对平台定价策略的最优反应，个性化定价使消费者剩余降低2.5%，使总剩余增加5.2%。与平台一样，司机也从个性化定价中受益。基于ETA的定价——即为不同的等待时间设定不同的价格，且无需大量使用消费者数据——可以捕获个性化定价所获利润的很大一部分，同时使消费者受益。

No. 205论文详情NBER w27086

Ambiguous Pollution Response to COVID-19 in China

中国COVID-19污染响应的模糊性

Douglas Almond, Xinming Du, Shuang Zhang

Abstract

Reductions in ambient pollution have been taken as an indisputable "silver lining" to the COVID-19 Pandemic. Indeed, worldwide economic contraction induced by COVID-19 lockdowns should generate global air quality improvements ceteris paribus, including to China's notoriously-poor air quality. We analyze China's official pollution monitor data and account for the large, recurrent improvement in air quality following Lunar New Year (LNY), which essentially coincided with lock-downs in 2020. With the important exception of NO2, China's air quality improvements in 2020 are smaller than we should expect near the pandemic's epicenter: Hubei province. Compared with LNY improvements experienced in 2018 and 2019 in Hubei, we see smaller improvements in SO2 while ozone concentrations increased in both relative and absolute terms (roughly doubling). Similar patterns are found for the six provinces neighboring Hubei. We conclude that COVID-19 had ambiguous impacts on China's pollution, with evidence of relative deterioration in air quality near the Pandemic's epicenter.

中文摘要

环境污染物减少被视为COVID-19大流行一个无可争议的“一线希望”。确实，COVID-19封锁导致的世界经济收缩，在其他条件不变的情况下，应会带来全球空气质量改善，包括中国臭名昭著的恶劣空气质量。我们分析了中国的官方污染监测数据，并考虑了农历新年后空气质量的显著、周期性改善，而2020年的农历新年基本上与封锁同时发生。除了NO2这一重要例外，2020年中国空气质量的改善幅度小于我们在疫情中心——湖北省——附近的预期。与2018年和2019年湖北省农历新年期间的改善相比，我们看到SO2的改善幅度较小，而臭氧浓度在相对和绝对意义上均有所增加（大约翻倍）。在湖北省周边的六个省份也发现了类似模式。我们得出结论，COVID-19对中国污染的影响是模糊的，有证据表明疫情中心附近的空气质量相对恶化。

No. 206论文详情NBER w27085

Which Workers Bear the Burden of Social Distancing?

哪些工人承担了社交距离的负担？

Simon Mongey, Laura Pilossoph, Alex Weinberg

Abstract

Using data from O∗NET, we construct two measures of an occupation’s potential exposure to social distancing measures: (i) the ability to conduct that job from home and (ii) the degree of physical proximity to others the job requires. After validating these measures with comparable measures from ATUS as well as realized work-from-home rates during the pandemic, we employ the measures to study the characteristics of workers in these types of jobs. Our results show that workers in low-work-from-home and high-physical-proximity jobs are more economically vulnerable across various measures constructed from the CPS and PSID: they are less educated, of lower income, have fewer liquid assets relative to income, and are more likely renters. Consistent with the idea that high physical proximity or low work-from-home occupations were more exposed to the Coronavirus shock, we show that the types of workers predicted to be employed in them experienced greater declines in employment during the pandemic. We conclude by comparing the aggregate employment losses in these occupations to their employment losses in the 2008 recession, and ﬁnd evidence that these occupations were disproportionately exposed to the pandemic shock, and not just comprised of more cyclically sensitive workers.

中文摘要

利用O*NET的数据，我们构建了衡量职业在社交距离措施下潜在暴露程度的两项指标：（i）在家完成该工作的能力，以及（ii）该工作所需与他人身体接近的程度。在用美国时间使用调查的可比指标以及大流行期间实现的居家工作率验证这些指标后，我们利用这些指标来研究从事这些类型工作的工人的特征。我们的结果表明，根据当前人口调查和收入动态面板研究构建的各种指标，低居家工作率和高身体接近度工作的工人在经济上更脆弱：他们受教育程度较低、收入较低、流动资产相对于收入较少，并且更可能是租房者。与高身体接近度或低居家工作率的职业更容易受到冠状病毒冲击的观点一致，我们表明，预计从事这些职业的工人在大流行期间经历了更大的就业下降。最后，我们将这些职业的总就业损失与2008年衰退期间的就业损失进行比较，发现证据表明这些职业不成比例地暴露于大流行冲击，而不仅仅是包含更多周期性敏感的工人。

No. 207论文详情NBER w27084

Interest Rate Uncertainty as a Policy Tool

利率不确定性作为政策工具

Fabio Ghironi, G. Kemal Ozhan

Abstract

We study an unconventional policy tool–interest rate uncertainty–that may be used to discourage inefficient capital inflows and to adjust the composition of external accounts between short-term securities and foreign direct investment (FDI). Identified interest rate volatility shocks in several emerging markets cause a decline in GDP growth, increase in inflation, an improvement in the current account, and a depreciation in real exchange rate. Using a calibrated open-economy New Keynesian model, we introduce an interest rate uncertainty policy rule that adjusts the volatility of emerging market economy interest rate shocks in response to drivers of capital flows. The uncertainty policy discourages short-term inflows through portfolio risk and consumption smoothing channels. A markup channel combined with exchange rate depreciation generates FDI inflows. The transmission of uncertainty via markups is influenced by the extent of exchange rate pass-through. The uncertainty policy may be welfare improving if designed against uncertainty shocks that drive capital flows. However, it may be welfare reducing against level shocks that drive capital inflows. We further investigate new channels under different scenarios, including various assumptions about currency of export invoicing, varying degrees of risk aversion, interaction with different types of Taylor rules, and effective-lower-bound in the rest of the world.

中文摘要

我们研究了一种非常规政策工具——利率不确定性——它可用于阻止低效的资本流入，并调整外部账户在短期证券和外国直接投资之间的构成。在几个新兴市场中，已识别的利率波动冲击导致GDP增长下降、通胀上升、经常账户改善以及实际汇率贬值。利用校准后的开放经济新凯恩斯模型，我们引入了一项利率不确定性政策规则，该规则根据资本流动驱动因素调整新兴市场经济体利率冲击的波动性。不确定性政策通过投资组合风险和消费平滑渠道阻止短期流入。加价渠道与汇率贬值相结合，产生了外国直接投资流入。通过加价传导不确定性的程度受到汇率传递程度的影响。如果针对驱动资本流动的不确定性冲击进行设计，不确定性政策可能改善福利。然而，针对驱动资本流入的水平冲击，它可能降低福利。我们进一步研究了不同情景下的新渠道，包括关于出口计价货币的各种假设、不同程度的风险厌恶、与不同类型泰勒规则的相互作用，以及世界其他地区的有效下限。

No. 208论文详情NBER w27083

Steering Incentives of Platforms: Evidence from the Telecommunications Industry

平台的引导激励：来自电信行业的证据

Brian McManus, Aviv Nevo, Zachary Nolan, Jonathan W. Williams

Abstract

We study the trade-offs faced by Internet Service Providers (ISPs) that serve as platforms through which consumers access both television and internet services. As online streaming video improves, these providers may respond by attempting to steer consumers away from streaming video toward their own TV services, or by attempting to capture surplus from this improved internet content. We augment the standard mixed bundling model to demonstrate the trade-offs the ISP faces when dealing with streaming video, and we show how these trade-offs change with the pricing options available to the ISP. Next, we use unique household-level panel data and the introduction of usage-based pricing (UBP) in a subset of markets to measure consumers' responses and to evaluate quantitatively the ISP's trade-offs. We find that the introduction of UBP led consumers to upgrade their internet service plans and lower overall internet usage. Our findings suggest that while steering consumers towards TV services is possible, it is likely costly for the ISP and therefore unlikely to be profitable. This is especially true if the ISP can offer rich pricing menus that allow it to capture some of the surplus generated by a better internet service. The results suggest that policies like UBP can increase ISPs' incentive to maintain open access to new internet content.

中文摘要

我们研究了互联网服务提供商所面临的权衡，这些提供商是消费者访问电视和互联网服务的平台。随着在线流媒体视频的改进，这些提供商可能会通过尝试引导消费者远离流媒体视频转向其自有电视服务，或通过尝试从改进的互联网内容中获取剩余价值来做出反应。我们扩展了标准的混合捆绑模型，以展示互联网服务提供商在处理流媒体视频时所面临的权衡，并展示了这些权衡如何随着互联网服务提供商可用的定价选项而变化。接下来，我们利用独特的家庭层面面板数据以及部分市场引入基于使用量的定价，来衡量消费者的反应并定量评估互联网服务提供商的权衡。我们发现，基于使用量的定价的引入导致消费者升级其互联网服务计划并降低整体互联网使用量。我们的研究结果表明，虽然引导消费者转向电视服务是可能的，但这对于互联网服务提供商来说可能成本高昂，因此不太可能盈利。特别是如果互联网服务提供商能够提供丰富的定价菜单，使其能够捕获由更好的互联网服务产生的部分剩余价值，情况更是如此。结果表明，像基于使用量的定价这样的政策可以增加互联网服务提供商维持对新互联网内容开放接入的激励。

Global Behaviors and Perceptions at the Onset of the COVID-19 Pandemic

COVID-19大流行初期的全球行为与认知

Thiemo R. Fetzer, Marc Witte, Lukas Hensel, Jon Jachimowicz, Johannes Haushofer, Andriy Ivchenko, Stefano Caria, Elena Reutskaja, Christopher P. Roth, Stefano Fiorin, Margarita Gómez, Gordon Kraft-Todd, Friedrich M. Götz, Erez Yoeli

Abstract

We conducted a large-scale survey covering 58 countries and over 100,000 respondents between late March and early April 2020 to study beliefs and attitudes towards citizens’ and governments’ responses to the COVID-19 pandemic. Most respondents reacted strongly to the crisis: they report engaging in social distancing and hygiene behaviors, and believe that strong policy measures, such as shop closures and curfews, are necessary. They also believe that their government and their country’s citizens are not doing enough and underestimate the degree to which others in their country support strong behavioral and policy responses to the pandemic. The perception of a weak government and public response is associated with higher levels of worries and depression. Using both cross-country panel data and an event-study, we additionally show that strong government reactions correct misperceptions, and reduce worries and depression. Our findings highlight that policy-makers not only need to consider how their decisions affect the spread of COVID-19, but also how such choices influence the mental health of their population.

中文摘要

我们在2020年3月底至4月初进行了一项大规模调查，覆盖58个国家、超过10万名受访者，旨在研究公民与政府对COVID-19大流行反应的信念与态度。大多数受访者对危机反应强烈：他们报告采取了社交疏离和卫生行为，并认为关闭商店和宵禁等强力政策措施是必要的。他们还认为本国政府和公民做得不够，并低估了本国其他人对强力行为和政策应对大流行的支持程度。对政府与公众反应薄弱的认知与更高程度的担忧和抑郁相关。利用跨国面板数据和事件研究法，我们进一步表明，强有力的政府反应能够纠正错误认知，并减少担忧和抑郁。我们的发现强调，政策制定者不仅需要考虑其决策如何影响COVID-19的传播，还需考虑这些选择如何影响民众的心理健康。

No. 210论文详情NBER w27081

Electricity and Firm Productivity: A General-Equilibrium Approach

电力与企业生产率：一般均衡方法

Stephie Fried, David Lagakos

Abstract

The lack of reliable electricity in the developing world is widely viewed by policymakers as a major constraint on firm productivity. Yet most empirical studies find modest short-run effects of power outages on firm performance. This paper builds a dynamic macroeconomic model to study the long-run general equilibrium effects of power outages on productivity. The model captures the key features of how firms acquire electricity in the developing world, in particular the rationing of grid electricity and the possibility of self-generated electricity at higher cost. Power outages lower productivity in the model by creating idle resources, by depressing the scale of incumbent firms and by reducing entry of new firms. Consistent with the empirical literature, the model predicts that the short-run partial-equilibrium effects of eliminating outages are small. However, the long-run general-equilibrium effects are many times larger, supporting the view that eliminating outages is an important development objective.

中文摘要

发展中国家电力供应不可靠被政策制定者广泛视为企业生产率的主要制约因素。然而，大多数实证研究发现停电对企业绩效的短期影响较小。本文构建了一个动态宏观经济模型，研究停电对生产率的长期一般均衡效应。该模型捕捉了发展中国家企业获取电力的关键特征，特别是电网电力的配给以及以更高成本自行发电的可能性。模型中，停电通过造成资源闲置、抑制现有企业规模以及减少新企业进入来降低生产率。与实证文献一致，该模型预测消除停电的短期局部均衡效应较小。然而，长期一般均衡效应要大得多，这支持了消除停电是一项重要发展目标的观点。

No. 211论文详情NBER w27080

Economics of Research and Innovation in Agriculture

农业研究与创新的经济学

Petra Moser

Abstract

Feeding the world’s growing population is one of the most critical policy challenges for the 21st century. With tightening constraints on water, arable land, and other natural resources, agricultural innovation is quickly becoming the most promising path meet the nutrient needs for future generations. At the same time, the increasing variability in the world’s climate intensifies the need for developing new crops that can tolerate extreme weather. Despite the urgency of this task, there is an active discussion on the returns to public and private spending in agricultural R&D, and many of the world’s wealthier countries have scaled back their share of GDP devoted to agricultural R&D. Dwindling public support leaves universities, which, historically, have been a major source of agricultural innovation, increasingly dependent on funding from industry, with uncertain effects on agricultural research. All of these factors create an urgent need for systematic empirical evidence on the forces that drive research and innovation in agriculture. This book aims to provides such evidence through economic analyses of the sources of agricultural innovation, the challenges of measuring productivity, the role of universities and their interactions with industry, and emerging mechanisms to fund agricultural R&D.

中文摘要

养活全球不断增长的人口是21世纪最关键的政策挑战之一。随着水资源、可耕地和其他自然资源的约束日益收紧，农业创新正迅速成为满足未来几代人营养需求的最有希望的途径。与此同时，全球气候日益多变，加剧了开发能够耐受极端天气的新作物的需求。尽管这项任务紧迫，但关于公共和私人农业研发支出回报的讨论十分活跃，许多较富裕国家已削减了农业研发支出占GDP的比重。公共支持的减少使大学——历史上一直是农业创新的主要来源——越来越依赖行业资助，这对农业研究产生了不确定的影响。所有这些因素都迫切需要系统性的实证证据，以揭示推动农业研究与创新的力量。本书旨在通过经济分析提供此类证据，涵盖农业创新的来源、衡量生产率的挑战、大学的作用及其与行业的互动，以及资助农业研发的新兴机制。

No. 212论文详情NBER w27079

Incentivizing Behavioral Change: The Role of Time Preferences

激励行为改变：时间偏好的作用

Shilpa Aggarwal, Rebecca Dizon-Ross, Ariel D. Zucker

Abstract

How should the design of incentives vary with agent time preferences? We develop two predictions. First, “bundling” the payment function over time – specifically by making the payment for future effort increase in current effort – is more effective if individuals are impatient over effort. Second, increasing the frequency of payment is more effective if individuals are impatient over payment. We test the efficacy of time-bundling and payment frequency, and their interactions with impatience, using a randomized evaluation of an incentive program for exercise among diabetics in India. Consistent with our theoretical predictions, bundling payments over time meaningfully increases effort among the impatient relative to the patient. In contrast, increasing payment frequency has limited efficacy, suggesting limited impatience over payments. On average, incentives increase daily steps by 1,266 (13 minutes of brisk walking) and improve health.

中文摘要

激励设计应如何随代理人时间偏好而变化？我们提出两个预测。首先，如果个体对努力缺乏耐心，那么将支付函数在时间上“捆绑”——特别是使未来努力的支付随当前努力增加而增加——会更有效。其次，如果个体对支付缺乏耐心，那么增加支付频率会更有效。我们利用印度糖尿病患者运动激励计划的随机评估，检验了时间捆绑和支付频率及其与缺乏耐心的交互作用的有效性。与我们的理论预测一致，相对于有耐心的个体，时间捆绑支付显著增加了缺乏耐心个体的努力。相比之下，增加支付频率效果有限，表明对支付缺乏耐心的情况有限。平均而言，激励措施使每日步数增加了1266步（相当于13分钟快走），并改善了健康状况。

No. 213论文详情NBER w27078

Is the Supply of Charitable Donations Fixed? Evidence from Deadly Tornadoes

慈善捐赠的供给是固定的吗？来自致命龙卷风的证据

Tatyana Deryugina, Benjamin M. Marx

Abstract

Do new societal needs increase charitable giving or simply reallocate a fixed supply of donations? We study this question using IRS datasets and the natural experiment of deadly tornadoes. Among ZIP Codes located more than 20 miles away from a tornado's path, donations by households increase by over $\$1$ million per tornado fatality. We find no negative effects on charities located in these ZIP Codes, with a bootstrapped confidence interval that rejects substitution rates above 16 percent. The results imply that giving to one cause need not come at the expense of another.

中文摘要

新的社会需求是增加了慈善捐赠，还是仅仅重新分配了固定的捐赠供给？我们利用国税局数据集和致命龙卷风的自然实验来研究这一问题。在距离龙卷风路径超过20英里的邮政编码区，每起龙卷风死亡事件使家庭捐赠增加超过100万美元。我们未发现对这些邮政编码区内的慈善机构有负面影响，自助法置信区间拒绝了超过16%的替代率。结果表明，对某一事业的捐赠未必以牺牲另一事业为代价。

No. 214论文详情NBER w27077

Trade Credit and the Transmission of Unconventional Monetary Policy

商业信用与非常规货币政策的传导

Manuel Adelino, Miguel A. Ferreira, Mariassunta Giannetti, Pedro Pires

Abstract

We show that trade credit in production networks is important for the transmission of unconventional monetary policy. We find that firms with bonds eligible for purchase under the European Central Bank’s Corporate Sector Purchase Program act as financial intermediaries and extend more trade credit to their customers. The increase in trade credit flows is more pronounced from core countries to periphery countries and towards financially constrained customers. Customers increase investment and employment in response to the additional financing, while suppliers with eligible bonds increase their customer base, potentially favoring upstream industry concentration. Our findings suggest that the trade credit channel of monetary policy produces heterogeneous effects on regions, industries, and firms.

中文摘要

我们表明，生产网络中的商业信用对非常规货币政策的传导至关重要。我们发现，其债券符合欧洲央行企业部门购买计划购买条件的公司充当金融中介，并向其客户提供更多商业信用。商业信用流量的增加在核心国家向边缘国家以及向财务受限的客户中更为显著。客户利用额外融资增加投资和就业，而拥有合格债券的供应商则扩大了客户基础，这可能有利于上游行业集中。我们的发现表明，货币政策的商业信用渠道对地区、行业和企业产生异质性影响。

No. 215论文详情NBER w27076

Generosity Across the Income and Wealth Distributions

收入与财富分布中的慷慨程度

Jonathan Meer, Benjamin A. Priday

Abstract

Despite widespread interest, there is little systematic evidence on the relationship between income, wealth, and charitable giving. We use the Panel Study of Income Dynamics to provide descriptive statistics on this relationship. We find that, irrespective of specifica­tion, donative behavior increases with greater resources.

中文摘要

尽管人们普遍关注，但关于收入、财富与慈善捐赠之间关系的系统性证据很少。我们利用收入动态面板研究提供了这一关系的描述性统计。我们发现，无论采用何种设定，捐赠行为都随资源增加而增加。

No. 216论文详情NBER w27075

Immigration, Innovation, and Growth

移民、创新与增长

Konrad B. Burchardi, Thomas Chaney, Tarek Alexander Hassan, Lisa Tarquinio, Stephen J. Terry

Abstract

We show a causal impact of immigration on innovation and growth in US counties. To identify the causal impact of immigration, we use 130 years of detailed data on migrations from foreign countries to US counties to isolate quasi-random variation in the ancestry composition of US counties; interacting this plausibly exogenous variation in ancestry composition with the recent inflows of migrants from different origins, we predict the total number of migrants flowing into each US county in recent decades. We show immigration has a positive causal impact on innovation, measured as patenting of local firms, and on economic growth, measured as real income growth for native workers. We interpret those results through the lens of a quantitative model of endogenous growth and migrations. A structural estimation of this model targeting the well identified causal impact of migration on innovation suggests the large inflow of foreign migrants into the US since 1965 may have contributed to an additional 8% growth in innovation and 5% growth in wages.

中文摘要

我们展示了移民对美国各县创新与增长的因果影响。为识别移民的因果影响，我们利用130年来从外国到美国各县的详细迁移数据，以分离美国各县祖先构成的准随机变异；将这种看似外生的祖先构成变异与近期来自不同原籍地的移民流入交互作用，我们预测了最近几十年流入每个美国县的移民总数。我们发现，移民对创新（以当地企业的专利衡量）和经济增长（以本地工人的实际收入增长衡量）具有正向因果影响。我们通过一个内生增长与迁移的定量模型来解读这些结果。针对已识别的移民对创新的因果影响进行该模型的结构估计表明，自1965年以来大量外国移民流入美国可能贡献了额外的8%创新增长和5%工资增长。

No. 217论文详情NBER w27074

Optimal Bailouts and the Doom Loop with a Financial Network

最优救助与金融网络中的“厄运循环”

Agostino Capponi, Felix C. Corell, Joseph E. Stiglitz

Abstract

Banks usually hold large amounts of domestic debt which makes them vulnerable to their own sovereign's default risk. At the same time, governments often resort to costly bailouts when their banking sector is in trouble. We investigate how the network structure and the distribution of ownership of sovereign debt within the banking sector jointly affect the optimal bailout policy under this “doom loop”. We argue that rescuing banks with high domestic sovereign exposure is optimal if these banks are sufficiently central, even though that requires larger bailout expenditures than rescuing otherwise identical low-exposure banks. Our model illustrates how the “doom loop” exacerbates the “too interconnected to fail” problem.

中文摘要

银行通常持有大量国内债务，这使得它们容易受到本国主权违约风险的影响。同时，当银行业陷入困境时，政府往往采取代价高昂的救助措施。我们研究了网络结构以及银行业内主权债务所有权分布如何共同影响这种“厄运循环”下的最优救助政策。我们认为，如果持有高国内主权风险敞口的银行在金融网络中具有足够中心性，那么救助这些银行是最优的，尽管这需要比救助其他条件相同但低风险敞口的银行更大的救助支出。我们的模型说明了“厄运循环”如何加剧“过于互联而不能倒”的问题。

No. 218论文详情NBER w27073

Religion, Education, and the State

宗教、教育与国家

Samuel Bazzi, Masyhur Hilmy, Benjamin Marx

Abstract

This paper explores how state and religious providers of education compete during the nation building process. Using novel administrative data, we characterize the evolution of Indonesia’s Islamic education system and religious school choice after the introduction of mass public primary schooling in the 1970s. Funded through informal taxation, Islamic schools competed with the state by entering in the same markets. While primary enrollment shifted towards state schools, religious education increased overall as Islamic schools absorbed growing demand for secondary education. In the short run, electoral support for the secular regime weakened in markets with greater public school construction. Over the long run, Islamic schools established at this juncture are more differentiated in terms of religious curriculum, and cohorts exposed to mass public schooling as children are more invested in religion than in the national identity. Our findings offer a new perspective on the political economy of education reforms and the emergence of parallel systems of public goods provision.

中文摘要

本文探讨了在国家建设过程中，国家与宗教教育提供者如何竞争。利用新颖的行政数据，我们描述了20世纪70年代大规模公立小学教育引入后，印度尼西亚伊斯兰教育体系和宗教学校选择的演变。通过非正式税收资助，伊斯兰学校通过进入相同市场与国家竞争。虽然小学入学率转向公立学校，但宗教教育总体增加，因为伊斯兰学校吸收了日益增长的中学教育需求。短期内，在公立学校建设更多的市场中，对世俗政权的选举支持减弱。长期来看，在这一时期建立的伊斯兰学校在宗教课程方面更加差异化，而童年时期接触大规模公立教育的群体在宗教方面的投入多于国家认同。我们的发现为教育改革的政治经济学以及公共物品提供平行体系的出现提供了新视角。

No. 219论文详情NBER w27072

Geographic Mobility in America: Evidence from Cell Phone Data

美国的地理流动性：来自手机数据的证据

M. Keith Chen, Devin G. Pope

Abstract

Traveling beyond the immediate surroundings of one’s residence can lead to greater exposure to new ideas and information, jobs, and greater transmission of disease. In this paper, we document the geographic mobility of individuals in the U.S., and how this mobility varies across U.S. cities, regions, and income classes. Using geolocation data for ~1.7 million smartphone users over a 10-month period, we compute different measures of mobility, including the total distance traveled, the median daily distance traveled, the maximum distance traveled from one’s home, and the number of unique haunts visited. We find large differences across cities and income groups. For example, people in New York travel 38% fewer total kilometers and visit 14% fewer block-sized areas than people in Atlanta. And, individuals in the bottom income quartile travel 12% less overall and visit 13% fewer total locations than the top income quartile.

中文摘要

出行超出个人住所的周边范围，可以带来更多接触新思想、信息和工作的机会，但也增加了疾病传播的风险。在本文中，我们记录了美国个人的地理流动性，以及这种流动性如何在美国城市、地区和收入阶层之间变化。利用约170万智能手机用户在10个月内的地理定位数据，我们计算了不同的流动性指标，包括总出行距离、每日中位出行距离、离家最远出行距离以及访问的独特地点数量。我们发现城市和收入群体之间存在巨大差异。例如，纽约人比亚特兰大人总出行距离少38%，访问的街区规模区域少14%。此外，收入最低四分位的人比收入最高四分位的人总出行距离少12%，访问的总地点数量少13%。

No. 220论文详情NBER w27071

Team Players: How Social Skills Improve Group Performance

团队合作者：社交技能如何提升团队绩效

Ben Weidmann, David J. Deming

Abstract

Most jobs require teamwork. Are some people good team players? In this paper we design and test a new method for identifying individual contributions to group performance. We randomly assign people to multiple teams and predict team performance based on previously assessed individual skills. Some people consistently cause their group to exceed its predicted performance. We call these individuals “team players”. Team players score significantly higher on a well-established measure of social intelligence, but do not differ across a variety of other dimensions, including IQ, personality, education and gender. Social skills – defined as a single latent factor that combines social intelligence scores with the team player effect – improve group performance about as much as IQ. We find suggestive evidence that team players increase effort among teammates.

中文摘要

大多数工作需要团队合作。有些人是否是优秀的团队合作者？在本文中，我们设计并测试了一种识别个人对团队绩效贡献的新方法。我们将人员随机分配到多个团队，并根据先前评估的个人技能预测团队绩效。有些人始终使其团队超越预测绩效。我们称这些人为“团队合作者”。团队合作者在成熟的社交智力测量中得分显著更高，但在包括智商、人格、教育和性别在内的其他多种维度上没有差异。社交技能——定义为结合社交智力得分与团队合作者效应的单一潜在因素——对团队绩效的提升程度与智商相当。我们发现有提示性证据表明，团队合作者能提高队友的努力程度。

No. 221论文详情NBER w27070

Does Economics Make You Sexist?

经济学是否让人变得性别歧视？

Valentina A. Paredes, M. Daniele Paserman, Francisco Pino

Abstract

Recent research has highlighted unequal treatment for women in academic economics along several different dimensions, including promotion, hiring, credit for co-authorship, and standards for publication in professional journals. Can the source of these differences lie in biases against women that are pervasive in the discipline, even among students in the earliest stages of their training? In this paper, we provide evidence on the importance of explicit and implicit biases against women among students in economics relative to other fields. We conducted a large scale survey among undergraduate students in Chilean universities, among both entering first-year students and students in years 2 and above. On a wide battery of measures, economics students are more biased than students in other fields. Economics students are somewhat more biased already upon entry, before exposure to any economics classes. The gap is more pronounced among students in years 2 and above, in particular for male students. We also find an increase in bias in a sample of students that we follow longitudinally. Differences in political ideology explain essentially all the gap at entry, but none of the increase in the gap with exposure. Exposure to female students and faculty attenuates some of the bias.

中文摘要

近期研究强调了学术经济学界在多个不同维度上对女性的不平等对待，包括晋升、招聘、合著署名以及专业期刊发表标准。这些差异的根源是否在于该学科中普遍存在的对女性的偏见，甚至存在于处于培训早期阶段的学生中？在本文中，我们提供了经济学学生相对于其他领域学生中显性和隐性性别偏见重要性的证据。我们在智利大学本科生中进行了一项大规模调查，对象包括刚入学的一年级学生以及二年级及以上的学生。在一系列广泛的测量指标上，经济学学生比其他领域的学生偏见更强。经济学学生在入学时，即在接触任何经济学课程之前，就已经表现出稍强的偏见。这种差距在二年级及以上的学生中更为明显，尤其是男性学生。我们还在一个纵向跟踪的学生样本中发现了偏见的增加。政治意识形态的差异基本上解释了入学时的全部差距，但无法解释随着课程接触而增加的差距。接触女学生和女教师会减弱部分偏见。

No. 222论文详情NBER w27069

Inequality and the Safety Net Throughout the Income Distribution, 1929-1940

1929-1940年收入分配中的不平等与安全网

James J. Feigenbaum, Price V. Fishback, Keoka Grayson

Abstract

We explored two measures of inequality that described the full income distribution in cities. One measure is an income gini based on family incomes in 1929 for 33 cities and in 1933 for up to 48 cities in 1933 were spread throughout the country. We also estimated gini coefficients that made use of contract rents for renters and implicit rents for home owners for up to 955 cities throughout the country. We were able to expand to all counties when looking at a top-end inequality measure, the number of taxpayers per family. All three measures varied substantially across the country. We show the correlations between the various measures and also estimate the relationship between the measures and various relief programs developed by governments at all levels during the period.

中文摘要

我们探讨了两种描述城市完整收入分配的不平等指标。一种指标是基于1929年33个城市和1933年最多48个城市的家庭收入计算出的收入基尼系数，这些城市分布在全国各地。我们还利用最多955个城市中租房者的合同租金和房主的隐含租金估算了基尼系数。在考察一项顶端不平等指标（即每家庭纳税人数量）时，我们能够将范围扩大到所有县。所有三项指标在全国各地差异显著。我们展示了各指标之间的相关性，并估计了这些指标与这一时期各级政府制定的各种救济计划之间的关系。

No. 223论文详情NBER w26845

The Environmental Bias of Trade Policy

贸易政策的环境偏见

Joseph S. Shapiro

Abstract

This paper describes a new fact, then analyzes its causes and consequences: in most countries, import tariffs and non-tariff barriers are substantially lower on dirty than on clean industries, where an industry's “dirtiness” is defined as its carbon dioxide (CO2) emissions per dollar of output. This difference in trade policy creates a global implicit subsidy to CO2 emissions in internationally traded goods and so contributes to climate change. This global implicit subsidy to CO2 emissions totals several hundred billion dollars annually. The greater protection of downstream industries, which are relatively clean, substantially accounts for this pattern. The downstream pattern can be explained by theories where industries lobby for low tariffs on their inputs but final consumers are poorly organized. A quantitative general equilibrium model suggests that if countries applied similar trade policies to clean and dirty goods, global CO2 emissions would decrease and global real income would change little.

中文摘要

本文描述了一个新事实，然后分析了其原因和后果：在大多数国家，对肮脏行业的进口关税和非关税壁垒显著低于对清洁行业的，其中行业的“肮脏程度”以其每单位产出的二氧化碳排放量定义。贸易政策上的这种差异为国际贸易商品中的二氧化碳排放创造了全球性隐性补贴，从而加剧了气候变化。这种全球性二氧化碳排放隐性补贴总额每年达数千亿美元。对相对清洁的下游行业提供更大保护，在很大程度上解释了这种模式。下游模式可以用以下理论解释：行业游说要求对其投入品征收低关税，而最终消费者组织性较差。一个定量的一般均衡模型表明，如果各国对清洁和肮脏商品实施类似的贸易政策，全球二氧化碳排放量将减少，而全球实际收入变化不大。
